  ✎ <u>It looked/ seemed/ appeared as if/ as though</u> she would be the first ship home, <u>but</u> during the race she had a lot of bad luck.（原文换用）
  ✎ <u>It looked/ seemed/ appeared certain that</u> there would be an exciting race across the Channel, <u>but</u> Latham failed to get up early enough. 看似肯定会有一场激动人心的穿越海峡的竞速比赛了，但是莱瑟姆未能起得足够早。
  ✎ <u>It looked/ seemed/ appeared as if/ as though</u> there would be an exciting race across the Channel, <u>but</u> Latham failed to get up early enough. 看似好像会有一场激动人心的穿越海峡的竞速比赛了，但是莱瑟姆未能起得足够早。
+ **home** ad. 到家，回家（相当于go home）
+ **luck** 如不做额外说明，一般就指好运气
  ✎ It was <u>an</u> incredible <u>piece of luck</u>. 这真是令人难以相信的运气。
  ✎ With <u>a bit of</u> luck, we’ll finish on time. 如果有点运气的话，我们会按时完成的。
  ✎ Often <u>there is an element of luck</u> in getting the right answer. 得到正确答案往往需要一些运气。
  **<u>bad/ ill/ rotten/ tough</u> luck** 坏运气，厄运
  ✎ The team has **had a run of bad luck** lately, losing their last five games. 这支球队最近有一连串的坏运气，输掉了最后五场比赛。（一连串的厄运（习语））
+ **strike(struck struck)**
  + **1.打点，报时**
  ✎ The big clock which used to <u>strike the hours</u> day and night was damaged many years ago and has been silent ever since.（L2）
  + **2.重击，砸某人/某物**
  ✎ One of the thieves <u>was struck by</u> a heavy statue, but he was too busy helping himself to diamonds to notice any pain.（L6）
  + **3.某人想到某事 it strikes sb. that……**（L13）
  ✎ <u>It</u> suddenly <u>struck Mrs. Richards that</u> it must be the man from the Electricity Board who had come to read the meter.（L13）
  + **4. 不幸的事情突然发生，且造成了严重的伤害**
  ✎ Most people were fast asleep when the earthquake <u>struck</u>.（L2）
  近义搭配：
  **be caught in……** 赶上/遭遇倒霉事（未必造成严重损害）
  ✎ We <u>were caught in</u> a heavy storm/ a traffic jam. 我们赶上暴风雨/堵车了。
+ **<u>heavy/ severe/ violent/ devastating/ disastrous</u> storm**
  特大/严重/暴烈/摧枯拉朽/灾难性的暴风雨
+ **during which** 在（暴风雨）期间
  ┏ In August, she was struck by <u>a very heavy storm</u> **during which** her rudder was torn away.（原文）
  ┗ In August, she was struck by <u>a very heavy storm</u> **and during <u>the storm</u>** her rudder was torn away.（啰嗦）
  ✎ A week before, he had completed a successful overland flight <u>during which</u> he covered twenty-six miles.（L20）
  ✎ As long ago as the 1930’s, the Red Army had completed the successful Long March <u>during which</u> they covered 25,000 li. 早在20世纪30年代，红军就完成了伟大的长征，在这期间他们走过了25,000里。
+ **tear sth. <u>away/ off/ up</u>……** 撕扯；揪掉，卷走
  ✎ The flag <u>was torn away</u> from the pole by the strong wind. 旗帜被强风从旗杆上扯走了。
  ✎ High winds nearly <u>tore</u> the roof <u>off</u>. 大风几乎把屋顶掀掉了。
  ✎ The storm had <u>torn</u> the old tree <u>up</u> by the roots. 暴风雨把那棵老树连根拔起了。
+ **roll <u>heavily/ violently</u> <u>from side to side/ to and fro</u>** 剧烈地来回摆动
  ✎ The ship was <u>rolling heavily to and fro</u>. 这艘船在剧烈地前后摆动。
  ✎ The plane <u>rolled violently from side to side</u> in the storm. 这架飞机在暴风雨中剧烈地左右摇摆。
  **from side to side**
  同结构搭配：
  **from place to place** 四处，到处
  ✎ His few material possessions make it possible for him to move <u>from place to place</u> with ease.（L27）
  read sth. **from cover to cover** 从头到尾阅读了某物（从头到尾）
  sell sth. **from door to door** 挨家挨户地推销某物（挨家挨户）
  vary **from person to person** 因人而异（从这个人到那个人）
  improve **from day to day** 日益改善（从这一天到那一天）
+ **on board** 在船上(本文)，到船上
  ✎ Before she had anchored, the men from the boats had climbed <u>on board</u> and the decks were soon covered with colourful rugs from Persia, silks from India,copper coffee pots, and beautiful hand-made silver-ware. 到船上（L28）
+ **spare** 备用的，多余的
  a <u>spare</u> key/ battery/ tire…… 一个备用钥匙/电池/轮胎
+ with difficulty = difficultly
  with great difficulty = very difficultly（语气更强）
  **with + n. 作状语相当于 ad.**
  ✎ A temporary rudder was made on board from spare planks and it was fitted <u>with great difficulty (= very difficultly)</u>.（原文）
  ✎ The Officer went through the case <u>with great care (= very carefully)</u>.（L11）
+ **there <u>is/ was</u> a danger that……** 有……的危险（某个不好的事可能会发生）
  ✎ <u>There was a danger that</u> the wave would rebound off the other side of the bank and send the dish plunging into the water again.（L43）
  ✎ <u>There is a danger that</u> the political disorder of the past will return. 过去的政治动荡有可能卷土重来。
  ✎ <u>There is a danger that</u> museums will attempt to entertain rather than educate. 博物馆有可能试图取悦而不是教育访问者。
  ✎ <u>There was a danger that</u> if Mrs. Ramsay went to the police, she would never see Rastus again. 如果Ramsay夫人报警，她可能就再也看不到Rastus了。
+ ┏ Because of this, the *Cutty Sark* <u>lost her lead</u>.（原文）
  ┗ Because of this, the *Cutty Sark* <u>lost the lead to</u> the *Thermopylae*.
  ┗ Because of this, the *Thermopylae* <u>took (over) the lead from</u> the *Cutty Sark*.
+ **equator** 赤道
  相关词：
  **pole** 极 ；**the North/ South Pole** 北极/南极
  **latitude** 纬度；**longitude** 经度；**axis** 地轴
+ **call in at somewhere** 顺路去某地
  **call in on sb.** 顺路去拜访某人
  ✎ Will you <u>call in at</u> the supermarket for some eggs and milk? 你能顺路去超市买些鸡蛋和牛奶吗？
  ✎ Could you <u>call in on</u> Mum on your way home? 你能在回家的路上顺道去看望一下妈妈吗？
+ **have sth. done** 请人做某事
+ **by now**（此处相当于by then。用by now代替by then更有代入感、现场感，如同身临其境，多见于小说，描述故事情节）
  ✎ I had expected to be near my objective <u>by now</u>, but everything still seemed alien to me.（L57）
+ ┏ ……, but by now the Thermopylae was over five hundred miles <u>ahead</u>.（原文：前文有交代，故可不多赘述）
  ┗ ……, but by now the Thermopylae was over five hundred miles <u>ahead of the *Cutty Sark*</u>. 在……之前
  ┗ ……, but by now the Thermopylae was over five hundred miles <u>ahead of her</u>.
+ **speed** 以……的速度
  1. speed做不可数名词时，与at,with搭配均可
  ✎ <u>at/ with</u> great speed
  2. speed做可数名词时，只能与at搭配
  ✎ <u>at</u> a speed of 60 mph 以时速60英里
+ **tremendous** 极大的；巨大的
  ✎ In his day, Mendoza enjoyed <u>tremendous</u> popularity.（L21）
  ┏ at <u>tremendous</u> speed（原文）
  ┗ at (a) <u>fantastic</u> speed（L6）
+ **after**
  **时间 + before/ after** 在……之前/之后多长时间
  She arrived in England **a week after** the *Thermopylae*.（原文）
  ✎ <u>Four days</u> <u>after setting out</u>, while the Titanic……（L10）
  ✎ <u>Three days</u> <u>after Rastus’ disappearance</u>, Mrs Ramsay received an anonymous letter.（L19）
  ✎ A man who had broken his right leg was taken to hospital <u>a few weeks</u> <u>before Christmas</u>.（L29）
+ **considering** prep. conj. 考虑到
  作介词（+ n.）
  ✎ <u>Considering</u> the amount she paid, he was dear in more ways than one!（L19）
  作连词（加不加that都行）
  ✎ Even this was remarkable, <u>considering (that)</u> she had had so many delays.（原文：作复合连词，有没有that都行）
+ **there is no doubt that……** 毫无疑问的是……
  ✎ <u>There’s no doubt that</u> one day a cure will be found. 毫无疑问，有朝一日会找到治愈的方法。
  同义替换：
  **undoubtedly** 毫无疑问地
  ✎ She was <u>undoubtedly</u> the best candidate. 她毫无疑问是最佳的候选人。
  ✎ <u>Undoubtedly</u>, public interest in folk music has declined. 毫无疑问，公众对民间音乐的兴趣已经下降。
  **needless to say,……** 不用说也能知道……
  ✎ <u>Needless to say,</u> the man’s name was Hans Bussman and he really was Franz’s long-lost brother.（L36）
  ✎ <u>Needless to say,</u> the bigger the risk an insurance company takes, the higher the premium you will have to pay.（L43）
  **it goes without saying that……** 无需多言
  ✎ <u>It goes without saying that</u> home is the warmest place in the world. 不用说，家是世界上最温暖的地方。
  ✎ <u>It goes without saying that</u> a real sportsman will never dream of cheating in a game. 不用说，一个真正的运动员是绝不会梦想在比赛中作弊的。
+ **If + S. + had done, S. + <u>would/ should/ could/ might</u> + have done**
  与过去事实相反的“if”型的虚拟语气（详见L17笔记）
+ 【✔】…… won the race（原文）
  【✘】…… won the *Thermopylae*
  【✔】…… beaten/ defeated the *Thermopylae*
  对输赢的表达（参见L21）
> 仿写末句
  毫无疑问，如果泰坦尼克号没有撞到冰山，她将抵达目的地而毫发无伤(intact)。
  <u>There is no doubt that</u> if the Titanic <u>had not been hit</u> by the iceberg, she <u>would have reached</u> her destination intact.

---

## **Lesson 26 - Wanted: a large biscuit tin**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>No one can avoid being influenced by advertisements. Much as we may pride ourselves on our good taste, we are no longer free to choose the things we want, for advertising exerts a subtle influence on us. In their efforts to persuade us to buy this or that product, advertisers have made a close study of human nature and have classified all our little weaknesses.

Advertisers discovered years ago that all of us love to get something for nothing. An advertisement which begins with the magic word FREE can rarely go wrong. These days, advertisers not only offer free samples, but free cars, free houses, and free trips round the world as well. They devise hundreds of competitions which will enable us to win huge sums of money. Radio and television have made it possible for advertisers to capture the attention of millions of people in this way.

During a radio programme, a company of biscuit manufacturers once asked listeners to bake biscuits and send them to their factory. They offered to pay ＄10 a pound for the biggest biscuit baked by a listener. The response to this competition was tremendous. Before long, biscuits of all shapes and sizes began arriving at the factory. One lady brought in a biscuit on a wheelbarrow. It weighed nearly 500 pounds. A little later, a man came along with a biscuit which occupied the whole boot of his car. All the biscuits that were sent were carefully weighed. The largest was 713 pounds. It seemed certain that this would win the prize. But just before the competition closed, a lorry arrived at the factory with a truly colossal biscuit which weighed 2,400 pounds. It had been baked by a college student who had used over 1,000 pounds of flour, 800 pounds of sugar, 200 pounds of fat, and 400 pounds of various other ingredients. It was so heavy that a crane had to be used to remove it from the lorry. The manufacturers had to pay more money than they had anticipated, for they bought the biscuit from the student for ＄24,000.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **influence** n. 影响
  **the influence of…… <u>on/ upon</u>……** （前者）对（后者）的影响
  ✎ <u>the influence of</u> parents <u>on/ upon</u> their children 父母对其子女的影响
  同义替换：
  **the effect of…… <u>on/ upon</u>……**
  ✎ <u>the effect of</u> fertilizers <u>on/ upon</u> the crops 肥料对庄稼的影响
  **the impact of…… <u>on/ upon</u>……**
  ✎ <u>the impact of</u> the oil spill <u>on/ upon</u> marine life 石油泄漏对海洋生物的影响（life 表示生命、生物时不可数）
+ **pride** v. 骄傲（参见L24）
  **be proud of……** a.
  **take pride in……** n.
  **pride oneself on……** v.
+ **taste** n.[U] 鉴赏力，品味
  ✎ a man/ woman of <u>taste</u> 一个有品位的男人/女人
  **have……taste in……** 在……方面有品位
  ✎ She <u>has</u> good <u>taste in</u> music. 她在音乐方面很有品味。
  ✎ He <u>has</u> terrible <u>taste in</u> clothing. 他在衣着方面的品味非常糟糕。
  **tasteless** a. 无品味的，粗俗的
+ **exert** v. 施加
  **exert…… on……** 对……施加……
  ✎ My wife <u>exerts</u> a lot of pressure <u>on</u> me to make more money. 我妻子给我施加了很大的压力，让我赚更多的钱。
  ✎ ……, for advertising <u>exerts</u> a subtle influence <u>on</u> us.（本文）
  ✎ Antique shops <u>exert</u> a peculiar fascination <u>on</u> a great many people.（L34）
  近义搭配：
  **impose sth. on sb.** 对某人强加某物
  ✎ Some parents <u>impose</u> their own moral values <u>on</u> their children. 有些父母把自己的道德价值观强加给孩子。
  **inflict sth. on sb.** 把令人痛苦的事情强加到某人身上（比上例语气更重）
  ✎ Please don’t <u>inflict</u> your love <u>on</u> me. 请不要把你的爱强加给我。
+ **devise** v. 设计出，想出，构思出
  ✎ The cartoon character Mickey Mouse <u>was devised</u> by Walt Disney in 1928. 卡通人物米老鼠是由沃尔特·迪斯尼于1928年设计的。
  近义词：
  **conceive** 想出；怀孕
  **come up with** 想出来
  ✎ M: What had they decided to call the stadium? 他们决定给体育场取什么名字？
  W: No one has <u>come up with</u> a good name. 没有人想出一个好名字。
  Q: What does the woman say about the stadium?
  Answer: A good name hasn’t been found for it.（托福听力真题）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **wanted**
  + 诚聘，求购
    **help wanted section** 招聘启示专栏
    ✎ W: Since when do you read the Sunday Times?
    M: Since I discovered its big <u>help-wanted section</u>. 自从我发现了它的大招聘专栏。
    Q: What can be assumed about the man? 关于这个人，我们可以推测出什么？
    Answer: He’s interested in finding a job. 他对找工作感兴趣。（托福听力真题）
  + 通缉某人
    ✎ The fugitive <u>is wanted by</u> the police. 这名逃犯正被警方通缉。
+ **avoid** v. 躲避，避免
  **avoid sb. like the plague** 像躲避瘟疫一样躲避某人
  **avoid doing** 躲避做某事
> 仿写第1句
  没有人可以避免受到社会的影响。
  No one can <u>avoid being influenced</u> by society.
  没有人可以避免受到金钱的引诱。
  No one can <u>avoid being tempted</u> by money.
  没有人可以避免犯错误。
  No one can <u>avoid making</u> mistakes.
+ ┏ No one can avoid being influenced by advertisements.（原文：双重否定，语气更强）
  ┗ Everyone is influenced by advertisements.
  ┏ No one can deny that…… 没有人否认……
  ┗ Everyone admits that…… 每个人都承认……
  ┏ No one can resist…… 没有人能抵制……的诱惑/不受吸引
  ┗ Everyone is attracted by…… 每个人都被……所吸引
+ **pride oneself on……** 对……很自豪（正式）
  **take pride in……**（正式）
  **be proud of……**（通俗）
+ ┏ <u>Much</u> <u>as</u> we may pride ourselves on our good taste,……（原文：副词much得到了强调）
  ┗ <u>Although</u> we may <u>much</u> pride ourselves on our good taste,……（普通让步）
  **让步状语从句的强调**
  此种强调仅用于书面语！！！
  + 强调副词
    **将被强调的副词放到句首取代连词，其后再加as，其它部分顺序不变。**
    ┏ <u>Much</u> <u>as</u> I admire Newton as a scientist, I don’t like him as a man.（强调副词much）
    ┗ <u>Although</u> I <u>much</u> admire Newton as a scientist, I don’t like him as a man.
    尽管牛顿作为科学家我钦佩他，但作为人来说，我不喜欢他。
  + 强调形容词
    **将被强调的形容词词放到句首取代连词，其后再加as，其它部分顺序不变。**
    ┏ <u>Proud</u> <u>as</u> we may be of our good taste,……（强调形容词proud）
    ┗ <u>Although</u> we may be <u>proud</u> of our good taste,……（原文换用）
    ┏ <u>Beautiful</u> <u>as</u> she is, I still don’t like her.（强调形容词beautiful）
    ┗ <u>Although</u> she is <u>beautiful</u>, I still don’t like her.
  + 强调动词
    **将动词原形放句首取代连词，其后再加as，原来动词的位置用助动词代替，其它部分顺序不变。**
    ┏ <u>Try</u> <u>as</u> he <u>does</u>, he never seems to do the work beautifully.（强调谓语动词try）
    ┗ <u>Although</u> he <u>tries</u>, he never seems able to do the work beautifully.
    尽管他努力了，但他似乎永远也无法把工作漂亮地完成。
  + 强调名词
    **将名词放句首取代连词，删掉冠词，其后再加as，其它部分顺序不变。**
    ┏ <u>Child</u> <u>as</u> he is, he can make a living.（强调名词child）
    ┗ <u>Although</u> he is <u>a child</u>, he can make a living. 
    尽管他是个孩子，但已经能够谋生了。
+ **be free to do……** 自由地/随意地做某事
  ✎ You <u>are free to</u> choose the things you want. 你可以自由选择你想要的东西。
  + 近义表达：
    **freely**
    ✎ You can choose the things you want <u>freely</u>.
    **be at liberty to do**
    ✎ You <u>are at liberty to</u> choose the things you want.
+ ┏ advertisements [C] 广告
  ┗ advertising [U] 广告宣传
+ **in sth./ doing** 在……的过程中
  ✎ <u>In trying</u> to persuade us to buy……（原文改）
  ✎ <u>In seeking</u> independence, they do not sacrifice their human dignity.（L27）
+ **persuade sb. <u>to do/ into doing</u> sth.** 说服某人做某事
  + 近义替换：
    **talk sb. into doing**
    ✎ We <u>talked</u> Father <u>into</u> buying the car. 我们说服爸爸买了这辆车。（Father大写之后表示称谓，不用再加冠词和属格）
    **get sb. to do**
    ✎ The rough road across the plain soon became so bad that we tried to <u>get</u> Bruce <u>to</u> drive back to the village we had come from.（L39）
  + 反义搭配：
    **persuade sb. <u>not to do/ out of doing</u>**
    **talk sb. out of doing**
    **get sb. not to do**
    **dissuade sb. from doing**
    ┏ 我劝他不要自杀。（commit 表示做错事/傻事）
    ┗ I <u>persuaded</u> him <u>not to commit/ out of committing</u> suicide. 
    ┗ I <u>talked</u> him <u>out of committing</u> suicide.
    ┗ I <u>got</u> him <u>not to commit</u> suicide.
    ┗ I <u>dissuaded</u> him <u>from committing</u> suicide.
+ ┏ **this or that** product 这个或那个；各种各样的
  ┗ **one** product **or another**
  ┗ **some** product **or other** 某个商品或别的
  ✎ In their efforts to persuade us to buy <u>some product or other</u>,…… （课后题-9）
+ **study……** 研究……
  **make a study of……** 对……做研究（名词结构）
  ✎ make a close study of…… 对……做仔细的研究
  ✎ Recently the New York Animal Medical Center <u>made a study of</u> 132 cats over a period of five months.（L9）
  + 相同变化举例：
    **discover**
    ✎ make an interesting discovery of…… 做出一个有趣的发现
    ✎ Some time ago, <u>an interesting discovery was made</u> by archaeologists on the Aegean island of Kea.（L3）
    ***describe**
    ✎ make a vivid description of…… 对……做生动的描述
    **investigate**
    ✎ make a thorough investigation of…… 对……做彻底的调查
    **summarize**
    ✎ make a comprehensive summary of…… 对……做全面的总结
    **analyze**
    ✎ make a detailed analysis of…… 对……做细致的分析
+ **weakness**
  1. n. [U] 懦弱，软弱
    ✎ So let us begin anew —— remembering on both sides that civility is not <u>a sign of weakness</u>, and sincerity is always subject to proof. Let us never negotiate out of fear, but let us never fear to negotiate.（John F.Kennedy就职演说）
  2. n. [C] 弱点，缺点
    + 反义词：
      **strength** n. [C] 优点，长处；[U] 力量
      **strength and weakness** 优缺点
      ✎ For we know that our patchwork heritage is <u>a strength</u>, not <u>a weakness</u>. We are a nation of Christians and Muslims, Jews and Hindus, and nonbelievers.
      因为我们知道，我们打补丁的文化遗产是一种优势，而不是劣势。我们是一个由基督徒、穆斯林、犹太人、印度教徒和无宗教信仰者组成的国家。（奥巴马就职演说）
+ **for nothing/ for free/ free of charge** ad. 免费……
  ✎ Guests can park <u>for nothing/ for free/ free of charge</u>. 客人可以免费停车
  **no charge for……** 某物免费
  ✎ There is <u>no charge for</u> parking.
  ✎ **be on the house** 店主请客
  ✎ —— How much do I owe you? 我该付你多少钱？
  —— Well, that’ll be eighteen dollars and seventy cents. <u>No charge for</u> the cleanup. It<u>’s on the house</u>. 擦车免费，本店请客。（《走遍美国》）
+ **begin with……** 以……开始
  ✎ —— Let’s go into the kitchen, and maybe you can help me set the table.
  —— Sounds good to me. What are we having?
  —— I prepared lamb chops, mashed potatoes, and a tossed green salad to <u>begin with</u>.
  —— Grandpa, you are a terrific guy!（《走遍美国》）
  + 反义词：
    **end with……** 以……来结束
    ✎ The rally <u>ended with</u> the singing of national anthem. 大会以唱国歌结束。
+ **go wrong** 出错，出问题，不顺利
  ✎ Something’s <u>gone wrong</u> with my computer. 我的电脑出故障了。（’s = has）
  ✎ We have all experienced days when everything <u>goes wrong</u>.（L33）
+ **<u>round[英]/ around[美]</u> the world** 世界各地
  + 同义搭配：
    **throughout the world**
    **all over the world**
    **the world over**

  ✎ Michael Jackson was popular <u>~</u> . 迈克尔杰克逊在世界各地都很流行。
+ **enable sb. to do……** 使某人能够做某事
  **= make it possible for sb. to do……**
  ✎ They devise hundreds of competitions which will <u>enable</u> us <u>to</u> win huge sums of money. Radio and television have <u>made it possible for</u> advertisers <u>to</u> capture the attention of millions of people in this way.（原文）
  ✎ Radio and television have <u>enabled</u> advertisers <u>to</u> capture the attention of millions of people in this way.（上例第2句换用）
+ **<u>capture/ attract/ draw/ catch/ arrest/ command/ get</u> <u>(one’s) attention/ the attention of……</u>** 吸引某人的注意力（L21）
  ✎ This <u>attracted the attention of</u> Richard Humphries who was then the most eminent boxer in England.（L21）
  ✎ True eccentrics never deliberately set out to <u>draw attention</u> to themselves.（L31）
+ 不同的“烤”的表达
  + **bake** 烤（多指用烤箱烤饼干或面包，不指烤鸭等）
    **baker** 面包师；**baker’s/ bakery** 面包房
  + **roast** 烤（用烤箱来烤肉）
    ✎ <u>roast</u> turkey 烤火鸡
    ✎ Peking <u>roast</u> duck 北京烤鸭
  + **grill/ broil[英]** 烤（在烤架、铁板上烤）
    ✎ <u>grilled/ broiled</u> chicken 烤鸡
  + **barbecue (BBQ)** 烤（户外，尤指野营时）
+ **offer to do** 主动提出
+ pay ＄10 a pound **for** the biggest biscuit 介词**for**表示**等价交换**
  ┏ She paid me ＄30 <u>for</u> my bike.
  ┗ She bought my bike <u>for</u> ＄30.
  ✎ Advertisers discovered years ago that all of us love to get something <u>for</u> nothing.（本文）（**for nothing** 免费）
  ✎ The manufacturers had to pay more money than they had anticipated, for they bought the biscuit from the student <u>for</u> $24,000.（本文）
+ **the response to…… <u>is/ was</u> <u>tremendous/ lukewarm</u>** 对……反响很热烈/平淡
  ✎ The university offered a prize of $1,000 to the first student who would find a solution to the problem. <u>The response to</u> the competition <u>was tremendous/ lukewarm</u>. 学校提供了一笔1000美元的奖金给第一个能解决这个问题的学生。大家对这次比赛的反应很热烈/很平淡。
+ **before (very/ too) long** 不久之后
  **= before much longer**
  **= shortly afterwards**
  **= a little later** 
  **= after a <u>little/ short</u> <u>time/ while</u>**
  ✎ <u>Shortly afterwards</u>, the police stopped the car and both men were arrested.（B2L35）
  ✎ <u>A little later</u>, a man came along with a biscuit which occupied the whole boot of his car.（本文）
  ✎ <u>After a little time</u>, she chose one of the most expensive dresses in the shop and handed it to an assistant who wrapped it up for her as quickly as possible.（B2L32）
+ biscuits of **all** shapes and sizes 各种，~~全部~~
  **all <u>sorts/ kinds/ types</u> of sth.** 各种各样的某物
  ✎ He added that a student had dressed up as a policeman and was playing <u>all sorts of silly jokes</u> on people.（L40）
  ✎ She has to deal with <u>all kinds of complaints</u> every day. 她每天必须要处理各种各样的投诉/抱怨。
+ **weigh……**
  It <u>weighed</u> nearly 500 pounds.（weight 作系动词，译为有多重，~~称……的重量~~。后面用数量词作表语）（原文）
  ✎ The boy <u>weighs</u> 50 kilos. 这个男孩有50公斤重。
  + 近义搭配：
    **be…… (in weight)**（较上者通俗）
    ✎ The boy <u>is</u> 50 kilos <u>(in weight)</u>.
  + 相关搭配：
    **<u>be/ stand</u>…… <u>high/ tall</u>** 有多高（L3）
    ✎ She <u>stood</u> three feet <u>high</u> and her hands rested on her hips.（L3）
    ✎ He <u>stands/ is</u> 1.8m <u>tall</u>. 他有一米八高。
    **rise to a height of……** 高达……（暗指特别高）（L17）
    ✎ Above the surface of the water, the towers <u>rise to a height of</u> nearly 700 feet.（L17）
    **be…… <u>deep/ in depth</u>** 有多深
    ✎ The hole <u>is</u> 2 feet <u>deep/ in depth</u>. 这个洞有两英尺深。
    **extend to a depth of……** 深达……（强调特别深）
    ✎ The platforms <u>extend to a depth of</u> over 100 feet under the sea.（L17）
    **be…… <u>long/ in length</u>** 有多长
    ✎ The bed <u>is</u> 2 meters <u>long/ in length</u>. 这张床有2米长。
    **be…… <u>wide/ across/ in width</u>** 有多宽
    ✎ The river <u>is</u> 20 meters <u>wide/ across/ in width</u>. 这条河有20米宽。
+ **along with……** 与……在一起
  ✎ Mr. Taylor, <u>along with</u> two assistants, <u>is</u> trying to stop the thieves. 泰勒先生和两名助手一起，正试图阻止小偷。（主语是“Mr. Taylor”，“along with two assistants”修饰主语。谓语动词对应主语，用单数。）
  同类词（修饰主语，不算到主语里）：
  **together with……** 在一起的还有…… ；**coupled with……** 再加上……
  **accompanied by……** 被……所陪伴
  **followed by……** 跟着……
  **besides……** 除了……之外 ；**as well as……** 除了……之外还有
  **no less than……** 某人也…… ；**including……** 也
+ ┏ The largest <u>was</u> 713 pounds <u>(in weight)</u>.（原文）
  ┗ The largest <u>weighed</u> 713 pounds.（换用系动词表达）
> 仿写最后1段倒数第2句（英文被动 → 中文主动）：
  ┏ 箱子太沉了，用了一辆卡车才把它运到目的地。
  ┗ The box was so heavy that a lorry had to be used to carry it to the destination.
  ┏ 两年多来这条街上新开了很多商店。
  ┗ In the past two years many shops have been set up in the street.
  ┏ A new government was organized after the war.
  ┗ 战后成立了新政府。

---

## **Lesson 27 - Nothing to sell and nothing to buy**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>It has been said that everyone lives by selling something. In the light of this statement, teachers live by selling knowledge, philosophers by selling wisdom and priests by selling spiritual comfort. Though it may be possible to measure the value of material goods in terms of money, it is extremely difficult to estimate the true value of the services which people perform for us. There are times when we would willingly give everything we possess to save our lives, yet we might grudge paying a surgeon a high fee for offering us precisely this service. The conditions of society are such that skills have to be paid for in the same way that goods are paid for at a shop. Everyone has something to sell.

Tramps seem to be the only exception to this general rule. Beggars almost sell themselves as human beings to arouse the pity of passers-by. But real tramps are not beggars. They have nothing to sell and require nothing from others. In seeking independence, they do not sacrifice their human dignity. A tramp may ask you for money, but he will never ask you to feel sorry for him. He has deliberately chosen to lead the life he leads and is fully aware of the consequences. He may never be sure where the next meal is coming from, but he is free from the thousands of anxieties which afflict other people. His few material possessions make it possible for him to move from place to place with ease. By having to sleep in the open, he gets far closer to the world of nature than most of us ever do. He may hunt, beg, or steal occasionally to keep himself alive; he may even, in times of real need, do a little work; but he will never sacrifice his freedom. We often speak of tramps with contempt and put them in the same class as beggars, but how many of us can honestly say that we have not felt a little envious of their simple way of life and their freedom from care?</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ ┏ **philosopher** n. 哲学家
  ┗ **philosophy** 哲学
  + 词根1：**phil** = love
    ┏ <u>phil</u>ology 语文学；语言学（**log(y)** = speech）
    ┗ <u>phil</u>ologist 语文学家；语言学家
  + 词根2：**soph** = wisdom
    ┏ <u>soph</u>omore 大二学生
    ┗ <u>soph</u>isticated (指人)老练的，经验丰富的；(指机器)精密的，高级的
+ **spiritual** a. 精神的
  ┏ <u>spiritual</u> civilization 精神文明
  ┗ <u>material</u> civilization 物质文明
  + 易混词：
    ┏ **mental** 脑力上的（L4） ✎ <u>mental</u> labor 脑力劳动
    ┗ **manual/ physical** 体力的，手工的 ✎ <u>~</u> labor
    **intellectual** 智力方面的 ✎ <u>intellectual</u> development 智力的发展
    **intelligent** 聪明的，智商高的 ✎ <u>intelligent</u> beings 智慧生物
+ **grudge**
  + v. 吝惜，不愿意给
    **grudge + <u>n./ doing</u>**
    ┏ He <u>grudges</u> paying taxes. 他不愿意纳税。
    ┗ He <u>grudges</u> the money he pays in tax.
  + a. **grudging** 勉强的，不情愿的
    同义词：**reluctant, unwilling**
  + n. 恶意，怨恨
    **<u>have/ bear/ hold</u> a grudge** 怀恨在心
    ✎ W: I wish I hadn’t hurt Mary’s feelings like that. You know I’ve never meant to.
    M: The great thing about Mary is that she doesn’t <u>hold a grudge</u>. By tomorrow she’ll have forgotten all about it.
    Q: What does the man say about Mary?
    Answer: She’s quick to forgive people.（托福听力）
+ **dignity** n. 尊严
  **beneath one’s dignity** 有失尊严
  ✎ Arguing with you is <u>beneath my dignity</u>. 跟你争执，有失我的尊严。
  **self-respect, self-esteem** 自尊(心)
  + 同根词：
    **indignity** 侮辱
    近义词：**shame, disgrace, humiliation**
  + 形近词：
    **indignation** 气愤，愤慨
    近义词：**anger, rage, fury**
+ **deliberately** ad. 故意地
  同义词：
  **intentionally, on purpose**
  （intention 目的，意图；intentional 有意的）
  反义词（意外地，偶然地，无预谋地）：
  **accidentally, by accident, by chance, unintentionally, fortuitously**
+ **afflict** v. 使苦恼，折磨
  **afflict sb.** 使某人苦恼/痛苦
  **be afflicted <u>with/ by</u>** 因为某事而痛苦
  ✎ He <u>was afflicted with/ by</u> his injured leg. 他因为腿受伤而痛苦。
  ✎ He <u>was afflicted with/ by</u> the death of his wife. 他因为妻子的去世而难受。
  + 形近词：
    ◇ **inflict** vt. 使遭受打击；使吃苦头
    **inflict sth. on sb.** 把令人痛苦的事强加到某人身上（L26）
    ✎ Please don’t <u>inflict</u> your love <u>on</u> me. 请不要把你的爱强加给我。
    ◇ **conflict** n. 冲突，矛盾，分歧，不和
    **in conflict** 有矛盾，有冲突
    ✎ The employers and workers are still <u>in conflict</u>. 雇主和工人之间仍然存在冲突。
  + 相关表达（某人因为某事而痛苦，某事令某人很痛苦）：
    **sb. suffer (from) sth.**（L9）
    **sth. distress sb.**（多指精神上的痛苦）
    **sth. <u>torture/ torment/ rack</u> sb.**
    ✎ God Almighty, where are you when the world <u>is racked by</u> war? 全能的上帝，当世界被战争折磨时，你在哪里？（人作主语时，用被动即可）
+ **ease** n. 容易；舒适
  容易 **with ease = easily**
  ✎ He passed the exam <u>with ease</u>. 他轻而易举地通过了考试。
  舒适 **at ease = in comfort = comfortably**
  ✎ He sat there <u>at ease</u>. 他舒服地坐在那里。
+ **contempt**
  + n. 蔑视，鄙视
  **hold…… in contempt** 鄙视某人（L23）
  + a. **contemptuous** 轻蔑的，鄙夷的
  + v. 蔑视，鄙视，瞧不起（contempt 无同根动词，以下列举同义词）
  **despise, scorn, look down on upon……**
+ **envious** a. 羡慕的(较常用)；嫉妒的(不常用)
  **be envious of……** 对……很羡慕/嫉妒
  **envy** v./n.
  ✎ You lucky dog, I <u>envy</u> you. 你真是个幸运儿，我真羡慕你。（v.）
  ✎ You are my <u>envy</u>. 你真是我羡慕的对象。（n.）
  ✎ His talent <u>is the envy of</u> his colleagues. 他的才华是他同事们羡慕的对象。/ 他的同事们都羡慕他的才华。
  + 近义词：
    **jealous** 嫉妒的
    **be jealous of……** 对……嫉妒
    **jealousy** n. 嫉妒


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **“据说”，“……的是”**
  **It is said that……**（本文用的完成时，表示对现在仍有影响）
  **They say that……**
  **People say that……**
  It is reported that…… 据报道……
  It is believed that…… 据信……
  It is estimated that 据估计……
  It must be admitted that…… 必须要承认的是……
  It must be pointed out that…… 必须要指出的是……
  It must be stressed that…… 必须要强调的是……
  It can be foreseen that…… 可以预见到的是……
+ **live by doing** 靠某种职业为生
  ✎ He <u>lives by</u> writing. 他靠写作为生。
  ✎ He <u>lives by</u> sewing. 他靠缝纫为生。
  ✎ The nomads who made these markings <u>lived by hunting and fishing</u> during the last Ice Age which began about 35,000 B.C. and ended about 10,000 B.C.（L38）
  + 辨：
    **live on sth.** 靠某种食物或生活来源为生（指人）
    ✎ He <u>lives on</u> meat and milk. 他靠吃肉和牛奶为生。
    ✎ He <u>lives on</u> salary. 他靠工资为生。
    ✎ He <u>lives on</u> his parents. 他靠父母为生。
    **feed on sth.** 动物以……为主食（泛指人以外的动物）
    ✎ Cows <u>feed on</u> hay. 奶牛以干草为食。
    **prey on sth.** 肉食性动物以别的动物为食（指肉食动物）
    ✎ Owls <u>prey on</u> mice. 猫头鹰捕食老鼠。
+ **in (the) light of sth.** 根据……；鉴于……（美式英语一般去掉the）
  ✎ Reading is thought to be a kind of conversation between the reader and the text. The reader puts questions, as it were, to the text and gets answers. <u>In the light of</u> these he puts further questions, and so on.
  阅读被认为是类似于读者与文本之间的一种对话。读者好像是在向文本提问并得到答案。根据这些答案，他再提出更深入的问题，等等。（四级阅读真题）（as it were 好像是，仿佛是，可谓是）
  ✎ He explores such problem consciously, articulately,and frankly, first by asking factual questions, then by asking moral questions,finally by suggesting action which seems appropriate <u>in the light of</u> the factual and moral information which he has obtained.
  他有意识地、条理清晰地、坦诚地钻研这个问题，首先通过提出有关事实的问题，然后提出有关道德的问题，最后根据他获得的有关事实和道德方面的信息提出看似比较恰当的行动建议。（2006考研英语真题-英译汉）
  ✎ I am afraid that you have to alter your <u>(C)optimistic</u> views <u>in light of</u> the tragic news that has just arrived.
  (A) indifferent；(B) distressing；(C) optimistic；(D) pessimistic（六级-单选）
  + 同义搭配：
    **according to sth.**
    **in accordance with sth.**
    **considering sth.**
    **taking into account sth.**
+ In the light of this statement, teachers <u>live by</u> selling knowledge, philosophers <u>(live) by</u> selling wisdom **and** priests <u>(live) by</u> selling spiritual comfort.
  **并列句中，重复的谓语动词一般可去掉，但介词不可去掉。**
  ✎ Mary was happy, <u>but/ and/ while/ whereas</u> Jane <u>(was)</u> miserable.
  ✎ Mary was happy <u>when</u> Jane <u>was</u> miserable.（主从句，不可去掉）
+ parallelism 排比
  ✎ Some books <u>are</u> to be tasted, others to be swallowed, and some few to be chewed and digested. —— Francis Bacon
  有些书应该浅尝即可，其他书应该囫囵吞下，只有少数书应该咀嚼和消化。（弗朗西斯·培根《论读书》）
  ✎ Reading <u>makes</u> a full man, conference a ready man, and writing an exact man. 读书使人充实，讨论使人机敏，写作使人精确。（弗朗西斯·培根《论读书》）
  ✎ It is said that in England <u>death is</u> pressing, in Canada <u>(death is)</u> inevitable and in California <u>(death is)</u> optional. Small wonder. Americans’life expectancy has nearly doubled over the past century. Failing hips <u>can be</u> replaced, clinical depression (<u>can be</u>) controlled, cataracts (<u>can be</u>) removed in a 30-minutes surgical procedure.
  据说，在英国，死亡是迫在眉睫的，在加拿大，死亡是不可避免的，而在加利福尼亚，死亡则是可选择的。难怪。在过去的一个世纪里，美国人的预期寿命几乎翻了一番。髋关节坏了可以更换，临床抑郁症可以被控制，白内障可以在30分钟的手术中被摘除。（2003考研真题片段-阅读）
+ **in terms of……** 以某种方式；从某个角度
  ✎ <u>In terms of</u> money we’re rich, but not <u>in terms of</u> happiness. 从金钱这个角度，我们很富有，但不是从幸福这个角度。
  ✎ Which sport has the most expenses <u>(B) in terms of</u> training equipment, players personal equipment and uniforms?
  (A) in place of；(B) in terms of；(C) by means of；(D) by way of（四级-单选）
+ **perform**: do; carry out 做
+ **there are times when…… = sometimes** 有时候（详见L14）
  ✎ <u>There are times when</u> even the tiger sleeps. 老虎也有打盹的时候。
  ✎ <u>There are times when</u> silence has the loudest voice. 有时候，沉默是最响亮的声音。
+ ┏ …… we might <u>grudge paying a surgeon a high fee</u> for offering us precisely this service.（原文：grudge + doing）
  ┗ …… we might <u>grudge the high fee we would pay a surgeon</u> for offering us precisely this service.（grudge + n.）
> 仿写第4句
  有时候我们愿意给为我们服务的侍者小费(pay tips)并称赞(pay compliments)他们，但是在母亲为我们提供一样的服务的时候我们却吝惜感谢(give thanks to……)之辞。
  There are times when we would willingly pay tips and compliments to the waiters who serve us, yet we might grudge giving thanks to our mothers for offering us precisely this service.
+ …… the same way **in which**……（最正式）（which为关系代词，指代way）
  …… the same way **that**……（that为关系副词）
  …… the same way **/**……
> 仿写第5句
  学校里的情况就是这样，优等生(A students)受到尊敬(respect)，正如社会上成功者(achievers)受人景仰(esteem)一样。
  The conditions of schools are such that A students are respected in the same way that achievers are esteemed in the society.
+ **“正如”**
  **in the same way that……**（本文）
  **just as** 和……一样；正如……
  ✎ The conditions of society are such that skills have to be paid for <u>just as</u> goods are paid for at a shop.（原文换用）
  **alike** 一样地……
  ✎ He was adored by rich and poor <u>alike</u>.（L21）
  **six of one and half a dozen of the other** 半斤八两（习语）
  ✎ W: I can’t decide whether to take anthropology or geology this term.
  M: It's <u>six of one and half a dozen of the other</u>.
  Q: What does the man mean?
  Answer: It doesn’t matter which class the woman takes.（托福听力真题）
  **be equivalent to** 相当于……；与……相当
  ✎ The volcanic eruption had an explosive power <u>equivalent to</u> 20,000 tons of TNT. 火山爆发的爆炸力相当于20000吨TNT。
  **bear a resemblance to……** 像……；跟……很类似
  ✎ Tina <u>bears a striking resemblance to</u> her mother. 缇娜跟她妈妈特别像。
  ✎ Your school may have done away with winners and losers,but life has not. In some schools they have abolished failing grades; they’ll give you as many times as you want to get the right answer. This <u>doesn’t bear the slightest resemblance to</u> anything in real life.
  你的学校可能已经废除了赢家和输家，但生活并没有。在一些学校，他们废除了不及格的成绩；他们会给你想要多少就有多少的机会来得到正确的答案。这与现实生活中的任何事情都没有丝毫相似之处。（比尔盖茨给年轻人的10条生活准则-最后一条）
+ 第1段总结
  + 首句和末句对应。
  + 本段大致层次：
    topic sentence 主题句
    supporting sentences 扩展句（论证和论据）
    concluding sentence 总结句
  + 上下句之间逻辑相连贯。
+ ┏ Tramps **seem to be** the only exception to this general rule.（原文）
  ┗ Tramps **appear to be** the only exception to this general rule.
  ┗ **It seems that** tramps are the only exception to this general rule.
  ┗ **It appears that** tramps are the only exception to this general rule.
+ exception
  **exception to** ……的例外（本文）
  ✎ Every rule has its <u>exception</u>. 任何规律都有例外。（谚语）
  **with the exception of……** 除了……之外
  ✎ I like all kinds of films <u>with the exception of</u> horror films. 除了恐怖电影之外，我喜欢各种各样的电影。
+ Beggars sell their human dignity **for** the pity of passers-by.（原文同义表达）
  The moment they reach out their hands they are beggars spiritually. 他们伸手的那一刻，精神上就成了乞丐。
+ **in doing = in the process of doing** 在做某事的过程中（L22、L26）
  ✎ <u>In</u> trying to solve one problem, I created another. 在设法解决一个问题过程中，我又想出了另一个问题。
  **<u>on/ upon</u> doing** 刚一……就……（类似as soon as）
  ✎ <u>On</u> being observed, it immediately ran away.（L1课后题-6）
  ✎ <u>Upon</u> arriving at the university, I went straight to the dormitory. 刚一到学校，我直接去了宿舍。
+ **seek** 追求，寻求，想得到（书面语）
  ✎ <u>seek</u> refuge/ asylum 寻求避难（refuge/ asylum 此处不可数，但表示**避难所**时可数）
  ✎ <u>seek</u> compensation 寻求补偿
  ✎ <u>seek</u> comfort 寻求安慰
  ✎ <u>seek</u> reelection 寻求连任
  ✎ Virgo woman <u>seeks</u> Scorpio man 处女座女生求偶天蝎男生
+ **feel sorry for……** 同情……，怜悯……，~~觉得遗憾，觉得对不起~~（习语）
  ✎ Even the bull seemed to <u>feel sorry for</u> him, for it looked on sympathetically until the drunk was out of the way before once more turning its attention to the matador.（B2L70）
  + 同义搭配：
    **<u>have/ feel</u> sympathy for……**（L24）
    **sympathize with……**（L24）
    **take pity on……**（L18）
+ He has deliberately chosen to **lead** the life he **leads**……（原文）
  加强语气，未同义替换
  ✎ We only <u>help</u> those who really need <u>help</u>. 我们只帮助那些真正需要帮助的人。
+ **be aware of……** 知道，明白，了解，清楚
  + 同义搭配：
    **be conscious of……**
  + 反义搭配：
    **be unaware of……**
    **be unconscious of……**
    **be ignorant of……**（略贬义，强调本来应该知道）
+ **be free from……** 没有……（某个不好的东西） ~~从……中自由出来~~
  ✎ He has <u>been free from</u> care since he retired. 他退休后就变得无忧无虑了。
  ✎ The composition <u>is free from</u> errors. 这篇作文没有错误。
  ✎ Organic produce <u>is free from</u> harmful chemicals. 有机农作物不含有害化学物质。（辨：produce [U] 农作物；product [C] 产品(一般用复数)）
  **free…… from……** 使（前者）没有（后者(不想要的东西)）
  ✎ …… but he <u>frees himself from</u> the thousands of anxieties……（原文换用）
  ✎ He dedicated his life to <u>freeing the world from</u> famine and disease. 他毕生致力于使世界摆脱饥荒和疾病。/他把一生的时间精力都献给了使世界没有饥荒和疾病。
+ ┏ …… which <u>afflict</u> other people.（原文）（afflict 折磨某人）
  ┗ …… which <u>distress</u> other people.
  ┗ …… which <u>torture/ rack/ torment</u> other people.
  ┗ …… which other people <u>suffer (from)</u>.
+ **make it possible for sb. to do = enable sb. to do**（L26）
+ **from place to place** 各处，四处（参见L25笔记）
  **= here and there**（习语）
  **= hither and thither**（偏文言）
  ✎ The *Cutty Sark* rolled <u>from side to side</u> and it became impossible to steer her.（L25）
  + 同结构搭配（前后不同词）：
    **from dawn to dusk** 从早到晚（固定搭配）
    **from head to foot** 从头到脚
    **from top to bottom** 从上到下
    **from start to finish** 从头到尾
    **from cradle to grave** 从生到死
+ **in the open (air)**: outdoors 在露天，在户外
+ …… than most of us (ever do).（原文）比较状语从句可以省略谓语动词。
  ┏ He is taller than <u>I am</u>.（未省略）
  ┗ He is taller than <u>I</u>.（省略）
  ┗ He is taller than <u>me</u>.（非正式场合）
+ **occasionally** 偶尔
  **= once in a while**（习语）
  **= from time to time**（习语）
+ **in times of……** 在……时候
  ✎ <u>in times of</u> happiness/ grief/ rage/ crisis/ boredom/ war/ peace/ ……
  ✎ <u>In times of peace</u>, when business was bad, Hawkwood and his men would march into a city-state and, after burning down a few farms, would offer to go away if protection money was paid to them.（L14）
+ ┏ We often speak of tramps <u>with contempt</u>……（原文）
  ┗ We often speak <u>contemptuously</u> of tramps……
+ **put…… in the same class as……** 把（某人某物）归到同一类别
  **= classify…… as……**
  ✎ …… and <u>classify</u> them <u>as</u> beggars.（原文换用）

#### **rhetorical question 修辞疑问句**
答在问中，不需要回答。常用于段落或文章末尾附近，增强文章表现力，引发读者思考。
✎ O, wind, if winter comes, can spring be far behind? —— P.B.Shelley ‘Ode to the West Wind’（雪莱《西风颂》）
✎ Who among us has not dreamed of that? 我们当中有谁没有梦想过那件事呢？
✎ What is the use of our studying grammar if we can’t put the grammatical rules into practice? 如果我们不能把语法规则运用到实际生活中去，那么我们学习语法又有什么用呢？
✎ Could any spectacle, for instance, be more grimly whimsical than that of gunners using science to shatter men’s bodies while, close at hand, surgeons use it to restore them? 难道有任何情景比方说比下面的情景更可怕更怪异吗？炮兵用科学把人体打碎，而近在咫尺处外科医生再用科学修复人体。（B4L22）

---

## **Lesson 28 - Five pounds too dear**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>Small boats loaded with wares sped to the great liner as she was entering the harbour. Before she had anchored, the men from the boats had climbed on board and the decks were soon covered with colourful rugs from Persia, silks from India, copper coffee pots, and beautiful handmade silverware. It was difficult not to be tempted. Many of the tourists on board had begun bargaining with the tradesmen, but I decided not to buy anything until I had disembarked.

I had no sooner got off the ship than I was assailed by a man who wanted to sell me a diamond ring. I had no intention of buying one, but I could not conceal the fact that I was impressed by the size of the diamonds. Some of them were as big as marbles. The man went to great lengths to prove that the diamonds were real. As we were walking past a shop, he held a diamond firmly against the window and made a deep impression in the glass. It took me over half an hour to get rid of him.

The next man to approach me was selling expensive pens and watches. I examined one of the pens closely. It certainly looked genuine. At the base of the gold cap, the words ‘made in the U.S.A.’ had been neatly inscribed. The man said that the pen was worth £50, but as a special favour, he would let me have it for £30. I shook my head and held up five fingers indicating that I was willing to pay £5. Gesticulating wildly, the man acted as if he found my offer outrageous, but he eventually reduced the price to £10. Shrugging my shoulders, I began to walk away when, a moment later, he ran after me and thrust the pen into my hands. Though he kept throwing up his arms in despair, he readily accepted the £5 I gave him. I felt especially pleased with my wonderful bargain — until I got back to the ship. No matter how hard I tried, it was impossible to fill this beautiful pen with ink and to this day it has never written a single word!</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **wares** n. 货物，商品（是泛指，所以必须带s）
  + **ware** n.[U] 某种产品（多用在复合名词里，由其构成的复合名词通通不可数）
    software 软件，hardware 硬件（这俩都不可数）
    silverware 银器，ironware 铁器，chinaware 瓷器，earthenware 陶器（都不可数）
  + 近义词：
    **goods，merchandise**
+ **anchor** v. 抛锚
  ┏ They <u>anchored</u> the ship in the harbor. 他们把船停泊在了港口。（及物）
  ┗ The ship <u>anchored</u> in the harbor.（不及物）
  + 同义表达：
    **<u>cast/ drop</u> anchor** 抛锚，停泊
  + 反义表达：
    **<u>weigh anchor/ set sail</u>** 起锚，启航
+ **tempt** v. 吸引，引诱（略贬义）（参见L9-fascinate）
  **tempt sb. to do sth.** 诱惑某人去做某事（一般指错事或傻事）
  **tempt sb. into doing sth.** 同上，更正式
  ┏ The serpent <u>tempted</u> Eve <u>to</u> pick the forbidden fruit.
  ┗ The serpent <u>tempted</u> Eve <u>into</u> picking the forbidden fruit.
  近义表达：
  **<u>lure/ seduce/ entice</u> sb. into doing sth.**
+ **bargain**
  + v. 讨价还价
    **bargain with sb. <u>over/ about</u> sth.** 关于某物与某人讨价还价
    ✎ He <u>bargained with</u> the vendor <u>over/ about</u> the price of the eggplants. 他与小贩就茄子的价格讨价还价。
    + 近义搭配；
      **haggle with sb. <u>over/ about</u> sth.**（语气更重）
      ✎ I know how to <u>haggle</u>. So let me handle this from here on out.（《老友记》）（from here on out 从现在开始 (口语)）
  + n. 便宜货 = buy n.
    ✎ Oh my! Here’s <u>a real buy</u>. It’s <u>a bargain</u>. This house just came on the market. 这个房子刚刚上市。（《走遍美国》）
+ **disembark** v. 下船，下飞机
  **disembark from……** 从（飞机/船）上下来
  ✎ The passengers <u>disembarked from</u> the ferry/ plane. 乘客下船/机登岸。
  + 反义词：
    **embark on……** 上（飞机/船）
    ✎ We <u>embarked on</u> the ship for Shanghai. 我们登船赴上海。（参见L10：for+目的地；from+出发地, to+目的地）
    **board**
    ✎ The couple <u>boarded</u> the train for New York. 这对夫妇登上了火车赴纽约。（及物）
    ✎ Flight No.714 is now <u>boarding</u> at Gate 8. 714号航班正在8号门登机。（不及物）
+ **assail** v. 纠缠，骚扰
  **be assailed <u>by/ with</u>……** 被……所纠缠
  ✎ He was <u>assailed by/ with</u> a street vendor. 他被街头小贩所纠缠。
  ✎ He was <u>assailed by/ with</u> worries. 他被烦恼所纠缠。
  + 同义替换：
    **pester, harry, harass**（这三个多表示人纠缠人，而非事纠缠人）
    ✎ …… than I <u>was pestered/ harried/ harassed by</u> a man who……（原文换用）
    ✎ From the moment he arrived there, he kept on <u>pestering</u> his doctor to tell him when he would be able to go home.（L29）
    ✎ sexual <u>harassment</u> 性骚扰（固定搭配）
+ **inscribe** v. 刻字；题写
  **inscribe in**
  ✎ He <u>inscribed</u> his name <u>in</u> the stone. 他在石头上刻了自己的名字。
  ✎ He <u>inscribed</u> his name <u>in</u> the book. 他在书上题写了自己的名字。
  + 同根词：
    ◇ 前缀**in-** = in 在里边
    ◇ 词根**scribe** = to write 写
    **describe** v. 描写（de- = down）
    **prescribe** 开药方（pre- (时间上)提前）
    **proscribe** 禁止（pro- (位置上)靠前）
    **subscribe** 订阅，认捐，赞同（sub- 在下面）
    **transcribe** 抄写（tran(s)- 穿过）
+ **outrageous** a. 出人意料的，过分的（常指价格）
  ✎ The price is <u>outrageous</u>. 这个价格太过分了。
  ✎ The price is **preposterous**. 这个价格太荒唐/可笑了。
  ✎ The man acted as if he found my offer <u>preposterous</u>……（课后题-11）
  ✎ The price is **absurd**. 这个价格太荒唐/荒谬了。
  ✎ That’s **highway robbery/ daylight robbery**.（习语）（L19笔记）
  ✎ The car **costs a fortune**. 这辆车很贵。
  ✎ The car **costs me an arm and a leg**. 这辆车花了我一大笔钱。（习语）（L19笔记）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ Five pounds (was) too dear（Five pounds作单独的整体看待，故谓语用单数。在标题中，be动词往往会省略）
  ✎ Italian ex-mayor (was) murdered 意大利的前市长遭谋杀
+ **dear**: expensive; costly; pricey; steep（L9）
+ ┏ Small boats loaded with wares……（原文-后置定语）
  ┗ Small boats (which were) loaded with wares……（定语从句，啰嗦）
  **be loaded with……** 满载着……（L12）
  ✎ They quickly <u>loaded</u> a small rubber dinghy <u>with</u> food, matches, and cans of beer and rowed for a few miles across the Caribbean until they arrived at a tiny coral island.（L12）
  + **……满**
    **be covered with……** 覆盖满……
    ✎ …… the decks were soon <u>covered with</u> colourful rugs……（本文）
    **be filled with……** 盛满/装满……；（某人）充满某种情绪
    ✎ …… it <u>is filled with</u> what looks like a thick, greyish substance.（L52）
    ✎ All at once, I noticed that my wife seemed to <u>be filled with</u> alarm.（L48）
    **be <u>packed/ crammed</u> with** 挤满了……（L17）
    ✎ It has been estimated that if the bridge <u>were packed with</u> cars, it would still only be carrying a third of its total capacity.（L17）
    ✎ The streets <u>were packed/ crammed with</u> Christmas shoppers. 街上挤满了圣诞购物者。
    **be stuffed with……** （内部/中间）填满了……
    ✎ a pillow <u>stuffed with</u> feathers 一个羽毛枕头
    ✎ duck <u>stuffed with</u> ‘eight treasures’ 八宝鸭
    ✎ <u>stuffed</u> birds 鸟标本（L59）
    ✎ I’m <u>stuffed</u>. = I’m full. 我吃饱了。
+ **speed** n. 速度；v1. 超速；v2. 快速移动，快速前进（本文）
  ✎ He was fined for <u>speeding</u>. 他因超速而被罚款。
  ✎ We <u>sped</u> down the ski slopes. 我们沿着滑雪坡疾驰而下。
+ **liner** 远洋客轮/班轮
  ✎ The tragic sinking of this <u>great liner</u> will always be remembered, for she went down on her first voyage with heavy loss of life.（L10）
+ ┏ **enter** the harbour 入港
  ┗ **depart from** the harbour 离港（**leave** the harbour 较通俗）
  ┏ **<u>pull/ draw</u> in** the station 进站
  ┗ **<u>pull/ draw</u> out of** the station 出站
  ┏ **take off** 起飞（L20）
  ┗ **land** 着陆
+ ┏ Before she had <u>anchored</u>,……
  ┗ Before she had <u>dropped/ cast anchor</u>,……
+ **on board = aboard** ad. & prep.（on board 较正式）
+ **colourful rugs** （指物）五颜六色的，鲜艳的；（指人）引人注目的，多姿多彩的
  + colourful
    ✎ one of the most <u>colourful</u> figures（L21）
  + rug 小块地毯（多装饰用）
    carpet 满铺地毯
    mat 垫子；地垫
    doormat 门前脚垫；bathmat 浴室垫子；blanket 毯子（床上用）
+ **copper** coffee **pots**
  + copper 泛指任何铜（[U]表示铜金属材料，[C]表示铜币）
    bronze 青铜（落后） ✎ the Bronze Age 青铜器时代
    brass 黄铜（先进） ✎ a brass band 铜管乐队
  + pot
    potbelly 大肚子，啤酒肚
    coffee pot 咖啡壶；teapot 茶壶
    flowerpot 花盆
    kettle 烧水壶
    **the pot calling the kettle black** 五十步笑百步（直译：锅说壶是黑的）（习语）
    pan 平底锅；frying pan 煎锅
    **out of the frying pan into the fire**  才出龙潭又入虎穴（习语）
+ ┏ It was difficult <u>not to be tempted</u>.（原文）
  ┗ It was difficult <u>to avoid being tempted</u>.（换用avoid，借鉴L26）
  No one can <u>avoid being influenced</u> by advertisements.（L26）
  ┗ It was difficult <u>to resist temptation</u>.（换用temptation，借鉴L9）
+ ┏ …… but I decided not to buy anything <u>until</u> I had disembarked.（原文：用until表达“然后”）
  ┗ ……but I decided to disembark <u>before</u> I bought anything.（用before表达“然后”，作连词，接时间状语从句）
  （时间状语从句常用一般时代替将来时，类似于条件状语从句。 ✎ 如果明天下雨 【✔】If it rains. 【✘】If it will rain.✎ 课后题-4-a：before I would buy）
  ┗ ……but I decided to disembark <u>before</u> buying anything.（用before表达“然后”，作介词，接动名词）（课后题-4）
  参考：I shaved <u>before</u> I went to the party. 我刮了胡子然后去参加了聚会。
+ **no sooner…… than……** 刚一……马上就……（no sooner 副词短语；than 连词）
  **= <u>hardly/ barely/ scarcely</u>…… <u>when/ before</u>……**
  前句时态通常是**过去完成时**，后句通常是**一般过去时**。
  ┏ I had <u>no sooner</u> got off the ship <u>than</u> I was assailed……（原文）
  ┗ <u>No sooner</u> <u>had</u> I got off the ship <u>than</u> I was assailed……（强调否定词no sooner，提前到句首形成部分倒装）
  ┗ I <u>had</u> <u>hardly</u> got off the ship <u>when</u> I was assailed……（句中）
  ┗ <u>Hardly</u> <u>had</u> I got off the ship <u>when</u> I was assailed……（句首）
+ **get off**（通常指容纳多人、比较大的交通工具）
  **get off** the bus/ ship/ plane 下车/船/飞机
  ┏ I had no sooner <u>got off</u> the ship than……（原文）
  ┗ I had no sooner <u>disembarked from</u> the ship than……（原文换用）
  + 反义词：
    **get on** the bus/ ship/ plane
  + 小型交通工具：
    ┏ **get into** the car/ taxi
    ┗ **get out of** the car/ taxi
+ ┏ **have no intention of doing sth.** 无意做某事
  ┗ **not intend to do sth.**
  ✎ She <u>intended to</u> dress up as a ghost and as she had made her costume the night before, she was impatient to try it on.（L13）
  ✎ I did<u>n’t intend to</u> buy one, ……（原文换用）
+ ┏ ……, but I could not conceal the fact that I was……（原文）
  ┗ ……, but the man <u>must have noticed</u> that I was……（同课后题-6）
  ┗ ……, but I <u>could not deny</u> that I was……
  ┗ ……, but I <u>had to admit/ acknowledge</u> that I was……
> 仿写第2段第2句
  我当时并没有打算在这家公司工作，但我不能掩饰这样一个事实：他们提供的丰厚的薪水(handsome salary)给我留下了深刻的印象。
  I had no intention of working for the company, but I could not conceal the fact that I was impressed by the handsome salary they offered.
+ **go to great lengths to do** 竭尽全力/不遗余力做某事
  ✎ They have <u>gone to great lengths to</u> make us feel welcome. 他们竭尽全力让我们感到受欢迎。
  + 同义搭配：
    **<u>do/ try</u> one’s best to do**
    ✎ Though the doctor <u>did his best</u>, the patient’s recovery was slow.（L29）
    **<u>do/ try</u> one’s utmost to do**
    ✎ You play to win, and the game has little meaning unless you <u>do your utmost to</u> win.（B4L6）
    **do <u>everything/ all</u> one can to do**
    ✎ Though the doctor <u>did all he could</u>……（L29课后题-9）
    **give one’s all to do**（较通俗）
    **spare no effort to do** 不遗余力去做某事
    ✎ China will <u>spare no effort to</u> realize peaceful reunification. 中国将不遗余力地实现和平统一。
    **go all out to do**（较通俗）
    ✎ W: Look at the delicious sandwiches. John’s really <u>gone all out</u> this time.
    M: Just wait until you see the dessert.
    Q: What does the man imply?
    Answer: The dessert also looks impressive.（听力真题）
+ real 🗘 genuine（本文同义替换）
+ impression 可表示物理上的印记，也可表示心理上的印象
  …… made a deep impression in the glass.（本文）
  …… and it <u>gave me the impression that</u> it was about to leap out at me.（L24）
  **<u>have/ get</u> the impression that……** 某人觉得……（感觉未必是错的）（参见L24、25）
  **be under the impression that……** 误以为……（习语）（强调感觉是错的）
+ made a deep impression **in** the glass 玻璃上（注意介词的使用）
  ✎ He hit me **on** the nose. 鼻子上
  ✎ He hit me **in** the face. 脸上
  ✎ If you are lucky enough to get a sleeper, you spend half the night staring at the small blue light **in** the ceiling, …… 天花板上（L44）
+ **take**（参见L5）
  ┏ It <u>took</u> me over half an hour <u>to</u> get rid of him.（原文，事作主语）
  ┗ I <u>took</u> over half an hour <u>to</u> get rid of him.（原文改，人作主语）
  ✎ The journalist immediately set out to obtain these important facts, but <u>he took a long time to send them</u>.（L5）
  ✎ I <u>spent</u> over half an hour <u>(in) getting</u> rid of him.（原文换用spend，只能人作主语）
+ **get rid of sb.** 打发走某人；干掉某人(派生)
  **= dispose of sb.**
  ✎ There is no quicker method of <u>disposing of</u> patients than by giving them what they are asking for, ……（B4L28）
  + 近义词：
    **expel** 开除
    ✎ He <u>was expelled from</u> school for bad behavior. 他因品行不端被学校开除了。
+ **the first, the second, the next, the last, the best, the only……后常跟不定式作定语**（L25）
  ✎ <u>The next</u> man <u>to approach me</u> was selling expensive pens and watches.（本文）
  ✎ When he landed near Dover, <u>the first</u> person <u>to greet him</u> was a local policeman.（L20）
  ✎ <u>The only</u> other ship <u>to match her</u> was the *Thermopylae*.（L25）
  ✎ <u>The first</u> of the two ships <u>to reach Java</u> after the race had begun was the *Thermopylae*, but on the Indian Ocean, the *Cutty Sark* took the lead.（L25）
  ✎ <u>The last</u> creature <u>to compete with man</u> was the mosquito.（B4L45）
+ **approach** 即可指空间，也可指时间
  ✎ My birthday <u>is fast approaching</u>. 我的生日快到了。
  ✎ My birthday <u>is coming soon</u>.
  ✎ My birthday <u>is near at hand</u>.
  ✎ My birthday <u>is just around the corner</u>.（L1）
+ **closely = carefully**
  ✎ …… advertisers have made a <u>close</u> study of human nature……（L26）
+ **at the base of……** 在……的底部
  **on the basis of……** 在……的基础上
  ✎ Decisions were often made <u>on the basis of</u> false information. 决策往往基于错误信息做出。
+ ┏ **gold** 金的 ✎ gold ring/ medal 金戒指/金牌
  ┗ **golden** 像金子的；金色的 ✎ golden sunshine/ hair 金色的阳光/头发
  ✎ Speech is silver, but silence is <u>golden</u>. 雄辩是银，沉默是金。
+ **neat** a. 工整的
  ┏ His handwriting is <u>neat</u>. 他的笔迹很工整。（handwriting 字迹，笔迹）
  ┗ He has a teacher’s handwriting.
  ┏ His handwriting is <u>illegible</u>. 他的笔记很潦草。
  ┗ He has a doctor’s handwriting.
+ **inscribe** 刻字
  **engrave** 雕刻（不一定是刻字）
  ✎ Historians have long been puzzled by dots,lines and symbols which have been <u>engraved</u> on walls, bones, and the ivory tusks of mammoths.（L38）
+ **shake one’s head** 摇头，不同意
  ┏ I <u>shook my head</u>……
  ┗ I <u>disagreed</u>……
  ┗ I <u>said no to him</u>……
+ **hold up = extend** 伸出
+ **indicate = signify** （间接地）表示
  ✎ Her tone <u>indicated</u> that she didn’t believe a word of my explanation. 她的语气表明她对我的解释一个字都不相信。
  ✎ She <u>signified</u> her agreement by nodding her head. 她点头表示同意。
  ✎ …… held up five fingers <u>signifying</u> that I was……（原文换用）
+ **eventually = at last = finally ≈ in the end** 最终，最后
  in the end只能放在句首或句末，不能放在句中，故本文无法换用。
+ **shrug one’s shoulders** 耸了耸肩膀（肢体语言含义：①不感兴趣；②不知道；③怀疑，不相信）
  **= with a shrug**
+ **when** 然后
  ✎ I will be on vacation till the end of the month <u>when</u> I return to shanghai. 我将度假到月底，然后回到上海。
+ **run after = chase** 追（L6）
  ✎ Just as it was leaving, Mr. Taylor rushed out and <u>ran after</u> it throwing ashtrays and vases,……（L6）
+ **readily = willingly** 乐意地，愿意地（L4）
  ✎ There are times when we would <u>willingly</u> give everything we possess to save our lives,……（L27）
+ **be pleased with** 对……既开心又满意（L23）
+ ┏ <u>No matter how</u> hard I tried,……（原文）
  ┗ <u>However</u> hard I tried,……
  ✎ Judges, <u>however</u> wise or eminent, are human and can make mistakes.（L35）
+ <u>beautiful</u> pen 此处是反语，表示中看不中用
  ✎ Imagine their dismay when they found a <u>beautifully-cooked</u> wallet and notes turned to ash.（L7）
+ **to this day = so far** 迄今为止（一般用在现在完成时）
+ **a single** word 加强语气
  ✎ I spent the whole day in my room, but I did not write <u>a single</u> card!（B2L3）
  ✎ He earned enormous sums of money and was paid as much as £100 for <u>a single appearance</u>.（L21）
  ✎ They had <u>a single</u> aim, <u>**a solitary**</u> goal —— the top! 同义词连用，加强语气（B4L3）
> 仿写最后1句
  无论我多么好地喂养(feed)这只鸡，它就是不肯产卵(breed)，直到今天它连一个蛋也没下过。
  No matter how well I fed her, it was impossible to persuade the beautiful hen to breed and to this day she has never laid a single egg!

---

## **Lesson 29 - Funny or not?**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>Whether we find a joke funny or not largely depends on where we have been brought up. The sense of humour is mysteriously bound up with national characteristics. A Frenchman, for instance, might find it hard to laugh at a Russian joke. In the same way, a Russian might fail to see anything amusing in a joke which would make an Englishman laugh to tears.

Most funny stories are based on comic situations. In spite of national differences, certain funny situations have a universal appeal. No matter where you live, you would find it difficult not to laugh at, say, Charlie Chaplin’s early films. However, a new type of humour, which stems largely from the U.S., has recently come into fashion. It is called ‘sick humour’. Comedians base their jokes on tragic situations like violent death or serious accidents. Many people find this sort of joke distasteful. The following example of ‘sick humour’ will enable you to judge for yourself.

A man who had broken his right leg was taken to hospital a few weeks before Christmas. From the moment he arrived there, he kept on pestering his doctor to tell him when he would be able to go home. He dreaded having to spend Christmas in hospital. Though the doctor did his best, the patient’s recovery was slow. On Christmas Day, the man still had his right leg in plaster. He spent a miserable day in bed thinking of all the fun he was missing. The following day, however, the doctor consoled him by telling him that his chances of being able to leave hospital in time for New Year celebrations were good. The man took heart and, sure enough, on New Year’s Eve he was able to hobble along to a party. To compensate for his unpleasant experiences in hospital, the man drank a little more than was good for him. In the process, he enjoyed himself thoroughly and kept telling everybody how much he hated hospitals. He was still mumbling something about hospitals at the end of the party when he slipped on a piece of ice and broke his left leg.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **largely** ad. 在很大程度上，主要地；广泛地，大量地
  英文释义：to a great extent; chiefly
  ✎ His success was <u>largely</u> due to his hard work. 他的成功在很大程度上归功于他的努力。
  ✎ The theory was <u>largely</u> adopted. 该理论得到了广泛地应用。
  + 易混词：
    **mostly**: in most cases 大多数情况下（表示时间的拼读）
    ✎ We’re <u>mostly</u> out on weekends. 在周末，我们大多数情况下都不在家。
+ ┏ **comic** a. 喜剧的；可笑的；滑稽的
  ┗ **comedy** n. 喜剧
  + 同义词：
    **funny, amusing, diverting**
  + 相关词：
    ┏ **tragic** 悲剧的；悲惨的
    ┗ **tragedy** 悲剧
    ┏ **farcical** 闹剧的；荒诞的，离奇的
    ┗ **farce** 闹剧，荒诞剧
    ┏ **dramatic** 戏剧的；戏剧性的
    ┗ **drama** 戏剧
+ **universal** a. 普遍的；世界性的，~~宇宙的~~
  + 易混词：
    **cosmic** 宇宙的；**cosmos** 宇宙
    + 形近词：
      **comic** 喜剧的；可笑的；滑稽的
      **comet** 彗星
      **cosmetics** 化妆品（侧重瓶瓶罐罐的化妆品）辨：**makeup** 化妆品（擦到脸上的化妆品）✎ The girl doesn’t wear makeup. 这个女孩素面朝天。
  + 同义替换：
    **global, international, world-wide**
    ✎ English has now become an <u>international</u> language. Therefore, if you have a good command of this language, you hold the key to success. 英语现在已经成为一种世界性的语言。因此，如果你精通这门语言，你就抓住了通向成功的钥匙。
  + **universally** ad. 普遍地；世界性地
    ✎ It is <u>universally</u> known that…… 大家普遍都知道……；众所周知……（习语）
+ **comedian** n. 喜剧演员，丑角；**comedienne** 喜剧女演员；**comedy** 喜剧
  相关词：
  **tragedian** 悲剧演员；**tragedienne** 悲剧女演员；**tragedy** 悲剧
  **leading <u>role/ part</u>** 主角，主人公；**protagonist** 主角
  **leading man, hero** 男主
  **leading lady, heroine** 女主
  **supporting role** 配角；**extra** 群演
+ **distasteful** a. 讨厌的，令人不愉快的
  **be distasteful to sb.** 对某人来说是讨厌的
  ┏ It <u>is distasteful to</u> me to say this, but…… 我不愿这么说，但是……
  ┗ I hate to say this, but……
  + 近义词（L23）：
    v. | a. 
    ---- | ---- 
    repel | repellent 
    repulse | repulsive 
    revolt | revolting 
    disgust | disgusting 
+ **pester** v. 纠缠，一再要求
  **pester sb. for sth.** 为了某事纠缠某人
  **pester sb. with sth.** 用某事来纠缠某人
  ✎ He <u>pestered</u> me <u>for</u> money. 他缠着我要钱。
  ✎ He <u>pestered</u> me <u>with</u> complaints. 他不断地向我抱怨。
  + 同义词（L28）：
    **harry, harass, assail**
+ **recovery** v. 康复；恢复原状
  **recovery from……** 从……状态中恢复到正常状态
  ✎ <u>recovery from</u> illness 从病中康复
  ✎ <u>recovery from</u> defeat 从失败中振作
  + **recover, restore, regain** v. 恢复了……
    ✎ <u>recover/ restore/ regain</u> one’s health 恢复健康
    ✎ <u>recover/ restore/ regain</u> one’s sight 恢复视力
    ✎ <u>recover/ restore/ regain</u> one’s consciousness 恢复意识
    ✎ <u>recover/ restore/ regain</u> one’s balance 恢复平衡
    ✎ <u>recover/ restore/ regain</u> one’s composure 恢复镇静
+ **console** v. 安慰，慰问
  **console sb. for sth.** 因为某事而安慰某人
  **console sb. with sth.** 用某物来安慰某人
  ✎ I <u>consoled</u> him <u>for</u> the loss of money. 我因为他金钱的损失而安慰他。
  ✎ I <u>consoled</u> him <u>with</u> money. 我用钱来慰问他。
  + 近义词：
    **comfort** 安慰
    ✎ <u>comfort</u> a dying man 抚慰一个垂死的人
    **soothe** 安慰
    **= calm sb. down = calm down sb.** 使某人平静下来
    ✎ <u>soothe</u> a crying baby 安抚哭闹的婴儿
  + 易混词：
    **condole with sb.** 吊慰某人
    ✎ The widow’s friends <u>condoled with</u> her at the funeral. 寡妇的朋友们在葬礼上吊慰她。
+ **compensate** v. 弥补，补偿
  **compensate (sb.) for sth.** 弥补（某人的）某事
  ✎ Nothing can <u>compensate (him) for</u> his loss. 没有任何东西能够弥补（他）他的损失。
  **more than compensate for……** 足以弥补……（固定习语）
  ✎ His rise in status <u>more than compensates for</u> the loss of money.（L4课后题-11）
  + 同义替换：
    **make up for……** 弥补……
    **redeem**
    **offset……**


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
#### 👾 表示“是否”时不能用 if 的几种情况
whether表示“是否”时是万用的，但if有以下几种限制：
1. **主语从句位于句首时**
  【✘】**If** she likes the present is not clear to me.
  【✔】It is not clear to me **if/ whether** she likes the present.
  【✔】**Whether** she likes the present is not clear to me.
1. **引导表语从句时**
  【✘】The question is **if** we have enough money.
  【✔】The question is **whether** we have enough money.
  问题在于我们是否有足够的钱。
1. **引导同位语从句时**
  【✘】You have yet to answer my question **if** I can count on your help.
  【✔】You have yet to answer my question **whether** I can count on your help.
  是否我能指望你的帮助，你还没有回答我这个问题。
  （have yet to do sth. 还没有做某事(应做未做)(固定搭配，偏文言)）
1. **作介词宾语时**
  【✘】He was worrying <u>about</u> **if** he had hurt her feelings.
  【✔】He was worrying <u>about</u> **whether** he had hurt her feelings.
  他担心他是否伤害了她的感情。
1. **引导动词不定式时**
  【✘】I don’t know **if** <u>to</u> see my doctor today.
  【✔】I don’t know **whether** <u>to</u> see my doctor today.
  我不知道是否今天应该去看医生。
1. **直接跟or not时**
  【✘】Please tell me **if** <u>or not</u> you agree.
  【✔】Please tell me **whether** <u>or not</u> you agree.
  【✔】Please tell me **if/ whether** you agree <u>or not</u>.
  请告诉我你是否同意。
+ **依赖，依靠，取决于** 总结
  + 主动（on都可以换成upon，以更显正式）
    **depend on……**
    **rest on……**
    **rely on/ upon……**
    **ride on……**
    **hinge on……**（hinge 铰链，合叶）
    **lean on……**（lean 倾斜，倚靠）
  + 加be动词的（要么是系表，要么是被动）
    **be dependent on……**（系表）
    **be based on……**（被动）
    **be built on……**（被动）
    **be founded on……**（被动）
  + 被动 + by
    **be decided by……**
    **be dictated by……**
    **be determined by……**
  ┏ Whether we find a joke funny or not largely <u>depends on</u> where we have been brought up.（原文）
  ┗ Whether you find a joke funny or not largely <u>rests/ relies/ rides/ hinges/ leans on</u> where we have been brought up.（原文替换①）
  ┗ Whether you find a joke funny or not <u>is</u> largely <u>dependent/ based/ built/ founded on</u> where we have been brought up.（原文替换②）
  ┗ Whether you find a joke funny or not <u>is</u> largely <u>decided/ dictated/ determined by</u> where we have been brought up.（原文替换③）
+ **bring up**
  + **养育**
    **bring up sb.** 把某人拉扯大（L23）
    ✎ He <u>was brought up</u> by his step-mother.
    **raise sb.** 抚养，养育（L2）
    **<u>foster/ adopt</u> sb.** 领养
    ✎ <u>adopted</u> son 养子
    ✎ <u>adoptive</u> parents = <u>foster</u>-parents 养父母
  + **be brought up to do** 从小就……（固定搭配，一般用于现在完成时）
    ✎ The sad truth is that most of us have <u>been brought up to</u> eat certain foods and we stick to them all our lives.（L23）
    ✎ We have <u>been brought up to</u> fear insects.（L54）
+ **the sense**
  ✎ the sense of pride 自豪感
  ✎ the sense of honor 荣誉感
  ✎ the sense of accomplishment 成就感
  ✎ the sense of responsibility 责任感
  ┏ the sense of superiority 优越感（superior 优越的；更高级的）
  ┗ the sense of inferiority 自卑感（inferior 较差的；更低级的）
+ **be bound up with……** 与……紧密相连（**bind** v. 绑）
  英文释义：**be closely connected with……**
  ✎ Everyone’s future <u>is bound up with</u> the destiny of the Chinese nation. 每个人的未来都与中华民族的命运紧密相连。
  + 相关搭配：
    **be bound to do……** 必然会……；肯定会……
    ✎ On our road ahead, we <u>are bound to</u> meet with difficulties. 在前进的道路上，我们必然会遇到困难。
    **<u>be/ feel</u> bound to do……** 觉得必须做某事
    ✎ I <u>felt bound to</u> tell him the truth. 我觉得必须把真相告诉他。
    **≈ <u>be/ feel</u> obliged to do……**（L1）
    ✎ However, as the evidence began to accumulate, experts from the Zoo <u>felt obliged to</u> investigate, for the descriptions given by people who claimed to have seen the puma were extraordinarily similar.（L1）
    **bind sb. to do** 约束某人必须做某事
    ✎ The Kyoto Protocol <u>binds</u> each country <u>to</u> reduce the emission of greenhouse gases. 《京都议定书》约束每个国家减少温室气体排放。
+ **泛指某国人** 的2种表达
  ┏ a Frenchman（+ 单数谓语）
  ┗ the French（+ 复数谓语）
  ┏ an Englishman（+ 单数谓语）
  ┗ the <u>English/ British</u>（+ 复数谓语）
  ✎ <u>The French</u>, for instance, might find it hard to……（课后题-4）
+ **in the same way** 同样地（辨：**in the same way that……** 像……一样）
  **= likewise, similarly, by the same token**（都一般在句首，加逗号）
+ **laugh to tears** 笑出眼泪来（固定搭配）
  类似搭配：
  **be bored to <u>tears/ death</u>** 无聊得要哭/死
  **laugh one’s head off** 笑得头都要掉了
  ✎ …… which would make an Englishman <u>laugh his head off</u>.（原文替换）
  **clap one’s hands off** 鼓掌鼓得手都要掉了
  **cry one’s eyes out** 哭得眼珠都要出来了

#### 👾 对比(修辞) contrast
✎ A mother takes twenty years to make a man of her boy, and another woman makes a fool of him in twenty minutes. 一个母亲花了二十年的时间才能把她的儿子变成一个男人，而另一个女人花了二十分钟就把他变成了一个傻瓜。
✎ Men always want to be a woman’s first love; women have a more subtle instinct: what they like is to be a man’s last romance. 男人总是希望成为女人的初恋；女人有一种更微妙的本能：她们希望成为的是男人的最后一段恋情。

+ funny 🗘 comic 🗘 amusing（原文同义替换）
  base on 🗘 depend on（原文同义替换）
+ **universal**: international, global, world-wide（同义替换）
  **appeal**: attraction, charm, fascination（L9）（同义替换）
  ┏ a universal appeal（原文）
  ┗ an international attraction（原文同义替换）
  ┗ a global charm（~）
  ┗ a world-wide fascination（~）
  + 搭配
    **appeal to sb.** 吸引某人，引起某人的兴趣（不及物）
    ✎ The idea never <u>appealed to</u> me very much,……（L23）
    **<u>attract/ charm/ fascinate</u> sb.** 吸引某人（及物）
    ✎ Cats never fail to <u>fascinate</u> human beings.（L9）
  + a.
    **appealing, attractive, charming, fascinating**
+ **No matter where**（L1，L2，L8）
  引导让步状语从句时，相当于**Wherever**
  No matter where you live,……（原文）
  = Wherever you live,……
  ┏ **“疑问词 + ever” 可以引导名词性从句**（详见L8）
  ┗ **“No matter + 疑问词” 只能引导让步状语从句**
+ **(let’s) say** 比如说，比方说（一般作插入语）
  ✎ …… , say,……（原文）
  ✎ Why don’t we have a break until, <u>(let’s) say</u>, 10:45?（作插入语）
  ✎ <u>Say/ Let’s say (that)</u> the journey takes three hours, you’ll arrive at 2 o’clock. 假设旅程需要三个小时，你将在两点钟到达。（作连词，引导条件状语从句）
+ **stem from……** 起源于……（stem 茎）（L15）
  **= originate in……**（origin n. 起源）
  **= have its roots in……**
  ┏ Printing <u>originates in</u> China.
  ┏ Printing <u>stems from</u> China.
  ┏ Printing  <u>has its roots in</u> China.
  ┗ 印刷术起源于中国。
  + 相近词：
    **arise from……** 源自于……（表示问题、困难、摩擦、纠纷、冲突等倒霉的事源自于）
    ✎ The argument <u>arose from</u> misunderstanding. 这次争执源于误会。
    **<u>come/ hail</u> from……** 某人来自于……
    ✎ I <u>come/ hail</u> from China.
+ **come into fashion** 开始流行（固定搭配）
  ✎ Miniskirts have <u>come into fashion</u>. 迷你裙现在开始流行起来了。
  ┏ **be in fashion** 正在流行
  ┗ **be out of fashion** 过时
  **fashionable** a. 流行的，时髦的
  ✎ <u>fashionable</u> clothes/ ideas/ hairstyles 流行的服装/观念/发型
  + come into
    **come into use** 开始得到使用
    ✎ Computers first <u>came into use</u> in the early 1950s. 计算机于1950年代早期开始得到使用。
    **come into effect** 开始生效
    ✎ The new seat-belt regulations <u>came into effect</u> last week. 新的安全带规章制度于上周生效。
    **come into blossom** 开花
    ✎ The trees are late <u>coming into blossom</u> this year. 这些树今年开花晚了。
    **come into being** 开始存在，开始出现，开始产生
    ✎ Up to now, historians have assumed that calendars <u>came into being</u> with the advent of agriculture,……（L38）
+ ┏ Comedians <u>base</u> their jokes <u>on</u> tragic situations……（原文）
  ┗ Comedians <u>build</u> their jokes <u>on</u> tragic situations……（原文同义替换）
  ┗ Comedians <u>found</u> their jokes <u>on</u> tragic situations……（原文同义替换）
+ ┏ **like** 较口语
  ┗ **such as** 较书面
+ ┏ Many people find this sort of joke <u>distasteful</u>.（distasteful 令人讨厌的，令人不愉快的）（原文）
  ┗ Many people find this sort of joke <u>unpleasant/ disgusting/ repellent/ revolting/ repulsive</u>.（原文同义替换）
  ┗ Many people <u>dislike/ hate/ despise/ abhor/ detest/ loathe/ abominate</u> this sort of joke.（动词同义表达）
  ┗ This sort of joke <u>repels/ revolts/ repulses/ disgusts/ sickens</u> many people.（玩笑作主语，同义表达）
+ **“举例”** 的表达
  ┏ the **following** example 下面这个例子
  ┗ the **ensuing** example
  ┗ the **under-mentioned** example
  ┗ the example **below**
  ┏ the **previous** example 上面这个例子
  ┗ the **preceding** example
  ┗ the **above-mentioned** example
  ┗ the example **above**
+ **enable sb. to do** 使某人能够……（L26）
  ✎ They devise hundreds of competitions which will <u>enable</u> us <u>to</u> win huge sums of money.（L26）
  + 同义替换：
    **<u>allow/ permit</u> sb. to do** 人做主语：某人允许某人做某事；物作主语：使能够
    **make it possible for sb. to do** 使能够
    ✎ Radio and television have <u>made it possible for</u> advertisers <u>to</u> capture the attention of millions of people in this way.（L26）
    ┏ …… will <u>enable</u> you <u>to</u> judge for yourself.（原文）
    ┗ …… will <u>allow/ permit</u> you <u>to</u> judge for yourself.
    ┗ …… will <u>make it possible for</u> you <u>to</u> judge for yourself.
+ **do sth for oneself** 亲自做某事，~~为自己做事~~（习语）
  ✎ So great is our passion for doing things <u>for ourselves</u>, that we are becoming increasingly less dependent on specialized labour.（L46）
+ ┏ A man who had broken his right leg……（原文）
  ┗ A man <u>whose right leg had been broken</u>……
+ take sb. to hospital 把某人送到医院（强调看病时，hospital前不能加冠词）
  = send sb. to hospital
  + **强调功能时，场所前不能加冠词**
    ✎ go to hospital 去医院（看病）；go to the hospital 去医院（目的未知）
    ✎ go to bed 去睡觉；go to the bed 去床那里
  + 医院相关
    **be in hospital = be hospitalized** 住院
    **leave hospital** 出院
    the outpatient department (OPD) 门诊部
    the inpatient department (IPD) 住院部
    casualty [英] / emergency room (ER) [美] 急诊室
+ From the moment he arrived there,……（原文）
  原文的省略：
  From the moment <u>when</u> he arrived there,……
  From the moment <u>at which</u> he arrived there,……
  From the moment <u>that</u> he arrived there,……
  From the moment <u>/</u> he arrived there,……
+ **自从**：
  **①from**（无时态限制，多接一般时，尤其一般过去时）；
  **②since**（通常接完成时）
  ┏ <u>From</u> the moment he arrived there, he kept on pestering……（原文）
  ┗ <u>Since</u> the moment he arrived there, he <u>had</u> kept on pestering……（换用since）
+ **keep (on) doing** 老是做某事（L2）
  ✎ Why do you <u>keep (on)</u> making the same mistakes? 你为什么总是犯相同的错误呢？
  ✎ How can I explain if you <u>keep (on)</u> interrupting me? 如果你一直打断我，那我该怎么解释？
  ✎ In the process, he enjoyed himself thoroughly and <u>kept telling</u> everybody how much he hated hospitals.（去掉on的例子）（本文）
+ **dread <u>sth./ doing sth.</u>** 害怕某事物/某事发生（L11）
  ✎ She dreads getting old. 她害怕变老。
  **dread to do** 一做某事就害怕
  ✎ I dread to think what will happen if I fail. 我一想到如果我失败了会发生什么，我就觉得害怕。
  【✘】She dreads to get old.
+ **<u>do/ try</u> one’s best to do** 竭尽全力（L28）
  **= <u>do/ try</u> one’s utmost to do**
  **= do <u>everything/ all</u> one can to do**
  ✎ Though the doctor <u>did all he could</u>……（L29课后题-9）
  **= give one’s all to do**
  **= spare no effort to do**
  **= go all out to do**
  **= go to great lengths to do**
  ✎ The man <u>went to great lengths to</u> prove that the diamonds were real.（L28）
+ ┏ **on** Christmas Day **在**圣诞节**这天**
  ┗ **on** Easter Day 在复活节这天
  ┏ **at** Christmas **在**圣诞节假期**期间**
  ┗ **at** Easter 在复活节假期期间
  ✎ The only regular visitors to the monastery in winter are parties of skiers who go there <u>at</u> Christmas and Easter.（L8）
+ ┏ …… the man still had his right leg in plaster.（原文）
  ┗ …… the man’s right leg was still in plaster.（通俗表达）
+ ┏ **one’s chances of doing…… are <u>good/ high</u>.** 某人做某事的可能性很大（用of引出同位语）
  ┏ **the chances that…… are <u>good/ high</u>.** （同位语从句）
  ┗ **one’s chances of doing…… are <u>small/ slight/ remote</u>.** 某人做某事的可能性很小（~）
  ┗ **the chances that…… are <u>small/ slight/ remote</u>.** （~）
  ✎ The following day, however, the doctor consoled him by telling him that <u>his chances of</u> being able to leave hospital in time for New Year celebrations <u>were good</u>.（本文）
  ✎ As she is not rich, <u>the chances that</u> she will ever be able to afford such purchases <u>are remote</u>; but she is never sufficiently strong-minded to be able to stop the practice.（L59）
  ┏ 他赢得这次比赛的可能性很小。
  ┗ <u>His chances of</u> winning the game <u>are remote</u>.
  ┗ <u>The chances that</u> he will win the game <u>are remote</u>.
+ celebrations 复数表示庆典、庆祝活动
+ ┏ **take heart = be encouraged** 受到鼓舞（习语）
  ┗ **lose heart** 灰心丧气
  **lose one’s heart to……** 爱上某人
+ **sure enough** 正如预料到的那样；果然、果不其然
  **= as expected**
+ **Eve** 表示重要日期的前一天/夜（搭配介词on）
+ along 向前，~~沿着~~
+ experiences 表示经验，不可数；表示具体的经历，可数。
+ …… than (what) was good for him.
  **than后面可以跟宾语从句，这个宾语从句的主语往往被省略。相当于than直接加谓语动词。**
  ✎ It seems that man was making a real effort to understand the seasons 20,000 years earlier <u>than has been supposed</u>.（L38）
  ✎ The project requires more labor than <u>has been put in</u> because it is extremely difficult.
  A. has been put in；B. have been put in；C. being put in；D. to be put in
  ✎ We often advise him not to drink more wine <u>than</u> is good for his health.
  A. as；B. than；C. that；D. but
  ✎ The experiment requires more money than <u>has been put in</u>.
  A. have been put in；B. being put in；C. has been put in；D. to be put in
  ✎ The indoor swimming pool seems to be a great deal more luxurious than <u>is necessary</u>.
  A. is necessary；B. being necessary；C. to be necessary；D. it is necessary
+ **enjoy oneself = have a <u>good/ great</u> time**
  ┏ ……, he <u>enjoyed himself</u>……（原文）
  ┗ ……, he <u>had a good/ great time</u>……（原文换用）
+ ┏ …… kept telling everybody <u>how much</u> he hated hospitals.（原文）
  ┗ …… kept telling everybody <u>to what extent</u> he hated hospitals.（原文换用）
  ✎ —— <u>To what extent</u> do you love her? —— I’ll die for her.
+ **mumble** 模糊不清地说（常表示抱怨）
+ **主句 (进行时/be about to do) + when……**（L23）
  “when”应译为 **“这时”** 或 **“突然”**。此句型还有一点特殊：句子重心在从句，而不在主句。
  ✎ He <u>was still mumbling</u> something about hospitals at the end of the party **when** he slipped on a piece of ice and broke his left leg.（本文）
  ✎ The idea never appealed to me very much, but one day, after a heavy shower, I happened <u>to be walking</u> in my garden **when** I noticed a huge number of snails taking a stroll on some of my prize plants.（L23）
  ✎ 更多例句见L23相关笔记
+ **slip** 滑；小失误，小疏忽，小错(派生)
  ✎ slip on a piece of ice 在一块冰上滑倒
  ✎ trip over a stone 被一块石头绊倒
  ✎ a slip of the pen 笔误
  ✎ a slip of the tongue 口误（B2L89）

---

## **Lesson 30 - The death of a ghost**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>For years, villagers believed that Endley Farm was haunted. The farm was owned by two brothers, Joe and Bob Cox. They employed a few farmhands, but no one was willing to work there long. Every time a worker gave up his job, he told the same story. Farm labourers said that they always woke up to find that work had been done overnight. Hay had been cut and cowsheds had been cleaned. A farm worker, who stayed up all night, claimed to have seen a figure cutting corn in the moonlight. In time, it became an accepted fact that the Cox brothers employed a conscientious ghost that did most of their work for them.

No one suspected that there might be someone else on the farm who had never been seen. This was indeed the case. A short time ago, villagers were astonished to learn that the ghost of Endley had died. Everyone went to the funeral, for the ‘ghost’ was none other than Eric Cox, a third brother who was supposed to have died as a young man. After the funeral, Joe and Bob revealed a secret which they had kept for over fifty years.

Eric had been the eldest son of the family, very much older than his two brothers. He had been obliged to join the army during the Second World War. As he hated army life, he decided to desert his regiment. When he learnt that he would be sent abroad, he returned to the farm and his father hid him until the end of the war. Fearing the authorities, Eric remained in hiding after the war as well. His father told everybody that Eric had been killed in action. The only other people who knew the secret were Joe and Bob. They did not even tell their wives. When their father died, they thought it their duty to keep Eric in hiding. All these years, Eric had lived as a recluse. He used to sleep during the day and work at night, quite unaware of the fact that he had become the ghost of Endley. When he died, however, his brothers found it impossible to keep the secret any longer.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ + **labour/ labor** n. [U] 劳动力（泛指）
    skilled/ unskilled <u>labor</u> 熟练工/非熟练工
    child <u>labor</u> 童工
    <u>labor</u> market 劳动力市场
    <u>labor</u> force 劳动力大军/队伍
    <u>labor</u> shortage 劳动力短缺
    <u>labor</u> relations 劳资关系
    【✘】My father is a <u>labor</u>.
    【✔】My father is a <u>laborer</u>.
  + **labourer/ laborer** n. [C] 劳动者，工人（一般表示体力工作者）
    farm <u>laborer</u>
    近义词：
    **hand** 工人（一般表示体力工作者，多作复合名词）
    farm<u>hand</u>
    **worker** 工人（体力脑力都可）
    blue-collar <u>worker</u>
    white-collar <u>worker</u>
+ **overnight**
  ad. 在夜里，在夜间；突然，很快
  a. 夜间的；突然的，很快的
  ✎ You can stay <u>overnight</u> if you want to. 如果你愿意，你可以过夜。
  ✎ an <u>overnight</u> journey 一次夜间旅行
  ✎ He became famous <u>overnight</u>. 他一夜成名了。
  ✎ an <u>overnight</u> success 一次突然的成功
+ **conscientious** a. 认真负责的
  ✎ a <u>conscientious</u> worker/ attitude 一个认真负责的工人/态度（指人指物都可以）
  **conscience** n. 良心
  ✎ have a clear/ guilty <u>conscience</u> 问心无愧/问心有愧
  ✎ A clear <u>conscience</u> is a soft pillow. 白天不做亏心事半夜不怕鬼敲门。（直译：一个干净的良心是一个柔软的枕头）（谚语）
  形近词：
  **conscious** a. 意识到的，知道的，有意识的
  **consciousness** n. 意识
  ✎ enhance people’s <u>consciousness</u> of public morality 提高人民群众的公德意识
+ **suspect** 
  + v. 怀疑（怀疑有还是没有，需要看逻辑）
    ✎ He <u>suspected</u> an ambush. 他怀疑有埋伏。（有）
    ✎ I suspected his honesty. 我怀疑他的诚实。（没有）
    **suspect sb. of (doing) sth.** 怀疑某人做某事
    ✎ I <u>suspected</u> him <u>of</u> lying. 我怀疑他撒谎。
  + n.
    **suspect** n. 嫌疑犯
    **suspicion** n. 怀疑
    **suspicious** a. 怀疑的，不相信的，可疑的
    **be suspicious of** 对……怀疑/不相信
  ✎ I<u>’m suspicious of</u> his motives. 我怀疑他的动机。
+ **recluse** n. 隐士，隐居者
  近义词：
  **hermit** 隐居者
  **anchorite** 隐居者（强调由于宗教原因）
  **loner** 喜欢独处的人；不喜欢与人打交道的人（最常用）
  ✎ She has been a <u>loner</u> all her life. 她终其一生都是个喜欢独处的人。
  ┏ **solitary** a. 喜欢独处的，不愿跟人打交道的；唯一的
  ┗ **sociable** a. 喜欢交际的
  **prefer one’s own company** 愿意独处（习语）
  ✎ We asked him to come and eat with us, but he said he <u>preferred his own company</u>. 我们请他来和我们一起吃饭，但他愿意一个人待着。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **传言** 的表达
  **rumor has it that……**
  **= it’s rumored that……**（**rumour/ rumor** n. 流言蜚语，谣言；v. 传谣言说）
  ✎ <u>Rumor has it that/ It’s rumored that</u> she only married him for his money. 有传言说她只是为了他的钱才嫁给他的。
  **word has it that……**（未必是贬义）
  ✎ <u>Word has it that</u> John is going to keep a dog as a pet. 听说约翰要养狗当宠物。（keep 养活，饲养，~~保持~~）
  **legend has it that……** 据传说……（多表示历史上的传说）（习语）
  ✎ <u>Legend has it that</u> Qu Yuan, a great poet of the Warring States period, threw himself into the Mi Luo River when he heard his homeland had been invaded. 传说战国时期伟大的诗人屈原听说自己的祖国被侵略，便投汨罗江自尽了。
+ **haunt** v. 鬼魂出没于某地；不愉快的情绪总缠着某人，挥之不去
  ┏ A headless man <u>haunts</u> the castle. 一个无头男人经常出没于这座城堡。（主动）
  ┗ The castle <u>is haunted</u>. 这座城堡闹鬼。（被动）
  **be haunted by……** 不愉快的情绪总缠着某人，挥之不去
  ✎ He <u>is haunted by</u> the experience of failure. 失败的经历总是缠着他，挥之不去。
  ✎ I<u>’m haunted by</u> homesickness. 我想家了。/我最近被思乡的情绪所缠绕。
+ ┏ The farm <u>was owned by</u> two brothers,……（原文）
  ┗ The farm <u>was possessed by</u> two brothers,……
  ┗ The farm <u>was in the possession of</u> two brothers,……
  ┗ Two brothers <u>were in possession of</u> the farm,……
  ┗ The farm <u>belonged to</u> two brothers,……
+ **雇佣 & 解雇** 的表达 
  + 雇佣
    **employ sb. = hire sb.**（较常见）
    **engage sb.**（较正式）
    **<u>take on sb. / take sb. on</u>**（较通俗）
    辨：**appoint sb.** 任命某人
    ✎ He has <u>been appointed (as)</u> chief executive officer of the company. 他已被任命为公司的首席执行官。
  + 解雇（L5）
    **fire sb.**（语气不客气）
    **dismiss sb.**（正式，委婉）
    **<u>sack sb./ give sb. the sack</u>**（口语）
    **lay off sb.** 使某人下岗，短期解聘（laid-off workers）
    **suspend sb.** 停职某人（L18）
