    ✎ The two police officers have been <u>suspended</u> until an enquiry is carried out. 这两位警官被停职察看直到我们开始做调查为止。
+ **be <u>willing/ ready/ prepared</u> to do** 乐意去做某事
+ **(for) long** 长时间（一般用于否定句或疑问句）
  ✎ ……, but no one was willing to work there <u>(for) long</u>.（原文）
  ✎ Have you known him <u>(for) long</u>? 你认识他很久了吗？
  ✎ I haven’t known him <u>(for) long</u>. 我并没有认识他很久。
  **(for) a long time**（用于肯定句）
  ✎ I have known him <u>(for) a long time</u>. 我已经认识他很久了。
+ ┏ **every time (when)** 每当
  ┗ **each time (when)**
  先行词是表示时间的名词，那么关系副词when通常可去掉。
  ┏ <u>Every time</u> a worker gave up his job,……（原文）
  ┗ <u>Every time when</u> a worker gave up his job,……
  ┗ <u>Each time when</u> a worker gave up his job,……
  + 同义替换：
    **whenever** 无论何时
    **no matter when**
+ **辞职** 的表达
  **give up one’s job**（通俗）
  **leave one’s job**（通俗）
  **quit one’s job**（通俗）
  **resign**（正式）
  辨：**retire** 退休
+ **story**
  **it’s the same old story** 还是老问题（一般指不好的事）（习语）
  ✎ <u>It’s the same old story</u>: too much work and not enough time. 还是老问题：工作太多，时间不够。 
  **it’s a long story** 说来话长（习语）
  **to <u>cut/ make</u> a long story short** 长话短说（习语）
  **It’s <u>another/ a different</u> story** 这是另一回事
+ **动词不定式一般可充当4种状语：①目的（最常见）；②原因（常见）；③结果（偶见）；④条件（罕见）。**
  **动词不定式作结果状语时（尤其在表示随后发生的动作时）多表示意料之外的不愉快的结果。此时常在动词不定式前加上only以进一步加强意料之外的语气。**
  ✎ He got home <u>to learn that his father was ill</u>. 他回到家，结果却得知父亲病了。
  ✎ Jim turned round <u>to see that Mary was weeping</u>. 吉姆转过身，结果却看见玛丽正在哭泣。
  ✎ He got to the station **only** <u>to be told the train had gone</u>. 他到了车站，结果却被告知火车已经开走了。
+ **<u>stay up/ sit up</u>** 熬夜（L2）
  ✎ He <u>sat up</u> all night, preparing for the exam.
  **burn the midnight oil** 熬夜（习语）
  **a night owl** 夜猫子
  **wait up (for sb.)** 等某人回家而没睡
  ✎ I should go —— Marie will be <u>waiting up</u> for me. 我该走了——玛丽还在等我呢。
  **toss and turn** 辗转反侧，难以入眠
  ✎ Last night I <u>tossed and turned</u> in bed, too exhausted to sleep.
  Answer: I was overtired and couldn’t sleep.（听力真题）
  ┏ **not sleep a wink** 一宿没合眼（动词sleep）
  ┗ **= not get a wink of sleep**（名词sleep）
  ┏ I <u>didn’t sleep a wink</u> last night with all that noise.
  ┗ I <u>didn’t get a wink of sleep</u> last night with all that noise.
  **sleep come in snatches** 忽睡忽醒，睡不安稳
  ✎ uring the day, <u>sleep comes in snatches</u>.（snatch n. 片段的时间）（L44）
  **lull sb. to sleep** 使某人沉沉入睡
  ✎ …… <u>lulls you to sleep</u>.（L44）
  ✎ The dream-like music <u>lulls me to sleep</u>. 这梦幻般的音乐使我沉沉睡去。
+ **claim to have done** 声称曾经做过某事（L1）
  ✎ …… for the descriptions given by people who <u>claimed to have seen</u> the puma were extraordinarily similar.（L1）
  ✎ Fishermen and sailors sometimes <u>claim to have seen</u> monsters in the sea.（B2L82）
  **claim to do** 声称做某事
  ✎ So far, no organization has <u>claimed to be</u> responsible for the accident.
+ ┏ 在月光中：**in the moonlight, by moonlight**
  ┗ 在阳光中：**in the sunlight, in the sunshine, in the sun**
+ **in time** 逐渐地，慢慢地，经过了适当时候就……（此处不译为“及时地”）
  ✎ You’ll get used to it <u>in time</u>. 你慢慢就会习惯他了。
  + 同义词：
    **in due time**
    **with time**
    **with the <u>passing/ passage</u> of time**
> 仿写第1段末句
  现在医务界(medical field)弥漫(prevail)着一种不正之风(a bad practice)，这已经成了一个公认的事实。医生给病人开出(prescribe)过分昂贵的药，而病人不得不给医生掏红包以换取更好的治疗和更安全的手术。
  It has become an accepted fact that a bad practice is prevailing in the medical field. Doctors prescribe much more expensive medicine than necessary and patients, for their part, have to give doctors ‘hongbao’,money in a red envelope, for better treatment and safer surgery.

> 仿写第2段首句
  谁也没想到在村子里竟然藏着一个从来也没有被认出来(recognize)过的谋杀犯。
  No one suspected that there might be a murderer hiding in the village who had never been recognized.
+ **the case**: a true situation 实情（详见L22笔记）
+ **听说，获悉**
  **learn <u>of/ about</u>**
  **know <u>of/ about</u>**
  **hear <u>of/ about</u>**
  后接that从句时，须删掉介词。that从句不用在介词后。
+ **everyone 与 every one**
  单独使用，几乎没有区别；其后加介词 of 时，必须用every one。
  ✎ …… poisoned <u>every one of</u> her five husbands.（L24）
+ **none other than** 不是别人，正是……
> 仿写第2段倒数第2句
  邻居们惊悉谋杀犯不是别人，正是受害者的妻子，而这个女人在年轻时一连毒死了自己的五个丈夫。
  Neighbors here were astonished to learn that the murderer was none other than the victim’s wife who had, in her youth, poisoned every one of her five husbands.
+ **a third = another** 另一个（辨：the third 第三）
  ✎ Mendoza met Humphries in the ring on a later occasion and he lost for <u>a second</u> time. 又一次（L21）
+ ┏ …… a third brother who was supposed to have died <u>as a young man</u>.（原文）
  ┗ …… a third brother who was supposed to have died <u>when (he was) a young man</u>.
  ┗ …… a third brother who was supposed to have died <u>in his youth</u>.
  ┗ …… a third brother who was supposed to have died <u>when young</u>.
  ┗ …… a third brother who was supposed to have died <u>young</u>.
  （✎ Only the good die <u>young</u>. 好人不长命。）
+ ┏ keep a secret 保密
  ┗ reveal a secret 揭秘
  a secret becomes known 秘密被公开了（L24）
+ **old - older - oldest** 没有对象限制，即可指人也可指事物
  **old - elder - eldest** 通常指人，但在比较人的年龄时要用前者——older
  ✎ Eric had been <u>the eldest</u> son of the family, very much <u>older</u> than his two brothers.（原文）
+ **be obliged to do** 被迫做某事；必须/不得不做某事（L1）
+ join
  + 直接 + 宾语：表示加入一个组织，成为长期成员。
    ✎ <u>join</u> the army 参军
    ✎ <u>join</u> the party 入党
  + join in：参加某次活动
    ✎ <u>join in</u> the party 参加聚会
  + 参军的相关表达：
    **enlist in** the army 参军
    **be in the service** 在服役
    **recruit** 募兵（非强制）
    **conscript [英]/ draft [美]** 征兵（强制）
    ✎ He was <u>conscripted</u> during the Second World War.（课后题-10）
    Have you ever <u>been in the service</u>? 你当过兵吗？
    So why did you <u>enlist</u>? 所以你为什么参了军？
    I <u>was drafted into the army</u> last year. 我去年入伍的。
+ 基数词与序数词
  ┏ 第二次世界大战
  ┗ the Second World War（序数词）
  ┗ World War Ⅱ（基数词）
  ┏ 第一章
  ┗ the First Chapter（序数词）
  ┗ Chapter One（基数词）
+ army life = life **in** the army（L12）
  ✎ As he hated <u>life in the army</u>, he decided to desert……（课后题-6）
+ ┏ <u>Fearing</u> the authorities,……（原文）
  ┗ <u>Afraid of</u> the authorities,……（同义表达）
  ┗ Fearing <u>the penalty from</u> the authorities,……（原文补全）
+ **the authorities** 当局，政府，管理部门，~~权威们~~（通常复数，固定搭配）
  ✎ the local authorities 地方政府
  ✎ the French/ Chinese authorities 法国政府/中国政府
  ✎ It is all too easy to blame <u>the railway authorities</u> when something does go wrong. 铁路当局（L37）
  + 表示 **政府** 的词：
    **government**
    **administration** 表示某一届政府
    ✎ the Clinton/ Bush <u>administration</u> 克林顿政府/布什政府
    **regime** 政府，当局，政权（带贬义，强调非民选）
    ✎ a fascist <u>regime</u> 一个法西斯政权
+ **in hiding** 处在藏匿状态/之中（习语）
  ✎ The frightened family lived <u>in hiding</u> for three years. 这家人吓坏了，隐姓埋名躲藏了3年。
+ in action 在战斗中，~~在行动中~~（通常用于以下习语）
  **be killed/ wounded in action** 在战斗中牺牲/负伤
  **be reported missing in action** 在战斗中被报道失踪
  表示战斗的词：**battle**
  ✎ Young men who have reason to fear that they will <u>be killed in battle</u> may justifiably feel bitter in the thought that they have been cheated of the best things that life has to offer.（B4L11）
+ They were **tight-mouthed**. 守口如瓶的
  相同结构的词（名词 + ed = 形容词，多表示人的特征）：
  **big-mouthed** 大嘴巴的；多嘴的
  **big-eyed** 大眼睛的
  **blue-eyed** 蓝眼睛的
> 仿写第3段倒数第4句（形式宾语）
  他觉得有责任把这个孤儿抚养成人。
  He thought **it** <u>his duty</u> **to bring up the orphan**.
  我觉得无法抵制诱惑。（仿写末句，同样是形式宾语）
  I found **it** <u>impossible</u> **to resist temptation**.
  I found that it was impossible to resist temptation.（复合句，啰嗦）
  总结：真正宾语较长，且有宾语补足语时，可将形式宾语放至原宾语位置，将真正宾语放至宾语补足语后面。
+ **<u>live/ lead</u> a…… life** 过着一种……样的生活
  ✎ Eric <u>had lived/ led the life of a recluse/ hermit</u>.（原文同义改写）
  ✎ All these years, Eric had lived <u>the life of a hermit</u>.（课后题-11）
  ✎ They can be friendly and affectionate towards humans, but they <u>lead mysterious lives</u> of their own as well.（L9）
+ **不知道**
  **be unaware of……**
  **be unconscious of……**
  **not know……**
  **not realize……**
  **have no idea……**
  ┏ …… quite unaware of the fact that……（原文）
  ┗ …… quite unconscious of the fact that……
  ┗ …… never knowing/ realizing that……
  ┗ …… not having the slightest idea that……
  ✎ He used to work at night, <u>never realizing</u> that he had become the ghost of Endley.（课后题-12）

---

## **Lesson 31 - A lovable eccentric**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>True eccentrics never deliberately set out to draw attention to themselves. They disregard social conventions without being conscious that they are doing anything extraordinary. This invariably wins them the love and respect of others, for they add colour to the dull routine of everyday life.
Up to the time of his death, Richard Colson was one of the most notable figures in our town. He was a shrewd and wealthy businessman, but most people in the town hardly knew anything about this side of his life. He was known to us all as Dickie and his eccentricity had become legendary long before he died.

Dickie disliked snobs intensely. Though he owned a large car, he hardly ever used it, preferring always to go on foot. Even when it was raining heavily, he refused to carry an umbrella. One day, he walked into an expensive shop after having been caught in a particularly heavy shower. He wanted to buy a £300 watch for his wife, but he was in such a bedraggled condition that an assistant refused to serve him. Dickie left the shop without a word and returned carrying a large cloth bag. As it was extremely heavy, he dumped it on the counter. The assistant asked him to leave, but Dickie paid no attention to him and requested to see the manager. Recognizing who the customer was, the manager was most apologetic and reprimanded the assistant severely. When Dickie was given the watch, the presented the assistant with the cloth bag. It contained £300 in pennies. He insisted on the assistant’s counting the money before he left — 30,000 pennies in all! On another occasion, he invited a number of important critics to see his private collection of modern paintings. This exhibition received a great deal of attention in the press, for though the pictures were supposed to be the work of famous artists, they had in fact been painted by Dickie. It took him four years to stage this elaborate joke simply to prove that critics do not always know what they are talking about.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **lovable/ loveable** a. （人或动物）可爱的
  ✎ a <u>lovable</u> eccentric/ actor/ dog 可爱的怪人/演员/狗
  同义替换：
  **adorable, endearing, winsome**
  近义词：
  **cute** 小而可爱
  ✎ a <u>cute</u> baby/ puppy/ kitten 一个可爱的婴儿/小狗/小猫
  **beloved** 深爱着的（多指亲人，尤指配偶，偏书面）
  ✎ my <u>beloved</u> wife/ husband
+ **eccentric** n. 古怪的人；a. 异常的，古怪的（仅指人-无贬义）
  **eccentricity** n. 怪癖，古怪行为
  ✎ One of his <u>eccentricities</u> is sleeping under the bed. 他的怪癖之一是在床底下睡觉。
  + 发音变化相同的例子：**exhibit** v. 展览；n. 展览品；**exhibition** n. 展览，展览会 
  + 近义词（含贬义）
    **freak, oddball, weirdo** 怪胎
    **sicko, pervert** 变态
+ **disregard** v. 漠视，不顾，不理睬
  **= ignore**
  ✎ You shouldn’t <u>disregard/ ignore</u> safety problems. 你不应该漠视安全问题。
  ✎ When I saw Jane, I stopped and smiled, but she <u>ignored</u> me and walked on.
  (A) refused; (B) ignored; (C) denied; (D) missed（1987考研英语27题）
  + 近义词：
    **neglect, overlook** 忽视
    ✎ The joys of travel, having long <u>neglected</u> the disabled, are opening up to virtually anyone who has the means.（means 钱，~~方法~~）
    (A) omitted; (B) missed; (C) neglected; (D) discarded
  + 同义替换（漠视）：
    **pay no attention to……**
    **take no notice of……**
    **turn a deaf ear to……** 充耳不闻
    **turn a blind eye to……** 视而不见
+ **convention** n. 习俗，风俗，惯例
  ✎ social <u>conventions</u> 社会习俗
  ✎ accepted <u>conventions</u> 公认的惯例
  ✎ international <u>conventions</u> 国际惯例
  + **习俗，惯例**：
    **custom, tradition**
    **institution, practice**
    ✎ On the other hand, your stomach would turn at the idea of frying potatoes in animal fat — the normally accepted <u>practice</u> in many northern countries.（L23）
  + **conventional** a. 传统的；约定俗成的
    <u>conventional</u> values 传统价值观
    <u>conventional</u> lifestyle 传统生活方式
    <u>conventional</u> measures 传统/常规措施
    同义替换：
    **customary, traditional**
+ **conscious** a. 感觉到的，意识到的
  + 搭配：
    **be conscious of……** 知道某事，意识到某事（+ 名词）
    **be conscious (of the fact) that……**（+ 从句）
    **be aware of……**
    **be aware (of the fact) that……**
    反义搭配（加前缀un-）：
    **be unconscious of……** 不知道某事，没有意识到某事
    **be unconscious (of the fact) that……**
    **be unaware of……**
    **be unaware (of the fact) that……**
  + **consciousness** n. 意识
    ✎ enhance people’s <u>consciousness</u> of public morality 提高人民群众的公德意识
+ **intensely** ad. 强烈地
  **intense** a. 强烈的（常指感觉、感情）
  <u>intense</u> heat/ cold/ pain 酷热/严寒/剧痛
  <u>intense</u> love/ hatred/ suffering 强烈的爱/恨/痛苦
  + 易混词：
    **intensive** a. 密集的
    ✎ an <u>intensive</u> English course 高强度的英语课程
    ✎ two weeks of <u>intensive</u> negotiations 两周密集的谈判
    ┏ <u>intensive</u> reading 精读
    ┗ <u>extensive</u> reading 泛读
    组成复合词：
    labor-<u>intensive</u> industry 劳动密集型产业
    capital-<u>intensive</u> industry 资金密集型产业
    technology-<u>intensive</u> industry 技术密集型产业
    knowledge-<u>intensive</u> industry 知识密集型产业
+ **apologetic** a. 道歉的，表示歉意的
  **be apologetic about……** 对……表示歉意
  ✎ He <u>was apologetic about</u> his late arrival. 他对迟到表示歉意。
  **apologize** v. 道歉
  **apologize to sb. for sth.** 因为某事而向某人道歉
  ✎ He <u>apologized to</u> me <u>for</u> his late arrival.
  **apology** n. 道歉，歉意
  **make an apology to sb. for sth.** 因为某事而向某人道歉
  **owe sb. an apology** 欠某人一个道歉
  **say sorry to sb. for sth.** 因为某事而向某人道歉
+ **reprimand** v. 训斥，批评（L16）
  **= rebuke**
  **<u>reprimand/ rebuke</u> sb. for sth.** 因为某事而批评某人（多用于上下级之间的责备）
  ✎ I <u>was reprimanded/ rebuked</u> by my manager <u>for</u> being late.
  + “**批评**” 的相关表达（部分复制于L16）：
    **accuse sb. of sth.** 指控，控告/（愤怒地）指责某人（L16）
    ✎ Dimitri immediately went to Aleko’s house and angrily <u>accused</u> him <u>of</u> stealing the lamb.（L16）
    **criticize sb. for sth.** 因为某事而批评某人（正式地，无感情色彩）
    ✎ He <u>was criticized for</u> his delay in dealing with the matter. 他因为在处理这个事件中耽搁了而受到了批评。
    **censure sb. for sth.** 严厉地批评某人（措辞重，不一定有感情色彩）
    ✎ Ministers <u>were censured for</u> their lack of decisiveness during the crisis. 因为在危机期间不够果断，部长们受到了严厉的指责。
    **scold sb. for sth.** 因为某事指责某人（多用于长辈对晚辈）
    ✎ His mother <u>scolded</u> him <u>for</u> breaking her favorite vase. 因为他打碎了妈妈最心爱的花瓶，他的妈妈批评了他。
    **reproach sb. for sth.** 强调因为没有做该做的事而指责（偏文言）
    ✎ He <u>reproached</u> me <u>for</u> not answering his letter. 他因为我没有回他的信而指责我。
    **<u>blame sb. for sth. / blame sth. on sb.</u>** 强调把某事归咎于某人，强调某人应该为此负责
    ┏ 他们把这次的失败归咎到了乔治头上。
    ┗ They <u>blamed</u> George <u>for</u> the failure.
    ┗ They <u>blamed</u> the failure <u>on</u> George.
    **condemn A <u>for/ as</u> B** 因为B而谴责A / 把A谴责为是B（大家一致地批评）
    ✎ The movie <u>was condemned for</u> its sexism. 这部电影因为性别歧视而受到谴责。
    ✎ The terrorist attack <u>was condemned as</u> an act of barbarism and cowardice. 这次恐怖袭击被谴责为是野蛮和懦弱的行径。（barbar 野蛮人）
+ **stage** v. 组织，策划，举行，举办；n. 舞台
  英文释义：organize
  ✎ <u>stage</u> a strike/ a riot/ a plot/ a coup/ an exhibition
  组织/策划一次罢工/暴动/阴谋/政变/展览
  ✎ China <u>staged</u> the 2008 Olympics. 中国举办了2008年奥运会。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **deliberately** 故意地，有意地，成心地（L27）
  同义替换：
  **intentionally, on purpose**
  （intention 目的，意图；intentional 有意的）
+ **set out to do** 带着目的去做某事（L5）
  英文释义：begin a job, task, etc with a particular aim or goal
  ✎ The journalist immediately <u>set out to obtain</u> these important facts, but he took a long time to send them.（L5）
  ✎ Dimitri at once <u>set out to find</u> the thief.（L16）
  ✎ We never <u>set out to hurt</u> you, Victor. And I’m sorry we did.（《绝望主妇》）
  **set <u>out/ off</u> = start <u>out/ off</u>** 动身，出发（不强调出行方式）（L10、L20）
  ✎ Four days after <u>setting out</u>, while the *Titanic* was sailing across the icy waters of the North Atlantic, ……（L10）
  ✎ After making a short test flight at 4,15 a.m., Bleriot <u>set off</u> half an hour later.（L20）
+ **draw (one’s) attention** 吸引(某人的)注意力
  **= <u>attract/ capture/ catch/ arrest/ command/ get</u> (one’s) attention**
  ✎ This <u>attracted the attention of</u> Richard Humphries who was then the most eminent boxer in England.（L21）
  反义搭配：
  **receive (one’s) attention** 受到(某人的)关注
  ✎ This exhibition <u>received a great deal of attention</u> in the press, ……（本文）
+ **without being conscious (of the fact) that……**（+ 从句）介词短语作状语（原文结构）
  **without being conscious of……**（+ 名词）
  **without being aware (of the fact) that……**（+ 从句）
  **without being aware of……**（+ 名词）
  ✎ People tend to amass possessions, sometimes <u>without being aware of</u> doing so.（L59）
  **(being) unconscious (of the fact) that……** 非谓语动词作状语
  **(being) unconscious of……**
  **(being) unaware (of the fact) that……**
  **(being) unaware of……**
  ✎ He used to sleep during the day and work at night, <u>quite unaware of the fact that</u> he had become the ghost of Endley.（L30）
  ✎ They disregard social conventions, <u>quite unconscious/ unaware of the fact that</u> they are doing anything extraordinary.（原文同义改写）
> 仿写第2句
  他们无视安全问题，意识不到自己的所作所为有什么危险之处。
  They disregard safety problems, without being conscious that they are doing anything dangerous.（介词短语作状语）
  They disregard safety problems, quite unconscious/ unaware of the fact that they are doing anything dangerous.（非谓语动词作状语）

+ **invariably: always** 总是……
+ ┏ **win sb. sth.** 为某人赢得某物
  ┗ **win sth. for sb.**
  ✎ My sincerity <u>won me her heart</u>. 我的真诚为自己赢得了芳心。
  ✎ My sincerity <u>won her heart for me</u>.
+ **add color to sth.** 给某物增添颜色；使某物更有趣/吸引人（固定搭配）
  ✎ Intelligent use of metaphors can <u>add color to</u> your writing. 巧妙地使用暗喻可以为你的写作增添色彩。
  + 同义搭配：
    **add <u>luster[美]/ lustre[英]</u> to sth.** 给某物增加光泽
    **add <u>flavor/ spice</u> to sth.** 给某物增加味道（flavor 风味；spice 调料）
    **add <u>variety</u> to sth.** 给某物增加多样性
+ **dull** 无聊的；单调的；颜色暗淡的；钝的；迟钝的
  本文相当于：**boring, monotonous**（mono-：一；ton：tone 声调）
  **the dull routine of everyday life** 平淡的日常生活
> 仿写第1段末句
  网上冲浪总是能赢得年轻人的痴迷(fascination)，因为它给平淡的日常生活增添了一丝亮色。
  Surfing the Net invariably wins itself the fascination of the young, for it adds color to the dull routine of everyday life.
+ **up to……** 
  + ① 直到……；
    **up until……**
    **up till……**（till单独使用，不太正式，一般不用于句首）
    **until……**
  + ② 不超过……：最多是……
    **less than……**
    ✎ In Europe, taxes account for <u>up to</u> four-fifths of the retail price. 在欧洲，税收最多占零售价格的五分之四。
+ **notable** 著名的，~~值得注意的~~
  ✎ …… ‘the most valiant soldier and most notable leader, Signor Giovanni Haukodue’.（L14）
+ **figure** 重要的人物
  ✎ One of the most colourful <u>figures</u> in boxing history was Daniel Mendoza, who was born in 1764.（L21）
+ **this side of his life**
  = his shrewdness and wealthiness
  ✎ Harry is very thrifty, but in the presence of his friends he never shows <u>this side of his life (= his thriftiness)</u>. 哈里非常节约，但在朋友面前，他从不展现自己生活的这方面。
+ **know sb./ sth. as sth.** 把某人/某事物称作某物（主动被动都可，被动更常见）
  ✎ The disease <u>is</u> commonly <u>known as</u> Mad Cow Disease. 这种疾病通常被称为疯牛病。
  ✎ He soon made a name for himself and came to <u>be known</u> **to** the italians <u>as</u> Giovanni Acuto.（L14）
  ✎ 美国人把Earvin Johnson称为魔术师约翰逊(Magic Johnson)。
  Earvin Johnson <u>is known</u> **to** the Americans <u>as</u> ‘Magic Johnson’.
  ✎ 中国人把李白称为诗仙(poet-immortal)。 
  Li Bai <u>is known</u> **to** the Chinese <u>as</u> ‘poet-immortal’.
+ **legendary** 
  + 传奇的，正史中没有的
    ✎ Robin Hood is a <u>legendary</u> hero. 罗宾汉是个传奇英雄。
  + 著名的 **= famous/ well-known**（本文）
    ✎ the <u>legendary</u> Hollywood director Steven Spielberg 好莱坞著名导演史蒂芬斯皮尔伯格
    ✎ The Chinese <u>are legendary for</u> their hospitality. 中国人以好客著称。
> 仿写第2段末句
  在上梁山前很久，武松的力量和勇敢就已经很有名了。
  Wu Song’s strength and courage had become legendary long before he joined the Liangshan rebels.（rebel 叛军，叛党；反叛）
+ ┏ Dickie <u>disliked</u> snobs intensely.
  ┗ Dickie <u>**hate**d/ **abhor**red/ **detest**ed/ **loathe**d/ **abominate**d</u> snobs intensely.
  ┗ Dickie found snobs <u>**repellent**/ **repulsive**/ **revolting**/ **disgusting**</u>.
  ┗ Snobs <u>**repel**led/ **repulse**d/ **revolt**ed/ **disgust**ed</u> Dickie intensely.（L23）
+ **hardly ever** 几乎从来没有发生过（L18）
  **= almost never, seldom, rarely**
+ **prefer**
  **prefer to do rather than do**
  ✎ ……, preferring always to go on foot <u>rather than go in his car</u>.（原文改）
> 仿写第3段第2句
  尽管他有几个保镖(bodyguard)，但他很少让他们陪着他(accompany him)，总是更喜欢独自一个人(on his own)去散步(take a stroll)。
  Though he owned several bodyguards, he hardly ever asked them to accompany him, preferring always to take a stroll on his own.
+ 雨下得大
  It’s raining <u>hard/ heavily</u>.
  It’s pouring.
  It’s raining cats and dogs.（口语）
+ having been caught
  **动名词的时态和语态**（L4）
  时态 / 语态 | 主动 | 被动 
  :----: | ----: | ----: 
  **一般时** | doing | being done
  **完成时** | having done | having been done
  
  ┏ …… **after** <u>having been caught</u> in a particularly heavy shower.（原文 - after作介词，引导时间状语）
  ┗ …… **after** he <u>had been caught</u> in a particularly heavy shower.（after作连词，引导时间状语从句）
+ **be caught in……** 赶上/遭遇倒霉事（被此事困住，未必造成严重损害）（L25）
  ✎ He <u>was caught in</u> a storm/ traffic jam. 他赶上暴风雨/塞车了。
  **be struck by……** 赶上/遭遇倒霉事（且遭受严重损失）
  ✎ In August, she <u>was struck by</u> a very heavy storm during which her rudder was torn away.（L25）
+ 价值多少钱的某物
  a £300 watch（本文）
  **金钱 + worth of + 物品**（L6）
  ✎ a £300 worth of watch（原文换用）
+ ┏ …… but he was in such a bedraggled condition that……（such + 名词 + that……（此结构有名词，更显正式））（原文）
  ┗ …… but he was so bedraggled that……（so + 形容词/副词 + that……）
  ┏ His family was <u>so impoverished that</u> he could hardly afford his tuition. 他的家庭是如此的贫困，以至于他几乎付不起学费。
  ┗ His family was <u>in such an impoverished condition that</u> he could hardly afford his tuition.
+ ┏ **serve sb. with sth.** 把商品拿给顾客
  ┗ **serve sth. to sb.**
  ┏ …… refused to <u>serve him with the watch</u>.（原文补全）
  ┗ …… refused to <u>serve the watch to him</u>.
+ leave without a word 一语不发地离开
  近义表达：**take French leave** 不辞而别，以法国人的方式离开（英国人讽刺法国人不讲礼貌）
  **Dumb dogs are dangerous.** 不声不响的人最可怕。（谚语）
+ **be extremely heavy** 特别沉
  **weigh a ton** 有一吨那么沉（习语-夸张）
  ┏ The chair <u>weighs a ton</u>.
  ┗ The chair <u>is extremely heavy</u>.
+ ……, he **dumped** it on the counter. **拟声词**-重物落地
  He **slammed** the door. 他砰地关上门。
  We all **clapped** our hands. 我们都鼓起掌来。
  The soldier **clicked** his heels. 士兵咔嗒一声碰了一下脚后跟。（表示立正的动作）
  Don’t **clatter** the dishes —— you’ll wake the baby up. 别把盘子弄得咣铛响，你会把婴儿吵醒的。
  I’ll **smack** your bottom if you don’t behave yourself. 如果你不守规矩，我就啪啪打你屁股。（辨：smash 打碎）
+ ┏ Dickie <u>paid no attention to</u> him（原文）
  ┗ Dickie <u>ignored</u> him.
  ┗ Dickie <u>took no notice of</u> him.
  ┗ Dickie <u>turned a deaf ear to</u> him.
  ┗ Dickie <u>turned a blind eye to</u> him.
+ **request** （客客气气地）请求
  ┏ You’re <u>requested</u> not to smoke here. 请您不要在这里抽烟。（客气请求）
  ┗ You’re <u>required</u> not to smoke here. 这里不允许你抽烟！（强制命令）
+ ┏ **most** apologetic **极其地**抱歉
  ┗ **the most** apologetic 最抱歉
+ ┏ When Dickie was given the watch, the presented the assistant with the cloth bag.（原文-**被动：避免频繁变化主语，使句子简洁流畅**）
  ┗ When the assistant gave Dickie the watch, Dickie presented the assistant with the cloth bag.（主动）
  ✎ She gave a lecture on modern American poetry and <u>was attentively listened to</u>. 她做了一场关于美国现代诗歌的讲座，大家都很专心地听。
  ✎ The old professor wheeled himself to the platform and <u>was warmly applauded by the students</u>. 老教授坐轮椅到讲台上，收到了学生们的热烈掌声。
+ ┏ **present sb. with sth.** 把某物呈递给某人（L22）
  ┗ **present sth. to sb.**
  ✎ He entered the cell and <u>presented</u> the letter <u>to</u> the aristocrat.（L22）
+ £300 **in** pennies 用……，以……
  ✎ He paid me <u>in</u> cash/ dollars. 他是用现金/美元支付的。
  ✎ Write it <u>in</u> ink/ pencil/ English. 用钢笔/铅笔/英语写。

#### 👾 **动名词的逻辑主语**
一般来说，动名词的逻辑主语在正式文体中用属格（所有格），在非正式文体中用普通格。在《新概念英语》和考试中，均以正式文体为准。
┏ Do you mind <u>**my** smoking</u> here?（正式）你介意我在这抽烟吗？
┗ Do you mind <u>**me** smoking</u> here?（非正式）
┏ <u>**Your** falling</u> into the river was the climax of the whole trip.（正式）你掉进河里是整个旅程的高潮。
┗ <u>**You** falling</u> into the river was the climax of the whole trip.（非正式）
**出现下列情况时，即使在正式文体中，动名词的逻辑主语也习惯使用普通格。**
1. **逻辑主语为名词，且指物而非指人。**
  ✎ The children are looking forward to <u>**spring** coming</u>. 孩子们正在盼望着春天的到来。
2. **逻辑主语为多个名词。**
  ✎ Do you remember <u>**Mary and her mother** coming</u> to see us last June? 你还记得去年六月玛丽和她妈妈来看我们吗？
3. **逻辑主语为以“s”结尾的名词。**
  ✎ It’s a disaster <u>**the bosses** shutting</u> all those factories. 老板们把那些工厂都关了，这真是场灾难。
4. **逻辑主语与动名词分离。**
  ✎ I remember <u>**mother**</u> once <u>telling</u> us a story about the fox. 我记得妈妈曾经给我们讲过一个关于狐狸的故事。
5. **逻辑主语为不定代词，如：someone，everything，something；**
  **或指示代词，如：this，that。**
  ✎ They complained about <u>**everything** going</u> wrong. 他们抱怨一切都出了问题。
  ✎ He disapproved of <u>**that** being</u> said about Mary. 他不赞成玛丽说的那些话。

+ ┏ **insist on + 名词** 坚持要求某物
  ┗ **insist that + 从句**（从句须用should do型虚拟语气）
  ✎ He insisted that the assistant <u>(should) count</u> the money before he left,……（原文补全）
  ✎ Even though the noble was expected to read the letter at each performance, he always <u>insisted that it should be written out in full</u>.（L22）
  ✎ He always <u>insisted on **its** being written out in full</u>.（L22课后题-5）（所有格）
  ┏ Next came a horse, swimming bravely, but we were afraid that the strength of the current would <u>prevent **its** landing anywhere</u> before it became exhausted.（L56）（所有格）
  ┗ The strength of the current would prevent <u>it from landing</u> anywhere before it became exhausted.（L56课后题-7）（prevent sb. from doing sth.）
+ **receive + n.** 受到，得到，遭到，~~收到某物~~（L8）
  ✎ No creature has <u>received</u> more <u>praise</u> and <u>abuse</u> than the common garden snail.（L23）
  ✎ These young people, who love the peace of mountains, always <u>receive a warm welcome</u> at St. Bernard’s monastery.（L8）
+ **the press** 新闻界（L5）
  **the freedom of <u>the press</u>** 新闻自由；出版自由
  ✎ In democratic countries any efforts to restrict <u>the freedom of the press</u> are rightly condemned.（L45）
+ **work** 表示“作品，著作”时，可数不可数都对
+ 末句近义表达
  ┗ …… critics do not always **talk sense**. 说得对，说得有理
  ┗ …… critics sometimes **talk nonsense**. 胡说八道

---

## **Lesson 32 - A lost ship**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>The salvage operation had been a complete failure. The small ship, <i>Elkor</i>, which had been searching the Barents Sea for weeks, was on its way home. A radio message from the mainland had been received by the ship’s captain instructing him to give up the search. The captain knew that another attempt would be made later, for the sunken ship he was trying to find had been carrying a precious cargo of gold bullion.

Despite the message, the captain of the <i>Elkor</i> decided to try once more. The sea bed was scoured with powerful nets and there was tremendous excitement on board when a chest was raised from the bottom. Though the crew were at first under the impression that the lost ship had been found, the contents of the chest proved them wrong. What they had in fact found was a ship which had been sunk many years before.

The chest contained the personal belongings of a seaman, Alan Fielding. There were books, clothing and photographs, together with letters which the seaman had once received from his wife. The captain of the <i>Elkor</i> ordered his men to salvage as much as possible from the wreck. Nothing of value was found, but the numerous items which were brought to the surface proved to be of great interest. From a heavy gun that was raised, the captain realized that the ship must have been a cruiser. In another chest, which contained the belongings of a ship’s officer, there was an unfinished letter which had been written on March 14th, 1943. The captain learnt from the letter that the name of the lost ship was the <i>Karen</i>. The most valuable find of all was the ship’s log book, parts of which it was still possible to read. From this the captain was able to piece together all the information that had come to light. The <i>Karen</i> had been sailing in a convoy to Russia when she was torpedoed by an enemy submarine. This was later confirmed by a naval official at the Ministry of Defence after the <i>Elkor</i> had returned home. All the items that were found were sent to the War Museum.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **salvage** v. 营救，拯救，打捞（L7-此部分内容全部复制于之前笔记）
  **salvage…… from……** 从……中把……救出来（仅指救东西，不能指救人）
  ✎ He tried desperately to <u>salvage</u> belongings <u>from</u> the burning house. 他拼命地试着从着火的房子里把他的财产救回来。
  **rescue/ save** 救，拯救（救物救人都可）
  ✎ When you <u>rescued</u> your trousers, did you find the note was whiter than white?（L7）
  ✎ When a passing tanker <u>rescued</u> them five days later, both men were genuinely sorry that they had to leave.（L12）
  **pick up sb.** （用飞机、轮船）搭救某人；（从机场、火车站）把某人接回来
  ✎ The ‘Antoinette’ floated on the water until Latham <u>was picked up</u> by a ship.（L20）
+ **sunken** a. 沉没的；深陷的（只能作定语）
  ✎ <u>sunken</u> treasure 沉入水中的宝藏（treasure 指金银财宝，不可数）
  ✎ a <u>sunken</u> ship 一艘沉船
  【✘】The ship was <u>sunken</u>.
  【✔】The ship <u>has sunk/ has been sunk</u>. 这艘船沉没了/被击沉了。
  ✎ her <u>sunken</u> eyes/ cheeks 她深陷的双眼/脸颊
  相关词：
  **unsinkable** a. 不可能沉没的（作定语、表语，无限制）
  ✎ At that time, however, she was not only the largest ship that had ever been built, but was regarded as <u>unsinkable</u>, for she had sixteen watertight compartments.（L10）
+ **scour** v. 彻底搜索
  + 相关表达：
    **search (a place) for……**（在某个地方）搜寻……
    ✎ The detective is <u>searching for</u> clues. 侦探正在寻找线索。
    ✎ The small ship, *Elkor*, which had been <u>searching</u> the Barents Sea for weeks, was on its way home.（本文）
    **hunt for……**（L1）
    ✎ I’m <u>hunting for</u> a job now. 我现在正在找工作。（动词hunt）
    ✎ The <u>hunt for</u> the puma began in a small village where a woman picking blackberries saw ‘a large cat’ only five yards away from her.（名词hunt）（L1）
    **fumble for……** 摸索着寻找……（谐音“翻包”）
    ✎ She <u>fumbled for</u> her keys in her purse. 她在钱包里摸索着找钥匙。
    ✎ If you are lucky enough to get a sleeper, you spend half the night staring at the small blue light in the ceiling, or <u>fumbling</u> to find your ticket for inspection.（fumble to do sth.，用for的话就会出现连续两个for，别扭）（L44）
  
  **scour a place for……**（scour 冲刷）
  ✎ The sea bed <u>was scoured</u> with powerful nets……（本文）
  近义搭配：
  **comb a place for……** 彻底搜索（comb 梳头，梳理）
  ✎ The police are <u>combing</u> the woods <u>for</u> the fugitive. 警察为了搜寻逃犯正在彻查树林。
+ **chest** n. 大箱子（多盛放贵重物品）
  各种**箱子**：
  cardboard box 纸板箱（L19）
  packing case 板条箱；装货箱（L34）
  suitcase 行李箱（L11）
  boot[英]/ trunk[美] 汽车后备箱（L26）
  money box / piggy bank 存钱罐（L15）
+ **belongings = things** n. 财产，动产，所有物（惯用复数）
  ✎ He told me to unpack my <u>things</u> and then come down to dinner.（L24）
  **<u>property/ real estate</u>** [U] 不动产
  ✎ the <u>property</u> market 房地产市场
  ✎ <u>real estate</u> agent 房产经纪人
  **possessions/ property** 泛指财产（possessions惯用复数；property不可数）
  ✎ People tend to amass <u>possessions</u>, sometimes without being aware of doing so.（L59）
  **assets** 资产（惯用复数）
  ✎ liquid/ fixed/ tangible/ intangible <u>assets</u>
  流动/固定/有形/无形资产
+ **cruiser** n. 巡洋舰
  前缀：**cru- = cross**
  同前缀词：**cruise** 巡航；**crucial** 至关重要的；**crusade** 圣战
  ✎ a <u>crusade</u> against official corruption 反腐运动
+ **find** n. 被发现的人或物（通常褒义）
  ✎ My new secretary is a real <u>find</u>. 我的新秘书真是找对人了。
  ✎ I made a great <u>find</u> in a second-hand bookstore. 我在一个二手书店淘到了一本好书。
  **buy/ bargain** n. 便宜货（L28）
  ✎ Oh my! Here’s a real <u>buy</u>. It’s a <u>bargain</u>. This house just came on the market. 这个房子刚刚上市。（《走遍美国》）
  **must** n. 必要的事物
  ✎ W1: What we need is a roommate who is neat and considerate.
  W2: Let’s write that in the ad: neatness and consideration a <u>must</u>. What do the speakers hope to do?
  Answer: Find a person to share their apartment.（托福听力真题）
+ **naval** a. 海军的
  相关词：**navy** 海军；**land force** 陆军；**air force** 空军
  词根：**nav/ nau =  ship**
  同根词：
  **<u>nav</u>igation** 航海
  **<u>nau</u>sea** 恶心；**<u>nau</u>seate** 使某人恶心
  **<u>nau</u>tical** 船舶的；航海的 ✎ <u>nautical</u> chart 航海图 ✎ <u>nautical</u> mile 海里
  **aero<u>nau</u>tics** 航空学；**astro<u>nau</u>tics** 航天学；**astro<u>nau</u>t** 航天员
  ✎ Beijing University of Aero<u>nau</u>tics and Astro<u>nau</u>tics 北京航空航天大学


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **operation**
  + work/ activity/ action 工作；活动；行动
    ✎ rescue/ relief/ cleanup <u>operation</u> 营救/救济/清洁工作/行动
    ✎ For them this is a major <u>operation</u> which involves considerable planning.（L41）
  + [C] 手术
    ┏ The patient will **have/ undergo** an operation **on** appendicitis. 患者表达
    ┗ The doctor will **<u>do/ perform/ carry out</u>** an operation **on** the patient **for** appendicitis. 医生表达
    近义词：**surgery** [U] 泛指外科手术
    ✎ He is an authority on <u>surgery</u>. 他是外科手术的权威。
+ ┏ The salvage operation <u>had been a complete failure</u>.（原文）
  ┗ The salvage operation <u>had proved (to be) a complete failure</u>.
  ┗ The salvage operation <u>had been a (complete) fiasco</u>.
  ┗ The salvage operation <u>had been in vain</u>.（be in vain 徒劳）
+ 作同位语时，冠词（尤其是定冠词the）一般可去掉。
  ┏ The loss of <u>the *Titanic*</u>（L10）
  ┗ The great ship, <u>Titanic</u>, sailed for New York from Southampton on April 10th, 1912.
  ┏ <u>The *Cutty Sark*</u>（L25）
  ┗ One of the most famous sailing ships of the nineteenth century, <u>the *Cutty Sark*</u>, can still be seen at Greenwich.
+ 当作状语理解的定语从句
  ┏ The small ship, Elkor, <u>**which** had been searching the Barents Sea for weeks</u>, was on its way home.（原文）该定语从句发挥的是时间状语的功能。
  ┗ The small ship, Elkor, <u>**after she** had been searching the Barents Sea for weeks</u>, was on its way home.（还原为时间状语从句）
  ┏ I have to be very careful not to offend the boss, <u>**who** could fire me at any time</u>. 我必须非常小心，不要冒犯老板，因为他随时都可能解雇我。
  ┗ I have to be very careful not to offend the boss, <u>**because he** could fire me at any time</u>.（原因状语从句）
  ┏ The action, <u>**which** has aroused universal disapproval</u>, is nevertheless the only solution. 这个行为尽管激起了普遍的反对，但它是唯一的解决方案。
  ┗ The action, <u>**although it** has aroused universal disapproval</u>, is nevertheless the only solution.（让步状语）
+ **on one’s way (to……)** 在……的路上；去往……的途中（L15）
  ✎ <u>On his way to the sweet shop</u>, he dropped his fifty pence and it bounced along the pavement and then disappeared down a drain.（L15）
> 仿写第2句
  在Ellesmere公司工作的垃圾工Alfred Bloggs，在连续工作了8小时之后，正在回家的途中。
  Alfred Bloggs, a dustman for the Ellesmere Corporation, who had been working for 8 hours on end, was on his way home.
  参考：
  …… Alfred Bloggs who worked as a dustman **for** the Ellesmere Corporation. 表示在某家公司工作（L4）
  Some plays are so successful that they run for years **on end**. 连续（L22）
+ **radio message, radiogram, telegram** 无线电报
+ **mainland** 大陆
  （英语中，默认大陆是欧洲大陆，默认海峡是英吉利海峡；中文中，默认大陆是中国大陆，默认海峡是台湾海峡）
  多作定语，修饰另外一个地方
  ✎ <u>mainland</u> Europe 欧洲大陆
  ✎ <u>mainland</u> China 中国大陆
+ 船上人员的称谓
  **captain/ skipper** 船长；**first mate** 大副
  **sailor/ seaman/ mariner** 船员/水手；**crew** 全体船员（指多艘船的船员要用复数）
  ✎ She was carrying 1,316 passengers and a <u>crew</u> of 891.（L10）
  ✎ Though the <u>crew</u> were at first under the impression that……（本文）
+ **instruct sb. to do……** 指示/指派/命令某人做某事（详见L5）
  ✎ The editor at once sent the journalist a fax <u>instructing</u> him <u>to</u> find out the exact number of steps and the height of the wall.（L5）
  ✎ Mrs. Ramsay <u>was instructed to</u> place the money in a cardboard box and to leave it outside her door.（L19）
+ ┏ **give up** the search
  ┗ **abandon** the search（更正式）
  ┗ **stop/ cease** the search 停止，终止
  ┗ **abort** the search 中止（半途而废）
> 仿写第3句（① 无灵主语，突出重点（中文习惯人作主语）；② 重要信息放句首和句尾。）
  老太太收到绑匪的一封信，命令她支付1,000英镑的赎金。
  A letter from the kidnappers had been received by the old lady instructing her to pay a ransom of £1,000.
  考古学家作出了一个有趣的发现，一尊古代的女神像原来竞是(turn out to be)一位看上去很摩登的女郎(a very modern-looking woman)。
  An interesting discovery was made by archeologists that an ancient statue of a goddess turned out to be a very modern-looking woman.
+ **make an attempt to do……** 尝试做某事
  ↓ The captain knew that <u>his attempt</u> would not be <u>the only attempt</u>.（中式英语，且啰嗦）
  ↓ The captain knew that <u>his attempt</u> would not be <u>the only one</u>.（仍然啰嗦）
  ↳ The captain knew that <u>his</u> would not be <u>the only attempt</u>.（简练。此句his是名词性物主代词，相当于his attempt；前面的his是形容词性物主代词）
  ✎ The captain knew that <u>his would not be</u> the only attempt.（课后题-4）
  **在表达效果相同的前提下，用字越少英语水平越高。**
  ↓ Our age is a tragic age. 我们的时代是一个悲剧的时代。
  ↓ Our age is a tragic one.
  ↳ Ours is a tragic age.（莎士比亚）
  **Brevity is beauty.** 简洁即是美。
+ **cargo** [C]（用**船或飞机**运输的）货物
  **freight** [U]（用各种交通工具运输的）货物
  ✎ The ship carries both <u>freight</u> and passengers. 这艘船既搭载货物也搭载乘客。
  cargo ship/ airplane 货轮/货机
  freight train 货运列车
+ **once more = one more time = once again**
+ sea bed/ sea floor/ sea bottom 海底
+ **tremendous** a. very great
  ✎ In his day, Mendoza enjoyed <u>tremendous</u> popularity.（L21）
  ✎ Though the new rudder was fitted at <u>tremendous</u> speed, it was impossible for the *Cutty Sark* to win.（L25）
  ✎ The response to this competition was <u>tremendous</u>.（L26）
+ **<u>on board/ aboard</u>**
+ 【✔】…… there was tremendous excitement on board ……（原文）
  【✘】…… people on aboard were very excited ……（中式英语）
> 仿写第2段第2句后半句（无灵主语）
  消息传来时，演播室(studio)里的人们非常激动。
  There was tremendous excitement in the studio when the news came.
  有越来越多的人对英语有兴趣。
  【✘】There are more and more people who are interested in English.
  【✔】There is growing interest in English.
  人们普遍同意妇女应该享有和男人完全的平等。
  【✘】People generally agree that women should enjoy full equality with men.
  【✔】There is general agreement that women should enjoy full equality with men.
+ **be under the impression that……** 还以为……（暗示想法其实是错的）
  ✎ Sorry, I <u>was under the impression that</u> you were the manager. 对不起，我以为你是经理。
  **give sb. the impression that……** 使某人觉得/认为……（L24）
  ✎ The sudden movement of the door made it sway slightly and it <u>gave me the impression that</u> it was about to leap out at me.（L24）
  **<u>be/ live</u> under the <u>illusion/ delusion</u> that……** 误以为……（更强调想法的错误）
  ✎ Even he still <u>lives under the illusion that</u> country life is somehow superior to town life.（L41）
  ✎ The worst thing about the do-it-yourself game is that sometimes even men <u>live under the delusion that</u> they can do anything, even when they have repeatedly been proved wrong.（L46）
+ **prove+宾语+宾补**（比加宾语从句简洁）
  ✎ The facts <u>proved their worries unnecessary</u>. 事实证明，他们的担忧是不必要的。
> 仿写第2段末句（从句夹主句，两头大中间小）
  哥伦布其实发现的不是印度，而是一个全新的大陆，在那里土著居民(aborigine)已经居住了(inhabit)两万多年了。
  What Columbus had in fact found was not India but a new continent which had been inhabited by aborigines for over twenty thousand years.
+ **clothing** [U] 衣服
  ✎ Food, <u>clothing</u>, shelter and transportation are daily necessities. 衣食住行是生活的基本必需品。
  **clothes** [C] 惯用复数
  ✎ Fine <u>clothes</u> make a man. 人靠衣裳马靠鞍。（直译：好衣服造就一个人。）（谚语）
+ **together with…… = along with……** 还有……
  ✎ Peter was murdered, <u>together/ along with</u> three guards. 皮特被谋杀了，还有三个守卫也一块死了。
  ✎ These new facts, <u>together/ along with</u> the other evidence, prove the prisoner’s innocence. 这些新的事实，加上其他证据，证明了囚犯的清白。
+ **one’s men** 表示手下的士兵/船员
  ✎ The general commanded <u>his men</u> to fire. 将军命令手下的士兵们开火。
  ✎ In times of peace, when business was bad, Hawkwood and <u>his men</u> would march into a city-state and,……（L14）
  **subordinate** 下级，下属
  ✎ He left the routine check to one of his <u>subordinates</u>. 他把例行检查留给了他的一个下属。
  **superior** 上级
  ✎ I’ll pass your complaint on to my superiors. 我会把你的投诉转交给我的上级。
  **counterpart** 对应方，（在另一个机构）与自己身份、地位相当的人
  ✎ Chinese President Xi Jinping and his American <u>counterpart</u> Barack Obama will hold talks on Monday.
  **the grassroots** （机构里）地位最低的那些人，“草根”
+ **wreck** 被毁掉的交通工具
  **shipwreck** 沉船
  ✎ Poor man! —— mentally a <u>wreck</u>. 可怜的人，简直就是脑残。（旧B4）

#### 👾 **of + 名词：描述人或事物的特征**
1. **做后置定语（比用形容词更正式）。**
  ✎ nothing <u>of value</u> = nothing <u>valuable</u> 没有什么有价值的东西
  ✎ a matter <u>of significance</u> = a <u>significant</u> matter 一件重要的事情
  也有些情况难以转换为形容词：
  ✎ a ship <u>of 46,000 tons</u> 一艘46,000吨级的船
  ✎ a man <u>of wide social relations</u> 一个社会关系很广的人
2. **在系动词后做表语（同样比用形容词更正式）。**
  ┏ …… proved to be <u>of great interest</u>. 被证明是非常有趣的
  ┗ …… proved to be <u>very interesting</u>.
  ✎ It is <u>of no use</u> =  it is <u>useless</u>.
  同样也有些情况难以转换为形容词：
  ✎ Her dress is <u>of dark crimson</u>. 她的裙子是深红色的。
  ✎ He is <u>of a peculiar disposition</u>. 他性格古怪。
  + 练习
    ┏ a man <u>of middle height</u>（后置定语）一个中等身高的男人
    ┗ The man is <u>of middle height</u>.（主系表结构）
    ┏ a girl <u>of remarkable imagination</u>（后置定语）一个想象力出众的女孩
    ┗ The girl is <u>of remarkable imagination</u>.（主系表结构）

+ **numerous/ countless** 数不胜数的，不计其数的（一定**修饰可数名词**）
  ✎ There are <u>countless</u> people who, ever since their early years, have learned to associate snails with food.（L23）
+ **from** prep. 考虑到，从……来<u>看/判断</u>
  ✎ <u>From</u> <u>her looks</u> I’d say she was Swedish. 从她的长相来看，我说她可能是瑞典人。
  ✎ <u>From</u> <u>what I heard</u> the company’s in deep trouble. 从我听到的情况来判断，这家公司深陷困境。
  ✎ <u>From</u> <u>this</u> the captain was able to piece together all the information that had come to light.（本文）
> 仿写第3段第5句
  从这些雕像的碎片来看，考古学家们明白了这座庙宇当初肯定是一个祭祀的场所。
  From the fragments of statues, the archaeologists realized that the temple must have been a place of worship.
+ **被写**
  ┏ …… which had been written on March 14th, 1943.（原文）
  ┗ …… which <u>was dated</u> March 14^th^,1943.
  **date** 标注日期于某处
  ✎ a newspaper <u>dated</u> October 1^st^,2005 日期为2005年10月1日的一份报纸
  其它被动表达：
  a girl <u>aged</u> 20 一个20岁的女孩
  a man <u>named</u> John 一个叫约翰的男人
  a novel <u>entitled</u> Three Kingdoms 一部叫《三国演义》的小说
  ┏ a movie <u>starring</u> Tom Hanks 一部由汤姆汉克斯主演的电影（主动）
  ┗ The movie <u>starred</u> Tom Hanks 这部电影由由汤姆汉克斯主演
  **主动、被动，得看单词搭配。**

#### 👾 **“名词+介词+关系代词”引导非限定性定语从句**
适用情况：定语从句修饰的不是先行词本身，而是先行词相关的东西或先行词的一部分。
✎ 他有两个儿子，其中的一个死于战火。
He has two sons, <u>one of whom</u> died in the war.（比并列句简洁）
✎ 演讲者提了(pose)四个问题，它们的答案被证明非常具有启发性(illuminating)。
The speaker posed four questions, <u>the answers to which</u> proved very illuminating.（同样比并列句简洁）

+ ┏ …… parts of which <u>it</u> was still possible <u>to read</u>.（原文-形式主语）
  ┗ …… <u>parts of which</u> were still possible <u>to read</u>.（同义表达）（形容词后加动词不定式，即便被动也要用主动，例如下组句子↓）
  ┏ Most of our fears are unreasonable, but <u>**they** are impossible **to erase**</u>.（L54）
  ┗ Most of our fears are unreasonable, but <u>**it** is impossible **to erase them**</u>.（换用形式主语表达）
  + 注：**possible和impossible主语不能是某个具体的人，动词不定式介词结尾除外**，举例如下↓。
    【✔】……, but <u>**it** was impossible **to stop the thieves**</u>.（L6）
    【✘】……, but <u>**the thieves** were impossible **to stop**</u>.
    【✔】**He** is impossible **to deal with**.
  + ┗ …… parts of which <u>could still be read</u>.（原文同义表达）
    ┗ …… parts of which <u>were still legible</u>.（原文同义表达-系表结构）
+ **piece <u>sth. 🗘 together</u>** 把……拼凑起来以发现事情的原貌/真相
  ✎ The police are still trying to <u>piece together the facts</u>. 警方仍在试图拼凑事实以发现案情的真相。
  ✎ The archaeologists <u>pieced the fragments together</u>. 考古学家把碎片拼凑在一起以发现雕像的原貌。
  **reconstruct** 拼凑起来发现原貌
  ✎ When the archaeologists <u>reconstructed</u> the fragments, they were amazed to find that the goddess turned out to be a very modern-looking woman.（L3）
+ **come to light = be brought to light** 被发现（习语）
  ┏ New evidence in this case has recently <u>come to light</u>.
  ┗ New evidence in this case has recently <u>been brought to light</u>.
  这起案件的新的证据，最近被发现了。
  + 跟视觉相关的搭配：
    **cast/ shed/ throw light on……** 揭示……(的真相)
    ✎ These discoveries may <u>cast some light on</u> the origins of the universe. 这些发现可能会揭示宇宙的起源。
    ✎ Even seemingly insignificant remains can <u>shed interesting light on</u> the history of early man.（L38）
+ **主句 (进行时 / be about to do) + when……** “**when**”应译为“**这时**”或“**突然**”。重点信息在从句而不在主句。（复习）
  ┏ I <u>was having</u> dinner **when** the phone rang.
  ┗ I <u>was about to leave</u> **when** the phone rang.
  ✎ He <u>was going</u> to the sweet shop **when** he dropped his fifty pence.（L15课后题-6）
  ✎ He <u>was</u> still <u>mumbling</u> something about hospitals at the end of the party **when** he slipped on a piece of ice and broke his left leg.（L29）
  ✎ The idea never appealed to me very much, but one day, after a heavy shower, I happened to <u>be walking</u> in my garden **when** I noticed a huge number of snails taking a stroll on some of my prize plants.（L23）
  ✎ The morning passed rapidly and Frank <u>was about to leave</u> **when** he noticed a large packing case lying on the floor.（L34）

---

## **Lesson 33 - A day to remember**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>We have all experienced days when everything goes wrong. A day may begin well enough, but suddenly everything seems to get out of control. What invariably happens is that a great number of things choose to go wrong at precisely the same moment. It is as if a single unimportant event set up a chain of reactions. Let us suppose that you are preparing a meal and keeping an eye on the baby at the same time. The telephone rings and this marks the prelude to an unforeseen series of catastrophes. While you are on the phone, the baby pulls the tablecloth off the table, smashing half your best crockery and cutting himself in the process. You hang up hurriedly and attend to baby, crockery, etc. Meanwhile, the meal gets burnt. As if this were not enough to reduce you to tears, your husband arrives, unexpectedly bringing three guests to dinner.

Things can go wrong on a big scale, as a number of people recently discovered in Parramatta, a suburb of Sydney. During the rush hour one evening two cars collided and both drivers began to argue. The woman immediately behind the two cars happened to be a learner. She suddenly got into a panic and stopped her car. This made the driver following her brake hard. His wife was sitting beside him holding a large cake. As she was thrown forward, the cake went right through the windscreen and landed on the road. Seeing a cake flying through the air, a lorry driver who was drawing up alongside the car, pulled up all of a sudden. The lorry was loaded with empty beer bottles and hundreds of them slid off the back of the vehicle and on to the road. This led to yet another angry argument. Meanwhile, the traffic piled up behind. It took the police nearly an hour to get the traffic on the move again. In the meantime, the lorry driver had to sweep up hundreds of broken bottles. Only two stray dogs benefited from all this confusion, for they greedily devoured what was left of the cake. It was just one of those days!</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **prelude** n. 序幕，前奏
  **pre- 提前**
  **lude = play 戏剧**
  **prelude (to sth.)** ……的序幕/前奏
  ✎ The high wind is the <u>prelude to</u> a heavy storm. 大风是一场暴风雨的前奏。（日常多作派生义使用）
  近义搭配：
  **prologue (to ……)** （书）的序言（**log：讲话**）
  **preface (to ……)** 同上
  **foreword (to ……)** 同上
  **epilogue (to ……)** （书）的后记/跋（**epi-：在外面，在后面**）
+ **unforeseen = unexpected** a. 意料之外的
  **unforeseenly = unexpectedly**
  **foresee = expect** v. 预见，预期，预料
  + 相近词：
    **foretell** v. 预言，预测；预兆，预示
    **predict** v. 预言，预测
    ✎ Timely snow <u>foretells</u> a bumper harvest. 及时的雪预示着大丰收。（瑞雪兆丰年）
    **forecast** n./v. 预告，预报（**词根cast 投掷，扔出去**）
    ✎ weather <u>forecast</u> 天气预报
+ **series** n. 系列（单复数同形）
  单复数同形的其它词：**species** 物种
  **a series of……** 一套，一系列，一连串
  ✎ <u>a series of</u> books 丛书，一套书
  ✎ <u>a series of</u> stamps 一套纪念邮票
  ✎ <u>A series of</u> rainy days spoiled my vacation. 一连串的阴雨天毁了我的假期。
  + 同义替换：
    **a chain of……**
    **a train of……**
    **a trail of……**（L1）
    **a string of……**（string 一串）
    **a stream of……**（stream 溪流）
+ **catastrophe** n. 大灾难
  近义词（程度由小到大）：
  **mishap** 小意外，小的事故
  **accident, contingency** 事故（后者更文言）
  **disaster** 大灾难（**dis- 不好的；aster：星** 直译：灾星）
  **calamity, catastrophe** 特大灾难
+ **crockery** n.[U] 陶器
  同义词：
  **pottery, earthenware**（都不可数）
  瓷器：
  **china, chinaware, porcelain**（都不可数，最后一个较书面）
+ **suburb** n. 郊区
  **suburban** a. 郊区的；目光短浅的，见识不广的
  相关词：
  **rural** 农村的
  **urban** 城市的
  **metropolitan** 大城市的，大都会的
  **cosmopolitan** 国际性大都市的
+ **panic** n. （突然的）惊慌
  **get into a panic** 陷入恐慌
  **in a panic** 恐慌地，惊慌失措地
  ✎ He fled <u>in a panic</u>. 他惊慌失措地逃跑了。（原形flee（L13））作名词
  ✎ Don’t <u>panic</u> in case of fire. 万一着火别惊慌。作动词
  + 动词变化：
    panic（原形）；panicked（一般过去式）；panicked（过去分词）；panicking（现在分词）（加k的目的是避免误读）
    相同变化的词：
    picnic（原形）；picnicked（一般过去式）；picnicked（过去分词）； picnicking（现在分词）
+ **stray** a. 迷路的，偏离(正确方向)的；v. 迷路，偏离(正确方向)
  ✎ a <u>stray</u> dog/ boy/ bullet 一条迷路的狗（野狗）/一个迷路的孩子/一颗偏离方向的子弹
  ✎ **stray sheep** 迷途的羔羊（出自圣经，上帝把人类比作羔羊）
  ✎ Some of the cattle have <u>strayed</u>. 有些牛迷路了/丢了。（cattle 本身为复数）
  ✎ Don’t <u>stray</u> from the point. 请不要偏离正题/跑题。
+ **confusion** n. 混乱；迷惑
  **confuse** v. 使混乱；使迷惑不解
  **confused** a. 混乱不堪的；迷惑不解的（来自过去分词）
  **confusing** a. 令人迷惑不解的（来自现在分词）
  + 近义词及其搭配：
    **disorder** 混乱；**in disorder** 处于混乱状态（L16）
    **mess**；**in a mess**（L11）
    **chaos**；**in (a state of) chaos**
    ✎ All the things I had packed so carefully were soon <u>in a dreadful mess</u>.（L11）
    ✎ Without it, nothing could ever be brought to a conclusion; everything would be <u>in a state of chaos</u>.（L60）
+ **greedily** ad. 贪婪地，贪吃地
  **greedy** a. 贪婪的，贪吃的
  近义词：**gluttonous** a. 贪吃的
  相关词：the seven deadly sins（七宗罪）:
  **greed** 贪婪，**gluttony** 贪吃，**lust** 好色，**envy** 嫉妒，**wrath** 愤怒，**sloth** 懒惰，**pride** 傲慢


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **…… to remember** 令人难忘的……（L22）
+ **go wrong** 出错，出问题，不顺利（L26）
  ✎ We have all experienced days when everything <u>goes wrong</u>.（本文）
  ✎ Our marriage began to <u>go wrong</u> after we had our first child. 我们的婚姻在我们生了第一个孩子后就开始出问题了。
  ✎ Something’s <u>gone wrong</u> with my computer. 我的电脑出故障了。（’s = has）
  ✎ An advertisement which begins with the magic word FREE can rarely <u>go wrong</u>.（L26）
  ✎ It is all too easy to blame the railway authorities when something does <u>go wrong</u>.（L37）
+ **We have all experienced days when……**
  ✎ <u>We have all experienced days when</u> life seems to be a bowl of cherries. 我们大家都经历过幸福如意的日子。（固定比喻）
  ✎ <u>We have all experienced moments</u> of misery and despair. 我们大家都经历过痛苦和绝望的时刻。
+ **suddenly = all of a sudden = all at once** 突然
  ✎ Seeing a cake flying through the air, a lorry driver who was drawing up alongside the car, pulled up <u>all of a sudden</u>.（本文）
  ✎ <u>All at once</u>, I noticed that my wife seemed to be filled with alarm.（L48）
+ **get out of <u>control/ hand</u>** 变得失控（习语）
  ✎ W: You know the noise in my dorm has really <u>gotten out of control</u>. My roommate and I can rarely get to sleep before midnight.
  M: Why don’t you take the problem up with the dorm supervisor?
  Q: What does the man suggest the woman do?
  Answer: Discuss the situation with the person in charge of the dormitory.（托福听力真题）
  ✎ We started burning some leaves in our yard, but the fire got <u>out of hand</u> and we had to call the fire department to put it out.
  (A)out of hand；(B)out of order（出故障，坏了）；(C)out of the question（不可能）；(D)out of the way（闪开路）（六级真题-选择）
  反义搭配：
  **get sth. under control** 控制住某物
  ✎ M: Look at all the pollution going into the air from those factories. Do you think they’ll ever <u>get that under control</u>?
  W: With the new laws and social awareness, we’ll turn things around.
  Q: What does the woman predict will happen?
  Answer: The situation will improve if changes are made.（听力真题）
+ **What invariably happens is that……** 往往总是……
  ✎ 往往总是干得最多的人收入最少。
  <u>What invariably happens is that</u> those who work most get paid least.
  ✎ 往往总是老师一走班里就陷入一片混乱状态。
  <u>What invariably happens is that</u> once teachers leave the class will be in a state of chaos.
+ **choose to do** ① 选择去做某事；② 决定去做某事（表示出乎意料的决定）
  ✎ More and more people are <u>choosing to</u> live alone. 越来越多的人选择独自生活。
  ✎ Catherine <u>chose to</u> ignore the doctor’s warning. 凯瑟琳决定不理睬医生的警告。
+ 句意延伸
  It never rains but it pours. 祸不单行。（直译：除了下瓢泼大雨之外从来不下雨。）（but 除了……情况之外）
  As the old saying goes, happiness comes alone while misfortune loves company. 正如老话说的，福无双至祸不单行。
  If anything can go wrong, it will. (Murphy’s law) 如果事情能变遭，它就几乎一定会变遭。（墨菲定律）
+ **set up** 导致
  ✎ The heavy fog <u>set up</u> a traffic jam. 浓雾导致了交通堵塞。
  + 表示**导致**的词：
    **cause, effect**
    **lead to, result in**
    **bring about, give rise to**（L4）
    **produce, create**
    **trigger, spark** 触发（这两个与原文替换更贴切）
    ✎ Even the smallest diplomatic incident can <u>trigger/ spark</u> a major international conflict. 甚至最小的外交事件也可能触发重大的国际冲突。
+ **a chain of** 一连串的（同义替换见本文单词讲解）
  相关表达：
  ┏ 连锁反应
  ┗ a **chain reaction**
  ┗ a **domino effect** （domino 多米诺）
  ┗ a **ripple effect** （ripple 涟漪）
+ **keep an eye on <u>sth./ sb.</u>** 照料/照看……
  ✎ Would you please <u>keep an eye on</u> my suitcase while I’m away? 我不在的时候，你能帮我照看一下我的行李箱吗？
  同义替换：
  **look after, take care of, watch**
  相关词：
  **babysit** v. 照料小孩（通常付费）
  **babysitter** n. 代人临时照看小孩的人
  ✎ He used to <u>babysit for</u> Mary when she worked nights. 当玛丽上夜班时，他过去曾经帮她照看孩子。（work nights 上夜班）
+ **ring** 铃声响起（及物不及物都行）
  ✎ The doorbell <u>rang</u>. 门铃响了。
  ✎ <u>ring</u> the doorbell 摁响门铃。
  其它表达**响**的词：
  **go off** 大的，刺耳的声音，如：闹钟声、枪声、爆炸声
  ✎ The alarm clock <u>went off</u>. 闹钟响了。
  **strike** 钟打点、报时
  ✎ The clock is <u>striking</u> the hours.（L2）
  ✎ The clock began to <u>strike</u> twelve.
+ **mark** 标志
  ✎ It <u>marked</u> the end of the great tradition of ships with sails and the beginning of a new era.（L25）
  ✎ The foundation of the People’s Republic of China <u>marked</u> the beginning of a new historical period in China. 中华人民共和国的成立标志着在中国新的历史阶段的开始。
+ **mark the prelude to……** 预示着……，标志着……的序幕/前奏
  ✎ The dark clouds <u>marked the prelude to</u> a heavy storm. 乌云预示着有一场暴风雨。
  ✎ The Lugouqiao Incident <u>marked the prelude to</u> China’s War of Resistance Against Japanese Aggression. 卢沟桥事变预示着中国抗日战争的开始。
+ **be on the phone** 正在通话，打电话
  **answer the phone** 接电话
  ✎ While you are <u>answering the phone</u>, ……（原文换用）
  **answer the door** 应门
  **I’ll get it.** 我去接电话/开门。（口语）
+ 电话中常用的口语
  ◇ May I speak to Mr. John Smith? 请叫史密斯先生讲话。
  ◇ This is John Smith speaking. 我就是史密斯先生。
  = This is he. 我就是。
  = Speaking. 我就是。
  ◇ Who is it? 您是哪位？
  = Who is there?
  = Who is calling?
  （注：Who are you? 只能当面说）
  ◇ One moment, please. 请稍等。
  = <u>Hold on/ Hang on</u>, please.
  ◇ John, there’s a phone call for you. 约翰，有你的电话。
  = John, you are wanted on the phone.
  = John, Tom’s on the line. Pick up the phone on your desk.
  ◇ Sorry, Mr. Smith is in a meeting right now. <u>Would you like to leave a message/ May I take a message</u>?
  ◇ Can you connect me with John Smith in the advertising department? 你能帮我接通广告部的约翰·史密斯吗？
  ◇ I’d like to <u>place/ make</u> a collect call to Australia. 我想打一个到澳大利亚的对方付费电话。（collect call 对方付费电话）
  ◇ The connection is very bad. I can barely hear you. 连接非常糟糕。我几乎听不见你说话。
  ◇ There’s something wrong with the phone. Let’s hang up. I’ll call you right back. 电话出了点问题。我们挂断电话吧。我马上给你回过去。
+ 结果状语
  分词作结果状语，往往表示正常结果；
  动词不定式 to do 也可作结果状语，一般表示意料之外且不大好的结果，尤其是连续发生的动作。常用副词only加强语气。（L30）
  ✎ He studied very hard <u>(only) to fail the exam</u>.
  ✎ The firefighters raced up the building, <u>(only) to be the first victims</u>. 消防员冲上了大楼，结果却成了第一批受害者。
  ✎ Farm labourers said that they always woke up <u>to find</u> that work had been done overnight.（L30）
+ **in the process = at the same time** 与此同时，在此过程中
  ✎ I stood up to say hello and spilt my drink <u>in the process</u>. 我站起来打招呼，结果把饮料洒了。
+ **hang up** 挂断电话
  同义表达：
  **put the phone down**
  **slam the phone down** 气愤地挂断电话
  **get cut off** 线路中断
  ✎ M: Did you <u>get cut off</u>?
  W: No, they asked me to <u>hang up</u> and try again later.
  Q: What has the woman been doing?
  Answer: Talking on the telephone.（托福听力真题）
+ **hurriedly** 匆忙地
  **= in a <u>hurry/ rush</u>**
  **= in haste**（较文言）
  There’s no <u>hurry/ rush</u>. 不着急/慢慢来。
  What’s the <u>hurry/ rush</u>? 着什么急呀？
  Take your time. 慢慢来。
+ **attend to……** 应付，处理，解决（表示应付比较难处理的问题）（L7）
  **= deal with……**
+ **etc.** 等等（拉丁文，全写：et cetera）（末尾的点，可写可不写）
  近义表达：
  **and so on, and so forth**（常用）
  **and the like, and what not**（口语）
+ **meanwhile** 与此同时（4种表达本文皆有换用）
  **= at the same time**
  **= in the process**
  **= (in the) meantime**
+ as if 引导虚拟语气
  ✎ <u>As if</u> this <u>were</u> not enough to reduce you to tears, your husband arrives, unexpectedly bringing three guests to dinner.（本文）
  ✎ It is <u>as if</u> a single unimportant event <u>set</u> up a chain of reactions.（本文）
  ✎ ‘Oh, that,’ he said with a smile <u>as if</u> he <u>were</u> talking about an old friend.（L24）
  ✎ Don’t act <u>as if</u> you <u>were</u> the only pebble on the beach. 不要自视太高。（习语）
+ **reduce sb. to sth.** 使某人陷入某个状态（通常是不好的状态）
  **reduce sb. to** tears 使某人伤心落泪
  **reduce sb. to** despair 使某人陷入绝望
  **reduce sb. to** silence 使某人陷入沉默
+ **scale** 规模（通常与介词on搭配）
  **on a <u>small</u> scale** 小规模的
  **on a <u>limited</u> scale** 有限规模的
  **on a <u>big/ large/ great/ grand/ vast</u> scale** 大规模的
  **on a <u>colossal/ huge/ enormous/ immense/ gigantic</u> scale** 特大规模的（L10）
  **on a <u>national/ nationwide</u> scale** 全国规模的
  **on a <u>global/ international/ worldwide</u> scale** 世界规模的

#### 👾 **as 引导的非限定性定语从句与 which 引导的非限定性定语从句的区别**
1. **as 作为关系代词指代整个主句，而 which 作为关系代词指代整个主句或先行词均可；**
2. **as 引导的非限定性定语从句位于主句前、中、后均可，而 which 引导的非限定性定语从句不能位于主句之前；**
as 引导的非限定性定语从句几乎是唯一一个可以放在主句前面的定语从句。
✎ <u>As a poet points out</u>, life is but a dream. 正如一位诗人指出的，人生不过是一场梦。（前）
✎ Children, <u>as/ which is always the case</u>, love their mother. 孩子们总是会爱自己的母亲。（中）
✎ She became angry, <u>as/ which many could see</u>. 她生气了，正如许多人所看到的。（后）
3. **as 引导的非限定性定语从句含有“众所周知”的意思，常译为“正如……”，而 which 引导的非限定性定语从句则未必有这个意思；**
✎ The sun heats the earth, <u>which makes it possible for plants to grow</u>. 太阳加热地球，使植物生长成为可能。
4. **在“as + is/was + done”结构中可省略“is/was”，而在“which + is/was + done”结构中，则要省略“which + is/was”，而不能只省略be动词。**
✎ <u>As (is) reported</u>, a foreign delegation will visit the city. 正如被报道的那样，一个外国代表团将访问该市。
✎ a puma <u>(which was) at large</u>（L1）
【✘】As Napoleon once pointed <u>it</u> out, attack is the best method of defense.（在英式语法中不算错）
【✔】As Napoleon once pointed out, attack is the best method of defense.
正如拿破仑曾经指出的那样，进攻是最好的防守的方法。（托福语法改错）

+ **rush hour** 交通高峰时段（是泛指，通常作不可数名词，即便作可数名词，也用作单数）
  ✎ the <u>morning/ evening</u> <u>rush hour</u> 早上/晚上的交通高峰时间段
  ✎ Don’t travel at <u>rush hour</u>. 不要在交通高峰时段出门。
  When the traffic was very heavy, ……（原文同义表达）
+ **immediately <u>behind/ above/ below/ in front of</u> sth.**（immediately 表示位置离得近，而非时间）
+ **happen to do** 碰巧（L3）
  ┏ …… <u>happened to be</u> a learner.（原文）
  ┗ …… <u>chanced to be</u> learner.（原文同义表达，下同）
  ┗ <u>It happened/ chanced that</u> the woman immediately behind the two cars <u>was</u> a learner.（从句）
  ┗ <u>As it happened/ As luck would have it</u>, the woman immediately behind the two cars <u>was</u> a learner.（习语）
+ ┏ She <u>suddenly got into a panic</u> and stopped her car.（原文）
  ┗ She <u>got into a sudden panic</u> and stopped her car.（原文同义表达，下同）
  ┗ She stopped her car <u>in a sudden panic</u>.
+ **brake <u>hard/ sharply</u>** 急刹车
  **= slam on the brakes**
  + 表示停车：
    **stop, draw up, pull up**
    ✎ Seeing a cake flying through the air, a lorry driver who was <u>drawing up</u> alongside the car, <u>pulled up</u> all of a sudden.（本文）
    **come to a <u>stop/ halt</u>**（L6）
    ✎ It <u>came to a stop</u> outside the jeweler’s.（L6）
    ✎ Bruce charged at it, but in the middle, the car <u>came to a grinding halt</u>.（L39）
+ **right** 刚好
+ **draw up** 车停下来
  ✎ A taxi <u>drew up</u> at the gate. 一辆出租车停在了门口。
  **draw <u>sth. 🗘 up</u>** 起草……（L21）
  ✎ ……, when the Marquis of Queensberry <u>drew up the first set of rules</u>.（L21）
+ **alongside** ad.&prep. 沿着……的边；与……并排
  ✎ A car drew up <u>alongside</u>. 一辆汽车靠边停了下来。（ad. 靠边）
  ✎ A police car pulled up <u>alongside</u> us. 一辆警车停在了我们的旁边。（prep. 并排）
+ **be loaded with……** 满载着……（复习）
+ ┏ …… <u>slid off</u> the back …… 意外地滑落/滑倒（原文）
  ┗ …… <u>slipped off</u> the back …… （同义替换）（L29）
+ **vehicle** 可指路上行驶的各种车辆
+ 上义词替换
  ✎ The <u>lorry</u> was loaded with empty beer bottles and hundreds of them slid off the back of the <u>vehicle</u> and on to the road.（本文）
  ✎ <u>Giant pandas</u> are considered a national treasure and the Chinese government are doing their best to protect this <u>endangered species</u>. 大熊猫被视为国宝，中国政府正在竭尽全力保护这一濒危物种。
  ✎ Moreover, in the past two years other nearby cities may have begun to build similar <u>golf courses</u> or <u>resort hotels</u>. Indeed, the fact that Ocean View has already built <u>these facilities</u> might actually portend failure for Hopewell, ……
  此外，在过去两年中，其他附近的城市可能已经开始建造类似的高尔夫球场或度假酒店。其实，Ocean View已经建造了这些设施，这实际上可能预示着霍普韦尔的失败……（GRE写作范文节选）
+ **<u>yet/ still</u> (<u>another/ one more</u>……)** 又一次，再一次（L5）
  ✎ <u>yet one more</u> question 再提一个问题
  ✎ <u>still another</u> example 再举个例子
  ✎ He sent <u>yet another</u> fax informing the journalist that if he did not reply soon he would be fired.（L5）
+ **traffic** 指路上行驶的全部车子，不能用复数
+ **pile up** 堆积，积聚（L1）
  ✎ The work just keeps on <u>piling up</u> and makes me want to scream. 工作不断堆积，让我想尖叫。
+ ┏ It took the police nearly an hour to get the traffic on the move again.（原文-物作take的主语）
  ┗ The police <u>took</u> nearly an hour <u>to get</u> the traffic on the move again.（人作take的主语）
  ┗ The police <u>spent</u> nearly an hour <u>(in) getting</u> the traffic on the move again.（spend的主语只能是人）
+ **on the + n.** 处于某种状态
  ◇ **on the move** 在前进（本文）
  ◇ The dog is **on the alert**. 处于警觉状态
  ◇ He is always **on the go**. 忙忙碌碌
  ◇ The patient is **on the recovery**. 正在康复中
  ◇ Crimes are **on the rise**. 正在上升中
  ◇ While you are **on the phone**,…… 正在打电话（本文）
  + 其它形式（不加the）：
    ◇ Even people who take no interest in art cannot have failed to notice examples of modern sculpture **on display** in public places. 处于陈列状态（L18）
    ◇ The house is **on sale**. 在售中；甩卖中(美)
    ◇ The workers are **on strike**. 在罢工
    ◇ I’m here **on vacation**. 在度假
    ◇ I’m here **on business**. 在公务中，公务在身
    ◇ The nurse is **on call** 24 hours a day. 听候召唤
+ ┏ **benefit from……** 得益于……
  ┗ **benefit……** 有益于……
  ┏ This food will <u>benefit</u> your brain. 这种食物对你的大脑有益。
  ┗ Your brain will <u>benefit from</u> this food. 你的大脑会从这种食物中受益。
+ **what is left of sth.** 某物剩下/残留的部分（leave 及物 → 被动）（L3）
  **= what remains of sth.**（remain 不及物 → 主动）
  ✎ ……, for they greedily devoured <u>what remained</u> of the cake.（原文换用）
  ✎ It is recounted of Thomas Carlyle that when he heard of the illness of his friend, Henry Taylor, he went off immediately to visit him,carrying with him in his pocket <u>what remained of a bottle of medicine</u> formerly prescribed for an indisposition of Mrs. Carlyle’s.（B4L28）

---

## **Lesson 34 - A happy discovery**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>Antique shops exert a peculiar fascination on a great many people. The more expensive kind of antique shop where rare objects are beautifully displayed in glass cases to keep them free from dust is usually a forbidding place. But no one has to muster up courage to enter a less pretentious antique shop. There is always hope that in its labyrinth of musty, dark, disordered rooms a real rarity will be found amongst the piles of assorted junk that litter the floors.

No one discovers a rarity by chance. A truly dedicated bargain hunter must have patience, and above all, the ability to recognize the worth of something when he sees it. To do this, he must be at least as knowledgeable as the dealer. Like a scientist bent on making a discovery, he must cherish the hope that one day he will be amply rewarded.

My old friend, Frank Halliday, is just such a person. He has often described to me how he picked up a masterpiece for a mere £50. One Saturday morning, Frank visited an antique shop in my neighbourhood. As he had never been there before, he found a great deal to interest him. The morning passed rapidly and Frank was about to leave when he noticed a large packing case lying on the floor. The dealer told him that it had just come in, but that he could not be bothered to open it. Frank begged him to do so and the dealer reluctantly prised it open. The contents were disappointing. Apart from an interesting-looking carved dagger, the box was full of crockery, much of it broken. Frank gently lifted the crockery out of the box and suddenly noticed a miniature painting at the bottom of the packing case. As its composition and line reminded him of an Italian painting he knew well, he decided to buy it. Glancing at it briefly, the dealer told him that it was worth £50. Frank could hardly conceal his excitement, for he knew that he had made a real discovery. The tiny painting proved to be an unknown masterpiece by Correggio and was worth hundreds of thousands of pounds.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **forbidding** a. 令人望而生畏的；冷冰冰的
  ✎ a <u>forbidding</u> place 一个令人望而生畏的地方
  ✎ a <u>forbidding</u> appearance 一个令人望而生畏的/冷冰冰的表情
  + 近义词：
    **unfriendly, unwelcoming**
    **inhospitable** 不热情好客的（**hospitable** 热情好客的）
    ┏ The Chinese are very <u>hospitable</u>. 中国人是非常热情好客的。
    ┗ The Chinese are noted for their <u>hospitality</u>. 中国人因好客而著称。（换用名词形式）
  + 同根词：
    **forbidden** a. 被禁止的
    ✎ the <u>Forbidden</u> City 紫禁城
    ✎ the <u>forbidden</u> fruit 禁果
+ **muster** v. 鼓起，激起，振作起
  **muster (up) sth. = summon (up) sth.**
  <u>muster/ summon (up)</u> courage 鼓起勇气
  <u>muster/ summon (up)</u> enthusiasm 激起热情
  <u>muster/ summon (up)</u> strength 振作起力量
+ **junk** n.[U] 废品，破烂货（相近意思的词基本都是不可数）
  ✎ a piece of <u>junk</u> 一件废品
  ✎ The cupboard is full of <u>junk</u>. 壁橱里装满了破烂货。
  ✎ <u>junk</u> food/ mail 垃圾食品/邮件
  + 同义词：
    **clutter** [U]
    ✎ Those who never have to move house become indiscriminate collectors of what can only be described as <u>clutter</u>.（L59）
  + 垃圾：
    **rubbish, trash, refuse**（都不可数）
    **garbage, litter**（都不可数）
  + **litter, clutter** v. 胡乱地堆满某个地方
    ✎ Magazines <u>littered/ cluttered</u> the floor. 一些杂志胡乱地堆在了地板上。
    **be littered/ cluttered with……** 某地胡乱堆满了某物
    ✎ The garden <u>was</u> soon <u>littered with</u> chunks of metal which had once made up a lawn mower.（L46）
+ **dealer** n. 商人（暗示专门出售某种品类的东西且大多具备相关专业知识，如古董商、家具商等）
  ✎ an antique <u>dealer</u> 古董商（本文）
  ✎ a furniture <u>dealer</u> 家具商
  相关词：
  **businessman/ merchant** 大商人（大量出售某种产品）（后者更正式）
  **vendor** 街头小商贩
  **retailer** 零售商；**wholesaler** 批发商
  （**retail** 零售；**wholesale** 批发）
  **supplier** 供应商
  **sales representative** 销售代表
  **assistant/ clerk** 售货员
  **real estate agent** 房地产经纪人
  **grocer** 杂货商
  **stationer** 文具商
+ **cherish** v. 珍爱，珍视；长期怀有某种感情
  + 珍爱，珍视
    ✎ I’ll <u>cherish</u> our friendship for ever.
    同义词：**treasure, value**（L16）（可与上例替换）
    + a.
      ┏ Mary’s <u>cherished</u> possessions 玛丽的心爱的财产
      ┗ Mary’s <u>prize</u> possessions
      **treasured, valued** a. 受珍视的，心爱的
  + 长期怀有某种感情
    ✎ He <u>cherished the hope</u> of winning an Olympic medal. 他一直以来都希望赢得一枚奥运奖牌。（比用have漂亮）
    ✎ He <u>cherished the memory</u> of his late wife. 他一直以来都非常怀念已故的妻子。（late放在亲属前，是“已故”的委婉表达）
    ✎ He <u>cherished the illusion</u> that the girl was in love with him. 他一直以来都怀有那个女孩爱上自己的错觉。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **happy**: lucky; fortunate 幸运的
  ✎ a <u>happy</u> coincidence 一个幸运的巧合
  ✎ the <u>happy</u> few 幸运的少数（固定习语）（B4L33）
  **sad** 不幸的
  ✎ The <u>sad</u> truth is that most of us have been brought up to eat certain foods and we stick to them all our lives.（L23）
  ✎ He made a <u>sad</u> mistake. 他犯了一个不幸的错误。
+ **exert** 施加某种力量（L26）
  **exert…… on……**
  ✎ Much as we may pride ourselves on our good taste, we are no longer free to choose the things we want, for advertising <u>exerts</u> a subtle influence <u>on</u> us.（L26）
+ **fascination** n. 魅力，魔力，吸引力（L9）
  ✎ Cats never fail to <u>fascinate</u> human beings.（L9）
  同义词：
  **charm, attraction, appeal**（L29）
  ✎ In spite of national differences, certain funny situations have a universal <u>appeal</u>.（L29）
  + **sth. exert a peculiar fascination on sb.** 某人非常喜欢某物/某物对某人施加了一种独特的魅力
    **exert A on B** 把A施加在B的身上
> 仿写第1句
  很多中国年轻人非常喜欢韩国的(Korean)电视剧(TV dramas)。
  Korean TV dramas <u>exert a peculiar fascination on</u> a great many Chinese young people.
+ **expensive** 高档的；豪华的（L6）
  ✎ The <u>expensive</u> shops in a famous arcade near Piccadilly were just opening. （不是商店贵，而是商店里卖的东西贵）（L6）
+ the more expensive **kind of** antique shop 种类
  ┏ **表示种类的词(kind, sort, type等) + of + 中心名词**（最正式的表达，可数名词作不可数来用；用复数也不算错，但不够正式）
  ┗ **中心名词 + of + 表示种类的词(kind, sort, type等)**（可数名词用复数）
  ┏ a new kind of <u>machine</u>
  ┗ <u>machines</u> of a new kind
+ **(be) free from……** 没有……（某个不想要的东西）（L27）
  ✎ He may never be sure where the next meal is coming from, but he <u>is free from</u> the thousands of anxieties which afflict other people.（L27）
  ✎ The composition <u>is free from</u> errors. 这篇作文没有错误。
  ✎ Organic produce <u>is free from</u> harmful chemicals. 有机农作物不含有害化学物质。
  **free…… from……** 使……没有……（某个不想要的东西）
  ✎ He dedicated his life to <u>freeing</u> the world <u>from</u> famine and disease. 他毕生致力于使世界摆脱饥荒和疾病。/他把一生的时间精力都献给了使世界没有饥荒和疾病。
+ **pretentious** a. 自命不凡的；装腔作势的
> 仿写第3句
  谁也不用壮着胆子去接近一个不那么装腔作势的女孩子。
  No one has to <u>muster up courage</u> to approach a less <u>pretentious</u> girl.

#### 👾 **there be + 无灵主语**
（以下多用于书面语）
+ **there is no denying that……** 不可否认的是……，谁也不能否认……
+ **there is no doubt that……** 毫无疑问/毋庸置疑的是……
+ ┏ **there is every likelihood that……** 很可能……
+ ┗ **there is little likelihood that……** 不太可能……
+ **there is no shortage of……** 有的是……
  ✎ Of course, New York is the ideal place for such an interesting study, because <u>there is no shortage of</u> tall buildings.（L9）
+ ┏ **there is an element of truth in……** ……有点道理
  ✎ Perhaps <u>there is an element of truth in</u> both these pictures, but few us have had the opportunity to find out.（L12）
+ ┗ **there is a good deal of truth in……** ……很有道理
  ✎ Apparently, <u>there is a good deal of truth in</u> this idea.（L9）
+ **hope** 希望/可能性（既可作可数，也可作不可数）
  ◇ **There is little hope of** any improvement in his condition. 他的状况几乎没有改善的希望/可能。（不可数）
  ◇ **There’s still a faint hope that** the two sides will reach an agreement. 双方仍有一线希望/可能达成协议。
  ◇ It was rush hour, and **there was no hope of** getting a seat. 当时是交通高峰期，根本不可能找到座位。
  ◇ **Is there any hope of** getting financial support for the project? 这个项目有希望/可能获得资金支持吗？
  ◇ **Is there any hope that** she will change her mind? 她有可能/希望改变主意吗？

+ **喻体 + of + 本体** 英语中的比喻方式之一
  ✎ <u>a boy **of** a girl</u> 男孩般的女孩
  ✎ <u>an angel **of** a wife</u> 天使般的妻子
  ✎ <u>a palace **of** a house</u> 宫殿般的房子
  ✎ <u>a garden **of** Switzerland</u> 花园般的瑞士
  ✎ Jane is <u>a submissive lamb **of** a girl</u>. 简是个像温顺小羊羔的小女孩。
+ **rarity** n. 稀罕，珍稀（不可数）；稀罕的东西，珍稀的东西（可数）
+ **amongst**: among（L17）
  **whilst**: while
  **midst**: middle
+ **assorted** 各式各样的；各种类型混杂在一块的；什锦的
  ✎ <u>assorted</u> vegetables 各式各样的蔬菜
  ✎ a box of <u>assorted</u> chocolates 一盒什锦巧克力
  ✎ tools in <u>assorted</u> sizes 各种尺寸的工具
  ✎ swimsuits in <u>assorted</u> colors 各种颜色的泳衣
+ **by chance** 偶然地，随随便便地，凭运气地，意外地（L27）
  **= by accident, accidentally**
  反义词（故意地，成心地，有目的地，有预谋地）：
  **intentionally, deliberately, on purpose**（**intention** n. 目的，意图）
  ✎ No one succeeds <u>by chance</u>. 没有人能随随便便成功。
+ **above all (else)** 最重要的是
  ✎ Max is clever, hardworking, and <u>above all (else)</u> honest. 马克斯聪明、勤奋，最重要的是诚实。
> 仿写第2段第2句
  一个真正全身心投入的猎头必须要有耐心，并且最重要的是，要有识才的慧眼。
  A truly dedicated head-hunter must have patience, and above all, an eye for talents.
  **an eye for……** ……的眼力；……的鉴赏力
  ✎ He <u>has an eye for</u> beauty. 他对美比较有鉴赏力。他有审美眼光。
+ **knowledgeable** 知识渊博的，~~可以知识的~~
+ **as^1^** knowledgeable **as^2^** the dealer.（1：副词，修饰knowledgeable； 2：连词，表示“像”。另：as……as……固定句型，谓语动词省略了）
  as 单独使用，翻译为“像”，一定是连词，谓语动词不可省略。同翻译为“像”，like是介词。
  ┏ When at Rome, do <u>as</u> the Romans do. 入乡随俗。（谚语原文）
  ┗ When at Rome, do <u>like</u> the Romans.（同义表达）
  + as 如果作介词，加名词，译为：是……；作为……身份
    ✎ …… Alfred Bloggs who worked <u>as</u> a dustman for the Ellesmere Corporation.（L4）
    ┏ She spoke <u>as</u> a lawyer. 她以律师的身份发言。（介词）
    ┗ She spoke <u>like</u> a lawyer. 她说话像个律师。
  + ┏ He must be <u>as</u> knowledgeable <u>as</u> the dealer <u>(is)</u>.（原文）
    ┗ He isn’t <u>as/ so</u> knowledgeable <u>as</u> the dealer <u>(is)</u>.（否定）
+ **be bent on <u>sth./ doing sth.</u>** 一门心思/打定主意做某事
  ✎ The boy <u>is bent on</u> mischief. 这男孩一门心思捣鬼/捣乱。
  ✎ He <u>is bent on</u> winning at all costs. 他打定主意不惜一切代价取胜。
  同义搭配：
  **be determined to do**
  **be resolved to do**
  **set one’s mind on <u>sth./ doing sth.</u>**
  ✎ Like a scientist + ①/②/③（原文换用）
  ① <u>determined to make a discovery</u>.
  ② <u>resolved to make a discovery</u>.
  ③ <u>setting his mind on making a discovery</u>.
+ **有**（L3）
  ◇ **nourish** 滋养；有某种感情
  ✎ Lisa has long <u>nourished</u> the hope of becoming a ballerina. 丽莎长期以来都希望成为芭蕾舞演员。
  ◇ **enjoy** 享有（L3）
  ✎ The city at one time must have been prosperous, for it <u>enjoyed</u> a high level of civilization.（L3）
  ◇ **boast** 有某个好的东西（及物动词，只能事物作主语）
  ┏ There is a lot of beautiful scenery in China.
  ┗ China <u>boasts</u> a lot of beautiful scenery. 中国有很多美丽的风光。
  ◇ **be blessed with**
  ┏ They have three lovely children.
  ┗ They <u>are blessed with</u> three lovely children.
  ◇ **be endowed with**（强调先天就具备）
  ┏ The girl has both beauty and brains. 她才貌双全。
  ┗ The girl <u>is endowed with</u> both beauty and brains.
+ **be rewarded** 获得回报/报答
  **be amply rewarded** 获得丰厚的回报/报答
  ✎ There is always hope that all my patience will <u>be amply rewarded</u>. 总是会有这样一种可能性：所有我的耐心终将获得丰厚的回报。
+ **describe sth. to sb.** 把某事描述给某人（如果“某事”太长可以先说“to sb.”）
  ✎ Let me <u>describe **to you** how it happened</u>. 让我向你描述一下事情是如何发生的。
  + 相同变化举例：
    ◇ Wherever it went, it <u>left **behind it** a trail of dead deer and small animals like rabbits</u>.（L1）
    ◇ On the occasions when they have <u>pushed **to shore** an unconscious human being</u>……（B4L18）
  + **describe…… as……** 把（前者）描述成为是（后者）
    ✎ He <u>described</u> it <u>as</u> ‘a very agreeable situation located within two small hills in the midst of which flowed a great river.’（L17）
    ✎ Those who never have to move house become indiscriminate collectors of what can only <u>be described as</u> clutter.（L59）
+ **pick <u>sth. 🗘 up</u>** 幸运地买到便宜货
  ✎ We managed to <u>pick up</u> a few bargains at the auction. 我们在这次拍卖中设法搞到了一些便宜货。
+ **a mere……** 仅仅……（直接加名词）
  ✎ He’s <u>a mere</u> child. 他只是个孩子。
  ✎ It took her <u>a mere</u> 20 minutes to win. 她的取胜仅仅花了20分钟。
  ✎ Glancing at his map, he informed us that the next village was <u>a mere</u> twenty miles away.（L39）
+ **在……附近**（L6）
  a famous arcade + (以下5行) 在皮卡迪利大姐的附近
  ↳ **near** Piccadilly
  ↳ **close to** Piccadilly
  ↳ **around** Piccadilly
  ↳ **off** Piccadilly
  ↳ **in the <u>neighborhood/ vicinity</u> of** Piccadilly
  + **距离近**的表达
    **only a short bus ride away** 坐公交车就能到（bus ride 公交车的车程）
    ✎ The latest exhibitions, films, or plays <u>are only a short bus ride away</u>.（L41）
    **within walking distance** 走着就能到
    **within driving distance** 开车能到
    **within commuting distance** 乘车往返可以到（commute 乘车往返，通勤）
    **only a stone’s throw away** 仅仅一箭之遥
+ ┏ As he had never been there before, he found a great deal to interest him.（原文）
  ┗ Having never been there before,……（状语从句主语和主句主语一致，状语从句可用非谓语动词表达）
  ┗ As this was his first visit there,……（同义表达-原因状语从句）
  ┗ This (being) his first visit there,……（同义表达-独立主格）
  ✎ <u>This being his first visit</u> there, he found a great deal to interest him.（课后题-7）
+ The dealer told him <u>**that** it had just come in</u>, but <u>**that** he could not be bothered to open it</u>.
  第2个连词that不能去掉：如果去掉，无法分辨其是主句还是从句。
  ✎ Galileo’s observations show <u>**(that)** Copernicus, another great astronomer, was right</u> and <u>**that** the earth moves around the sun, not the other way around</u>.
  伽利略的观测表明，另一位伟大的天文学家哥白尼是对的，地球绕着太阳转，而不是相反。（**the other way around** 正相反）
  ✎ He agreed <u>**that** a train did come into the station at the time on the paper</u> and <u>**that** it did stop,but only to take on mail,not passengers</u>.（L60）
+ **can’t be bothered (to do sth)** 嫌麻烦（而不愿……）（固定搭配）
  ✎ The grass needs cutting but I <u>can’t be bothered to</u> do it today. 草需要修剪，但我嫌麻烦今天不想做。
  ✎ He could produce excellent work but usually he <u>can’t be bothered</u>. 他可以做出出色的作品，但通常他嫌麻烦。
+ **reluctantly** 不情愿地，勉强地（L5）
  ✎ When the journalist again failed to reply, the editor <u>reluctantly</u> published the article as it had originally been written.（L5）
  同义替换：
  **unwillingly, with reluctance**
+ **<u>prise[英]/ pry[美]</u> sth. open** 撬开某物
+ **apart from……[英] = aside from……[美]**
  + **除了……之外**；
    同义替换：
    **<u>except/ except for</u>……**
    **<u>but/ but for</u>……**
    **excluding……**
    **other than……**
    **with the exception of……**
    ✎ <u>Apart/ Aside from</u> the ending, it’s a really good film. 除了结局，这是一部非常好的电影。（相当于but for或except for。but和except不能放在句首，且不适用于：排除的东西是整体的一部分）
    ✎ I hardly know anyone in town <u>apart/ aside from</u> William and you. 除了威廉和你，我在城里几乎不认识任何人。
  + **除了……之外还有**
    同义替换：
    **besides**
    **as well as……**
    **in addition to……**
    ✎ <u>Apart/ Aside from</u> the injuries to his face and hands, he broke both legs. 除了脸部和双手受伤外，他的双腿也破了。
    ✎ <u>Apart/ Aside from</u> these two books, he has written some plays and film scripts. 除了这两本书，他还写了一些戏剧和电影脚本。
+ ┏ …… the box was full of crockery, <u>much of it broken</u>.（原文-独立主格结构，简洁，主次分明）
  ┗ …… the box was full of crockery, <u>and much of it was broken</u>.（加连词，形成并列句：啰嗦，主次不分）
  ┗ …… the box was full of crockery, <u>much of which was broken</u>.（定语从句：依然啰嗦）

> 仿写第3段第9句
  这个箱子(chest)里除了一些金条(gold bullion)之外，装满了宝石(precious stone)，其中大多数都是钻石。
  Apart from some gold bullion, the chest was full of precious stones,most of them diamonds.

+ **miniature** 微型的
  类似于下文的 **tiny**
+ **remind sb. of sth.** 使某人回忆起某事
  ✎ That song always <u>reminds</u> me <u>of</u> our first date. 那首歌总是使我回忆起我们的第一次约会。
  **remind sb. about sth.** 提醒某人某事
  **remind sb. to do sth.** 提醒某人去做某事
  ✎ Can you <u>remind</u> us <u>about</u> your plans for the building? 你能提醒我们一下你对这栋楼的计划吗？/关于你的建筑方案你能再跟我们说一下吗？
  ✎ <u>Remind</u> me <u>to</u> buy some milk tonight. 提醒我今晚买些牛奶。
+ ┏ <u>As its composition and line reminded him of an Italian painting he knew well</u>, he decided to buy it.（原文-原因状语从句）
  ┗ <u>Its composition and line reminding him of an Italian painting he knew well</u>, he decided to buy it.（换用独立主格）
+ **glance at** 匆匆地扫视一眼
  ✎ <u>Glancing at his map</u>, he informed us that the next village was a mere twenty miles away.（作伴随状语）（L39）
+ **conceal** 掩饰，隐藏，藏起来（及物动词）
  **reveal** 揭示，揭露
  ✎ I had no intention of buying one, but I <u>could not conceal the fact</u> that I was impressed by the size of the diamonds.（L28）
  ┏ Frank could hardly <u>conceal his excitement</u>,…… 几乎无法掩饰他的兴奋（原文）
  ┗ Frank almost <u>revealed his excitement</u>,…… 几乎暴露了他的兴奋（同义改写）
  ✎ His function is analogous to that of a judge, who must accept the obligation of <u>revealing</u> in as obvious a manner as possible <u>the course of reasoning</u> which led him to his decision.
  他的作用类似于法官，法官必须承担这样的责任，即要以尽可能明显的方式揭示使他做出决定的推理的过程。（06考研英语-英译汉）

---

## **Lesson 35 - Justice was done**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
