<font color=gray size=4>The word *justice* is usually associated with courts of law. We might say that justice has been done when a man’s innocence or guilt has been proved beyond doubt. Justice is part of the complex machinery of the law. Those who seek it undertake an arduous journey and can never be sure that they will find it. Judges, however wise or eminent, are human and can make mistakes.

There are rare instances when justice almost ceases to be an abstract concept. Reward or punishment are meted out quite independent of human interference. At such times, justice acts like a living force. When we use a phrase like ‘it serves him right’, we are, in part, admitting that a certain set of circumstances has enabled justice to act of its own accord.

When a thief was caught on the premises of large jewellery store one morning, the shop assistants must have found it impossible to resist the temptation to say ‘it serves him right’. The shop was an old converted house with many large, disused fireplaces and tall, narrow chimneys. Towards midday, a girl heard a muffled cry coming from behind one of the walls. As the cry was repeated several times, she ran to tell the manager who promptly rang up the fire brigade. The cry had certainly come from one of the chimneys, but as there were so many of them, the fire fighters could not be certain which one it was. They located the right chimney by tapping at the walls and listening for the man’s cries. After chipping through a wall which was eighteen inches thick, they found that a man had been trapped in the chimney. As it was extremely narrow, the man was unable to move, but the fire fighters were eventually able to free him by cutting a huge hole in the wall. The sorry-looking, blackened figure that emerged, admitted at once that he had tried to break into the shop during the night but had got stuck in the chimney. He had been there for nearly ten hours. Justice had been done even before the man was handed over to the police.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **justice** n.[U] 正义，公正；司法，审判
  ✎ Children have a strong <u>sense of justice</u>. 孩子们有强烈的正义感。
  **justice has been <u>done/ served</u>** 正义得到了伸张（习语）
  ✎ We might say that <u>justice has been done</u> when a man’s innocence or guilt has been proved beyond doubt.（本文）
  **<u>do justice to…… / do…… justice</u>** 反映了……的真实水平（两种表达，依宾语长短选用）
  ✎ He didn’t <u>do himself justice</u> in the exams. 他在考试中没有正常发挥自己的水平。
  ✎ The photograph does not <u>do justice to</u> the rich colors of the gardens. 这张照片并没有反映出花园里丰富的色彩。
  **bring sb. to justice** 将某人绳之以法
  ✎ The killers will <u>be brought to justice</u>. 这些杀手一定会被绳之以法。
  **Justice has long arms.** 法网恢恢，疏而不漏。
+ **court** n. 朝廷，法庭；球场 v. 讨好，追求；招致
  + n.
    ✎ A friend in <u>court</u> is better than a penny in purse. 朝中有友，胜于囊中有钱。（谚语）
    形近词：**courtesy** 礼貌，礼节；**courteous** 讲礼貌的，懂礼节的
    **go to court** 打官司
    **settle sth. out of court** 私了
    ✎ a <u>tennis/ basketball</u> <u>court</u> 网球场/篮球场
  + v.
    ✎ Some businessmen <u>court</u> only wealthy clients. 一些商人只讨好富有的客户。
    ✎ John has been <u>courting</u> Mary for 3 years. 约翰追求玛丽已经三年了。
    ✎ <u>court</u> fame and gain 追求名和利/追名逐利
    ✎ Pride <u>courts</u> failure. 骄傲导致失败。
+ **innocence** n.[U] 清白，无辜；天真无邪（L11）
  反义词：**guilt** n.[U]
  ✎ It now remains for the jury to decide on the defendant’s <u>guilt</u> or <u>innocence</u>. 现在，陪审团将决定被告是否有罪。
  ✎ Children lose their <u>innocence</u> as they grow older. 随着年龄的增长，孩子们失去了天真。
  + **innocent** a. 清白的，无辜的
    ┏ **be innocent of……**
    ┗ **be guilty of……**
    ┏ He <u>is innocent of</u> murder. 他没有犯谋杀罪。
    ┗ He <u>is guilty of</u> murder.
+ **undertake** v. 承担，着手做；承诺
   + v. to accept that you are responsible for a piece of work, and start to do it 承担……并着手做
    **undertake <u>a task/ a project/ research/ a study/……</u>** 承担并开始做一项任务/一个项目/研究/一项研究
    ✎ University professors both teach and <u>undertake</u> research. 大学教授既教书又从事研究。
    ✎ The company has announced that it will <u>undertake</u> a full investigation into the accident. 该公司已宣布将着手开展对事故的一次全面调查。
  + 承诺
  **undertake to do sth. = promise to do sth.**
    ✎ He <u>undertook to</u> pay the money back in six months. 他承诺在六个月内还钱。
  + **undertaking** n. (重要而艰巨的)任务，工作；承诺
    ✎ The construction of the tunnel is a large and complex <u>undertaking</u>. 隧道的修建是一项庞大而复杂的工作/任务。
    ✎ Such <u>undertakings</u> require the precise planning and foresight of military operations.（L42）
    **give an undertaking** 做出承诺
    ✎ The landlord <u>gave</u> a written <u>undertaking</u> that repairs would be carried out before the end of the month. 房东做出书面承诺，称将在月底前进行维修。
+ **arduous** a. 艰苦的，费力的
  **arduous <u>task/ work</u>** 艰巨的任务/艰苦的工作
  ✎ the <u>arduous task</u> of loading all the boxes into the van 把所有箱子装进货车的艰巨任务
  **arduous <u>journey/ voyage</u>** 艰苦的旅行
  ✎ an <u>arduous journey</u> through the mountains 一次翻山越岭的艰苦旅行
  同义替换：
  **tough** a. 艰巨的，艰苦的
  ✎ a <u>tough</u> <u>game/ assignment/ journey</u> 艰苦的比赛/任务/旅行
  **laborious**
  ✎ Keeping the garden tidy all year round can be a <u>laborious</u> task. 一年到头把花园拾掇得干净整洁也不是件轻松活儿。
  **strenuous** 费力的
  ✎ a <u>strenuous</u> <u>climb/ walk</u> 艰苦的攀登/步行
  ✎ His doctor advised him not to take any <u>strenuous</u> exercise. 他的医生建议他不要做任何费力的运动。
+ **interference** n.[U] 干涉，管闲事（含贬义）
  **interference (in……)** 对……的干预；干涉某事
  ✎ I resent his <u>interference in</u> my work. 我讨厌他干涉我的工作。
  ✎ They expressed resentment at outside <u>interference in</u> their domestic affairs. 他们对外界干涉他们的内政表示不满。
  **interfere** v.
  **interfere (in……)** 干预某事
  ✎ Don’t <u>interfere in</u> matters that do not concern you! 不要干涉与你无关的事情！
  ✎ I wish my mother would stop <u>interfering</u> and let me make my own decisions.
  + 同义词：
    **meddle** 
    **meddle (in……)**
    ✎ You’re always <u>meddling</u>. 你总是爱管闲事。
    ✎ Don’t <u>meddle in</u> my affairs. 别干涉我的事。
    ✎ He accused the US of <u>meddling in</u> China’s internal affairs. 他指责美国干涉中国内政。
    **meddlesome = interfering** a.
    ✎ a/ an <u>meddlesome/ interfering</u> old woman 一个爱管闲事的老女人
  + 近义词：
    **intervene (in……)** 干预（褒义-避免坏事发生）
    ✎ She might have been killed if the neighbours hadn’t <u>intervened</u>. 如果邻居没有干预，她可能已经被杀了。
    ✎ The Central Bank <u>intervened in</u> the currency markets today to try to stabilize the exchange rate. 中央银行今天干预了货币市场，试图稳定汇率。
    **intervention** n.
    ✎ <u>military/ government</u> <u>intervention</u> 军事/政府干预
+ **accord** n. 一致；协议，条约
  + n. 一致
    **of one’s own accord** 主动地，自愿地，发自内心地
    ✎ He joined the army <u>of his own accord</u>. 他自愿参军了。
    ✎ The door seemed to move <u>of its own accord</u>. 门似乎自己会动。
    **with one accord** 一致地做某事，不约而同地，异口同声地
    ✎ <u>With one accord</u> they all stood up and cheered. 他们全体一致起立欢呼。
    **be in accord with sth.** 与……相一致
    ✎ These results <u>are in accord with</u> earlier research. 这些结果与早期研究相一致。
  + n. 协议，条约（常指国家间签订的、国际性的）
    ✎ the Helsinki <u>accord</u> on human rights 赫尔辛基人权条约/协议
    ✎ A peace <u>accord</u> was signed by both leaders. 双方领导人都签署了和平协议。
+ **convert** v. 改变（形式或用途）；改变信仰
  **convert (sth.) <u>to/ into</u> sth.** 把某物转变为新的用途/目的
  ✎ The stocks can <u>be</u> easily <u>converted to</u> cash. 这些股票可以很容易地转变为现金。
  ✎ They <u>converted</u> the spare bedroom <u>into</u> an office. 他们把这间多余的卧室转变成了办公室。
  ✎ The pub is a <u>converted</u> warehouse. 这家酒馆是由仓库改变而成的。（过去分词作形容词）
  ✎ a sofa that <u>converts into</u> a bed 一个可以转变成床的沙发
  **convert (sb.) to sth.** 转变某人的信仰
  ✎ European missionaries <u>converted</u> thousands <u>to</u> Christianity. 欧洲传教士使数千人皈依基督教。（Christian 基督徒）
  ✎ She <u>converted to</u> Catholicism. 她改信/皈依了天主教。（Catholic 天主教徒）
  **convertible** a. 可改变的，可转换的 n. 敞篷车
  ✎ a <u>convertible</u> sofa 一张沙发床


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **be associated with……** 与……联系起来（L8, L23）
  ✎ There are countless people who, ever since their early years, have learned to <u>associate</u> snails <u>with</u> food.（L23）
  近义搭配：
  **be related <u>with/ to</u>……**
  **be connected <u>with/ to</u>……**
  **be linked <u>with/ to</u>……**
+ **court of law** 法庭
> 仿写第1句
  成功这个词常常与勤奋联系到一起。
  The word success is usually associated with diligence.
  软弱这个词常常与女人联系到一起，然而这却不总是实情。
  The word frailty is usually associated with woman, yet this is not always the case.
  （参考：
  ① Frailty, thy name is woman.（莎士比亚）（thy: your；woman：泛指女人，可视作不可数）
  ② Yet this is not always the case.（L22））
+ **beyond (any) doubt** 确凿无疑地，毫无疑问地（加any语气更强）
  ✎ The research showed <u>beyond doubt</u> that smoking contributes to heart disease. 这项研究确凿无疑地表明吸烟会导致心脏疾病。（及物动词后，如果状语短宾语长，习惯先说状语后说宾语）
  ✎ His ability to succeed has been established <u>beyond any doubt</u>. 他获得成功的能力是毋庸置疑的。
  **beyond + n.** 无法……；不容……
  ◇ The situation is **beyond my control**. 这个形势我已经无法控制了。
  ◇ The rumor is **beyond belief**. 这样的谣言是无法令人相信的。
  ◇ The results are **beyond <u>dispute/ controversy</u>**. 这个结果是不容争辩的。
  ◇ Her beauty is **beyond <u>words/ description</u>**. 她的美丽是无法形容的。
  ◇ His conduct is **beyond <u>reproach/ criticism</u>**. 他的行为无可指摘。
  ◇ The pain is **beyond human endurance**. 这个疼痛是人无法忍受的。
  ◇ Working with you is **beyond my wildest dreams**. 和你一起工作是我梦寐以求的/做梦也想不到的。（wild 离奇的）
+ **part of**
  **当“part of”之前没有形容词修饰时，通常不加不定冠词“a”**
  ✎ <u>Part of</u> the building was destroyed in the fire. 这座建筑的一部分在火灾中被毁。
  ✎ Falling over is <u>part of</u> learning how to ski. 摔倒是学习如何滑雪的一部分。
  ✎ This idyllic pastoral scene is only <u>part of</u> the picture.（L41）
  ✎ Memory loss is <u>a **normal** part of</u> the aging process. 记忆力的丧失是衰老过程中一个很正常的部分。（aging 衰老，老化）
  ✎ …… so vast is the number of planets, that intelligent life is bound to be <u>a **natural** part of</u> the universe.（B4L43）
+ **machinery**
  + n.1.[U] organization or structure 组织，机构，体系
    **machinery of……**（引出同位语）
    **machinery for……**（表目的）
    ✎ the <u>machinery of</u> government 政府机构/体系
    ✎ The company has no effective <u>machinery for</u> resolving disputes. 这家公司没有解决争端的有效机构。
  + n.2.[U] machines 机器（L6, L21）
    ✎ a piece of <u>machinery</u> 一个机器
    ✎ You should not drive or operate <u>machinery</u> after taking the medicine. 服药后不应驾驶或操作机器。
+ **those** who seek it
  定语从句的**先行词**，在当代英语中，一般用**指示代词**不用人称代词。
+ **seek** 追求，想得到（L27）
  ✎ In <u>seeking</u> independence, they do not sacrifice their human dignity.（L27）
+ **arduous journey** 艰苦的旅程（固定用法）
  ✎ You will not have to spend the next few days recovering from a long and <u>arduous journey</u>.（L44）
> 仿写第1段倒数第2句
  追求完美(perfection)的人要走过一段艰苦的旅程，并且永远没有把握他们能达到(achieve)完美。
  Those who seek perfection undertake an arduous journey and can never be sure that they will achieve it.
+ ……, however wise or eminent **(they are)**,…… **状语从句的省略**（L5）
  需满足的条件：① 状语从句主语跟主句主语统一；② 状语从句谓语是be动词。
  ✎ Metals expand when <u>(they are)</u> heated. 当被加热后，金属会膨胀。
  ✎ While <u>(he was)</u> on a walking tour with his wife, he stopped to talk to a workman.（L36）
+ human a. 人的，人类的；~~n. 人~~
> 仿写第1段末句
  年轻人，无论多么年轻，多么没有经验(inexperienced)，也应该受到尊重。
  Young men, however young or inexperienced, should be treated with respect.
  罪犯，无论有多么残忍(cruel)或邪恶(vicious)，也是人，而且应该人道主义地(humanely)对待他们。
  Criminals, however cruel or vicious, are human and should be treated humanely.
+ **there are rare instances when…… = occasionally** 偶然地，个别情况下（L14, L27）
  ✎ <u>There are rare instances when</u> love turns to hatred. 在个别情况下，爱会变成恨。
  类似句型：
  **there are instances when……** 有时候
  **= there are times when……**
  **= sometimes**
  ✎ <u>There are times when</u> we would willingly give everything we possess to save our lives, yet we might grudge paying a surgeon a high fee for offering us precisely this service.（L27）
  **there was a time when……** 曾经，曾几何时
  **= once**
  ✎ <u>There was a time when</u> the owners of shops and businesses in Chicago had to pay large sums of money to gangsters in return for ‘protection’.（L14）
+ **cease <u>to do/ doing</u>** fml. 不再…… stop doing
  ✎ That department has <u>ceased to exist</u>. 那个部门已经不复存在了。（to do倾向静态的状态）
  ✎ The factory has <u>ceased making</u> bicycles. 这家工厂已经不再生产自行车。（doing倾向可延续的动作）
  辨：
  ┏ **stop doing** 停止做某事
  ┗ **stop to do** 停下正在做的事，去做另一件事
  ✎ Please <u>stop smoking</u>. Smoke really bothers me. 请停止吸烟。烟味真的让我很烦。
  ✎ I’m exhausted. Let’s <u>stop to smoke</u>. 我累坏了。我们停下来抽烟吧。
  ✎ <u>Stop to</u> smell the flowers. 驻足片刻闻花香。（谚语）
+ **abstract** 抽象的
  ✎ Beauty itself is <u>abstract</u>. 美本身是抽象的。
  反义词：
  **concrete/ solid** 具体的
  ✎ a <u>concrete/ solid</u> example 一个具体的例子
> 仿写第2段第1句
  在有些情况下爱国主义(patriotism)不再是(cease to be)一个空洞的(empty)口号(slogan)。（L14有类似的例句）
  <u>There are instances when</u> patriotism ceases to be an empty slogan.

+ Reward **or** punishment **are** meted out quite independent of human interference.
  奖励和惩罚确实都被施予了，作复数含义，故用are。（此例特殊，通常遵循就近原则即可）
  ✎ A man <u>or</u> a woman <u>is</u> waiting in the room. 房间里不可能是两个人，故遵循就近原则，a woman单数，用is。
+ **mete <u>sth. 🗘 out</u> (to sb.)** give or administer (punishment, rewards, etc) 给予，加以（奖、惩等）
  ✎ He felt he had a right to <u>mete out</u> physical punishment <u>to</u> the children. 他觉得他有权对孩子们进行体罚。
  ✎ Judges are <u>meting out</u> increasingly harsh sentences for car theft. 法官们对汽车盗窃的判决越来越严厉。
+ **be independent of……** 独立于……；不依赖于……（L9）
✎ We need a central bank that <u>is independent of</u> the government. 我们需要一个独立于政府的中央银行。
  反义搭配：
  **be dependent <u>on/ upon</u>……**
+ **quite independent of……** 在完全没有……的情况下（独自）……（此结构可直接作状语）
> 仿写第2段第2句“quite independent of……”结构
  计算机可以在完全没有人类干预的情况下发现潜在的问题并将其解决。
  Computers can find out potential problems and solve them <u>quite independent of</u> human interference.
  这个小男孩在完全没有父母帮助的情况下独立完成了这个拼图游戏(jigsaw puzzle)。
  The little boy finished the jigsaw puzzle <u>quite independent of</u> his parents’ assistance.
+ a **living** force 活的，有生命的（作定语）
  ✎ He is <u>living</u> proof of the wonders of modern medicine. 他是当代医学奇迹的活生生的证明。
+ it serves him right 他罪有应得
  同义表达：
  ◇ It serves you right.
  ◇ You deserve it.
  ◇ You got what you deserve.（多指倒霉事）
  ◇ You’re asking for it.
  ◇ As you’ve made your bed, now you have to lie on it.
+ **in part = partly = to some degree** 在某种程度上，部分地
  ✎ The accident was due <u>in part</u> to the bad weather. 事故的部分原因是恶劣的天气。
  ✎ Public distrust of scientists stems <u>in part</u> from the blurring of boundaries between science and technology, between discovery and manufacture.
  公众对科学家的不信任部分源于科学与技术、发现与制造之间边界的模糊。（六级阅读真题）
  ✎ Blacks have significantly shorter life spans, <u>in part</u> due to racism in the health establishment.
  黑人的寿命明显较短，部分原因是卫生机构里的种族歧视。（六级阅读真题）
  **for one’s part** 对某人来说，就某人而言，至于某人（part 无单复数变化）
  ✎ <u>For my part</u>, I prefer to live in the city. 就我而言，我更喜欢住在城市里。
  **<u>on the part of…… / on one’s part</u>** （前事）是某人做的（书面语）
  ┏ It was a mistake <u>on my part</u>. 这是我犯的一个错误。
  ┗ It was a mistake <u>on the part of</u> the authorities. 这是当局的一个错误。
  ✎ It was not a matter of choice for the traveler or merely a charitable impulse <u>on the part of</u> the settlers. It reflected the harshness of daily life: if you didn’t take in the stranger and take care of him, there was no one else who would. And someday, remember, you might be in the same situation.（take in ① 欺骗某人；② 收容某人）（考研英语阅读真题）
+ **enable sb. to do** 使某人能够做某事
+ **of one’s own accord** 主动地，自愿地（书面语）
  ✎ He joined the army <u>of his own accord</u>. 他自愿参军了。
+ **premises** n.[plural] the buildings and land that a shop, restaurant, company etc uses 房屋建筑物，经营场所
┏ **on the premises** 在经营场所内部，在店铺之内
┗ **off the premises** 在经营场所外部，在店铺之外
✎ There is always a manager <u>on the premises</u>. 总有一个经理在公司。
✎ The manager escorted him <u>off the premises</u>. 经理护送他离开了公司。
+ **find it impossible to resist the temptation to do……** 认为抵制做这件事的诱惑是不可能的事；忍不住做某事
  **忍不住做某事**的其它表达
  **can’t help doing……**（help 避免）
  **can’t help but do……**
  ✎ The shop assistants <u>couldn’t help saying</u> ‘it serves him right’.（原文同义换用）
  ✎ The shop assistants <u>couldn’t help but say</u> ‘it serves him right’.（原文同义换用）
> 仿写 <u>find it impossible to resist the temptation to do……</u>
  当我看到那只迷人的(fascinating)玩具熊(teddy bear)的时候，我忍不住买了下来。
  When I saw that fascinating teddy bear, I <u>found it impossible to resis the temptation to</u> buy it.
+ ┏ **disused** a. 废弃不用的
  ✎ Many <u>disused</u> railway lines have become public footpaths. 许多停用的铁路线已经成了公用的小路。
  ┗ **unused** a. 未使用过的
  ✎ an <u>unused</u> envelope 一个没用过的信封
+ **towards[英] / toward[美]** prep. near (a point in time) 临近（某一时间）
  ✎ <u>Toward</u> the end of the afternoon it began to rain. 傍晚时分，天开始下雨了。
  ✎ After having been wounded <u>towards</u> the end of the war, he had been sent to hospital and was separated from his unit.（L36）
+ **muffle** v. to make a sound less loud and clear, especially by covering something
  ✎ The falling snow <u>muffled</u> the sound of our footsteps. 飘落的雪使我们的脚步声变得沉闷。
  **muffled** a. muffled sounds cannot be heard clearly, for example because they come from behind a door or wall
  ✎ I could hear <u>muffled</u> voices in the next room. 我能听到隔壁房间里模糊不清的声音。
+ **副词和介词短语都可以作介词的宾语**（L10）
  ✎ <u>from</u> <u>behind one of the walls</u>（本文）
  ✎ There is a fine view <u>from</u> <u>here</u>.（here 副词）从这里可以看到很好的视野/景色。
  ✎ I heard them calling me <u>from</u> <u>below</u>.（below 副词）我听见他们从下面叫我。
  ✎ Suddenly, there was a slight trembling sound <u>from</u> <u>below</u>, and the captain went down to see what had happened.（L10）
  ✎ They have just returned <u>from</u> <u>abroad</u>.（abroad 副词）他们刚从国外回来。
  ✎ I took my watch <u>from</u> <u>under the pillow</u>.（under the pillow 介词短语）我从枕头下拿了出手表。
  ✎ He picked up the gun <u>from</u> <u>behind the counter</u>.（behind the counter 介词短语）他从柜台后面拿起了枪。
  ✎ I live <u>near</u> <u>here</u>.（here 副词）我住在这附近。
  ✎ We didn’t meet <u>until</u> <u>after the show</u>.（after the show 介词短语）我们直到演出结束后才见面。
  ✎ The weather has been fine <u>except</u> <u>in the north</u>.（in the north 介词短语）除了北部地区，天气一直很好。
+ 相当于**并列句**的**定语从句**
  句末的内容刚好是后半句的一个成分。
  ┏ As the cry was repeated several times, she ran to tell <u>the manager</u> **who** promptly rang up the fire brigade.（原文）
  ┗ As the cry was repeated several times, she ran to tell <u>the manager</u> **and** <u>the manager</u> promptly rang up the fire brigade.（换用并列句形式）
  ✎ John went to see his <u>bank manager</u> **who** sent the remains of wallet and the money to the special department of the Bank of England in Newcastle: the Mutilate Ladies!（L7）
  ✎ Much to the aristocrat’s amusement, the gaoler returned a few moments later with a pair of glasses and <u>the usual copy of the letter</u> **which** he proceeded to read to the prisoner.（L22）
+ **promptly**（L14）
  ① ad. immediately 立即，立刻，马上
  ✎ If the money was not paid <u>promptly</u>, the gangsters would quickly put a man out of business by destroying his shop.（L14）
  ✎ And he <u>promptly</u> handed the sheet of paper to the gaoler.（L22）
  ② ad. punctually 准时地
  ✎ They arrived <u>promptly</u> at two o’clock. 他们在两点钟准时抵达。
+ **<u>ring/ call/ phone</u> <u>sb. 🗘 up</u>** 给某人/某机构打电话（偏英式用法）
  ✎ She uses the office phone to <u>ring up</u> her friends in Sweden. 她使用办公室电话给在瑞典的朋友打了个电话。
  ✎ John <u>called</u> him <u>up</u> to make sure of the date of the graduation ceremony. 约翰给他打了个电话，来确定毕业典礼的日期。
  ┏ I’ll <u>phone</u> the manager <u>up</u> tomorrow. 明天我给经理打电话。
  ┗ I’ll <u>phone up</u> the manager tomorrow.
+ **the fire <u>brigade[英]/ department[美]</u>** 消防队（L15）
  **fireman, firefighter, fire fighter** 消防队员
+ **locate** v. discover the exact position or place of <u>sb./ sth.</u> 定位
  ✎ We couldn’t <u>locate</u> the source of the radio signal. 我们无法确定这个无线电信号的来源。
  ✎ Police are still trying to <u>locate</u> the suspect. 警方仍在试图找到嫌疑犯。
+ **tap** v. to hit your fingers lightly on something, for example to get sb.’s attention 轻拍某物
  **tap <u>at/ on</u>……**
  ✎ Someone <u>tapped at/ on</u> the door. 有人敲门。
  ✎ A sound made by <u>tapping on</u> the hull of a ship will be reflected from the sea bottom,……（B4L7）
  **tap sb. on the <u>shoulder/ arm/ chest/ etc.</u>** 轻拍某人的肩膀/胳膊/胸等
  ✎ Ralph <u>tapped me on the shoulder</u>. 拉尔夫轻轻地拍了拍我的肩膀。
+ **listen (out) for sth.** wait alertly in order to hear (a sound) 留神等着听（某声音）
  辨：**listen to** 仅表示“听”这个动作
  ✎ Please <u>listen (out) for</u> the phone while I’m in the bath. 我洗澡的时候，请留神听电话。
  ✎ Can you <u>listen (out) for</u> the doorbell? 你能留意听门铃吗？
+ **语言表达的准确与传神**
  ┏ They <u>located</u> the right chimney by <u>tapping at</u> the walls and <u>listening for</u> the man’s cries.（原文）
  ┗ They <u>knocked at</u> the walls **and** <u>listened to</u> the man’s cries, **and** then <u>found</u> the right chimney.（用词不准，句子主次不分）
  ┏ <u>The fire brigade was called</u> and two fire fighters <u>freed</u> George <u>using a special type of grease</u>.（L15）
  ┗ <u>Someone called the fire brigade</u> and two fire fighters <u>used</u> a special type of grease and then <u>freed</u> George.
+ **chip** 凿
  ✎ It took a long time to <u>chip</u> a hole in the wall. 在墙上凿一个洞花了很长时间。（及物）
  ✎ Archaeologists were carefully <u>chipping</u> away at the rock. 考古学家正在仔细地把多余的岩石凿掉。（不及物）
+ **trap** v. to prevent sb. from leaving a place, especially a dangerous place
  ✎ Twenty miners <u>were trapped</u> underground. 二十名矿工被困在了地下。
  ✎ Dozens of people <u>were trapped</u> in the rubble when the building collapsed. 大楼倒塌时，数十人被困在瓦砾中。
  ✎ There’s no way out! We<u>’re trapped</u>! 没有出路了！我们被困住了！
  + 近义替换：
    **<u>be/ get</u> stuck** 被卡住（原形：stick）
    ✎ A crowd of people gathered round him and a lady rubbed his arm with soap and butter, but George <u>was firmly stuck</u>.（L15）
    ✎ The sorry-looking, blackened figure that emerged, admitted at once that he had tried to break into the shop during the night but had <u>got stuck</u> in the chimney.（本文）
  + 近义搭配：
    **be cornered** 被逼到绝境；使走投无路
    ✎ It immediately ran away when she saw it, and experts confirmed that a puma will not attack a human being unless it <u>is cornered</u>.（L1）
    **be kept in……** 被关在……里面
    ✎ As there are so many people about, the dogs have to <u>be kept in</u> a special enclosure.（L8）
    **be imprisoned** 被关在监狱里面
    ✎ A famous actor in a highly successful play was once cast in the role of an aristocrat who had <u>been imprisoned</u> in the Bastille for twenty years.（L22）
+ <u>**As it was extremely** narrow</u>^1^, the man was unable to move, but the fire fighters were eventually able to **free**^2^ him by cutting a huge hole in the wall.
  ^1^ ✎ <u>As it was extremely heavy</u>, he dumped it on the counter.（L31）
  ^2^ ✎ The fire brigade was called and two fire fighters <u>freed</u> George using a special type of grease.（L15）
+ **sorry** a. feeling ashamed or unhappy about something bad you have done
  ✎ She <u>was</u> genuinely <u>sorry for</u> what she had done. 她对自己所做的事感到由衷地羞愧。
  + 相似的复合形容词（-looking 看起来……的）：
    ◇ the <u>sorry-looking</u>, blackened figure 看起来满面羞愧的（本文）
    ◇ a very <u>modern-looking</u> woman 看起来很摩登的/时髦的（L3）
    ◇ an <u>interesting-looking</u> carved dagger 看起来有趣的（L34）
    ◇ an <u>ugly-looking</u> black goat 看起来丑陋的（L48）
+ **blacken** v. to become black, or make something black （使）变黑
  ✎ The thunder became louder and the sky <u>blackened</u>. 雷声越来越大了，天空也变得黑了。
+ **figure** n. someone with a particular type of appearance or character, especially when they are far away or difficult to see
  ✎ In the torchlight, he caught sight of a <u>figure</u> whom he immediately recognized as Bill Wilkins, our local grocer. 模糊的人影（L2）
  ✎ A farm worker, who stayed up all night, claimed to have seen a <u>figure</u> cutting corn in the moonlight. 模糊的人影（L30）
+ **break into sth.** to enter a building or car by using force, in order to steal sth.
  ✎ Someone <u>broke into</u> my car and stole the radio. 有人闯进了我的车偷走了收音机。
  ✎ Her house <u>was broken into</u> last week. 她的房子上周被闯入了。
  **break in**: to enter a building by using force, in order to steal sth.
  ✎ If anyone tries to <u>break in</u>, the alarm will go off. 如果有人试图闯入，警报就会响起。
  **force an entry** 强行闯入（entry 入口）
  ✎ It was as clear as daylight then that burglars had <u>forced an entry</u> during her absence.（L58）
  ✎ There was no sign of a <u>forced entry</u>. 没有破门而入/强行进入的迹象。（作名词短语）
+ **hand sb. over to……** give a prisoner to another group of people, especially the police or the people in authority in another country
  ✎ The terrorists were taken to the airport, where they <u>were handed over to</u> the French authorities. 恐怖分子被带到了机场，在那里他们被移交给法国当局。

---

## **Lesson 36 - A chance in a million**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>We are less credulous than we used to be. In the nineteenth century, a novelist would bring his story to a conclusion by presenting his readers with a series of coincidences — most of them wildly improbable. Readers happily accepted the fact that an obscure maidservant was really the hero’s mother. A long-lost brother, who was presumed dead, was really alive all the time and wickedly plotting to bring about the hero’s downfall. And so on. Modern readers would find such naive solutions totally unacceptable. Yet, in real life, circumstances do sometimes conspire to bring about coincidences which anyone but a nineteenth century novelist would find incredible.

When I was a boy, my grandfather told me how a German taxi driver, Franz Bussman, found a brother who was thought to have been killed twenty years before. While on a walking tour with his wife, he stooped to talk to a workman. After they had gone on, Mrs. Bussman commented on the workman’s close resemblance to her husband and even suggested that he might be his brother. Franz poured scorn on the idea, pointing out that his brother had been killed in action during the war. Though Mrs. Bussman was fully acquainted with this story, she thought that there was a chance in a million that she might be right. A few days later, she sent a boy to the workman to ask him if his name was Hans Bussman. Needless to say, the man’s name was Hans Bussman and he really was Franz’s long-lost brother. When the brothers were reunited, Hans explained how it was that he was still alive. After having been wounded towards the end of the war, he had been sent to hospital and was separated from his unit. The hospital had been bombed and Hans had made his way back into Western Germany on foot. Meanwhile, his unit was lost and all records of him had been destroyed. Hans returned to his family home, but the house had been bombed and no one in the neighbourhood knew what had become of the inhabitants. Assuming that his family had been killed during an air raid, Hans settled down in a village fifty miles away where he had remained ever since.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **credulous** a. 轻信的（贬义）
  ✎ Anna is so <u>credulous</u> that she’ll believe anything you tell her. 安娜太轻信了，你告诉她什么，她都会相信。
  + 近义词：
    **naïve**[法] 天真的 naive
  + 字根：
    **cred = believe**
    **credit** n. 信用；赊账 ✎ credit card 信用卡
    ┏ **credulous** a. 轻信的，容易上当的
    ┗ **incredulous** a. 不容易上当的；有人生经验的
    ┏ **credible** a. 可信的
    ┗ **incredible** a. 难以置信的
    **credentials** n. 证书；证件
+ **obscure** a. 不起眼的；不出名的；难以理解的
  + ① unknown; little-known a. 不起眼的；不出名的
    ✎ an <u>obscure</u> little village 一个默默无闻的小村庄
    ✎ an <u>obscure</u> maidservant 一个不起眼的女佣
    **remain obscure** 一直默默无闻；一直不引人注意（固定短语）
    ✎ The environment is obviously important, but its role has <u>remained obscure</u>. 环境显然是重要的，但是它的作用却一直很少被大家了解。（考研阅读真题节选）
    反义词（著名的，大名鼎鼎的）：
    **well-known; famous; noted; notable;**
    **eminent; celebrated; renowned**
  + ② hard to understand a. 难以理解的
    ✎ Very few people could understand his lecture because it was very <u>obscure</u>.
    (A)faint; (B)obscure; (C)gloomy; (D)indefinite（六级单选真题）
+ **presume** v. 假定，推测，认为（暗示做出的假定是有依据的，是正确的合理的）
  ✎ From the way they talked, I presumed (that) they were a couple. 从他们的谈话方式来看，我推测他们是一对。
  **be presumed <u>dead/ innocent</u>……** 被认为已经死掉了/被推测是清白的
  ✎ A long-lost brother, who <u>was presumed dead</u>, was really alive all the time and wickedly plotting to bring about the hero’s downfall.（本文）
  ✎ You <u>are presumed innocent</u> until you are proved guilty. 直到你被证明有罪之前，你都被假定无罪。
  + 近义词：
    **believe, think, suppose, assume** 认为，推测，假定
    ✎ …… a German taxi driver, Franz Bussman, found a brother who <u>was thought to have been killed</u> twenty years before.（本文）
    ✎ Everyone went to the funeral, for the ‘ghost’ was none other than Eric Cox, a third brother who <u>was supposed to have died</u> as a young man.（L30）
    **be under the impression that……** 还以为……（暗示往往是错的）
    ✎ Though the crew <u>were</u> at first <u>under the impression that</u> the lost ship had been found, the contents of the chest proved them wrong.（L32）
    **take it for granted that……** 想当然地认为……
    ✎ You can’t <u>take it for granted that</u> the children will behave themselves. 你不能想当然地认为孩子们会规规矩矩。（behave oneself 老实的）
+ **plot** v. 秘密谋划，暗中策划；n. （电影或故事的）情节；阴谋诡计
  **plot to do = scheme to do** 谋划/密谋去做某事
  ┏ The criminal was <u>plotting/ scheming to</u> rob the bank. 罪犯正在密谋抢劫银行。
  近义搭配：
  **conspire to do** 密谋做某事（多指**合谋**坏事）
  ┗ The criminals <u>were conspiring to</u> rob the bank. 这伙罪犯正在密谋抢劫银行。
  + **conspire** 派生义：很多事情凑到一块，造成了一个不愉快的结果
    ✎ Bad weather and car trouble <u>conspired to</u> ruin our vacation. 恶劣的天气加上汽车故障毁掉了我们的假期。
+ **resemblance** n. 相似
  同根词：
  **resemble** v. 和某人某物非常像
  ✎ She closely <u>resembles</u> her mother in every way. 她在各方面都很像她的母亲。
  **bear a resemblance to……** 跟……很像
  ✎ The lady + ①/②/③
  ① <u>bears a resemblance to</u> my mother. 这个女士跟我妈妈有些像。
  ② <u>bears a close resemblance to</u> my mother. 这个女士跟我妈妈特别像。（加限定词）
  ③ <u>bears no resemblance to</u> my mother. 这个女士跟我妈妈一点都不像。
  ✎ Your school may have done away with winners and losers,but life has not. In some schools they have abolished failing grades; they’ll give you as many times as you want to get the right answer. This <u>doesn’t bear the slightest resemblance to</u> anything in real life.
  你的学校可能已经废除了赢家和输家，但生活并没有。在一些学校，他们废除了不及格的成绩；他们会给你想要多少就有多少的机会来得到正确的答案。这与现实生活中的任何事情都没有丝毫相似之处。（比尔盖茨给年轻人的10条生活准则-最后一条）（L27笔记）
+ **acquaint** v. 使某人熟悉或了解
  **<u>be/ get/ become</u> acquainted with……** 对……熟悉/对……变得熟悉
  ✎ I<u>’m not acquainted with</u> him. 我对他不熟悉。
  ✎ He <u>became acquainted with</u> the work. 他变得对这项工作熟悉起来了。
  同义替换：
  **<u>be/ get/ become</u> familiar with……** 
  ✎ He <u>was familiar with</u> the work.
  ✎ The work <u>was familiar to</u> him.（此结构可以倒着用）
  **acquaintance** n.[C] 熟人
  ✎ He is my only <u>acquaintance</u> in the little town. 他是我在这个小镇上唯一的熟人。
+ **reunite** v. 使团聚
  **be reunited with……** 与……团聚
  ✎ The lost children <u>were reunited with</u> their parents. 失踪的孩子与父母团聚了。
  **reunify** v. 使统一
  **reunification** n. 
  ✎ national <u>reunification</u> 国家统一大业


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ A chance in a million（夸张-L18）
+ We are less credulous than we <u>used to be (credulous)</u>.
  **used to do，如果do在前面出现过，do一般可去掉；**
  **used to be，如果be在前面出现过，be一般不可去掉。**
  ✎ We <u>spend</u> more time traveling than we <u>used to (do/ spend)</u>. 我们花在旅行上的时间比以前多了
+ ┏ **less + <u>a./ad.</u> + than……** 不像……那样……了
  ┗ **not <u>so/as</u> + <u>a./ad.</u> + as……**
  ✎ We are <u>not so/ as</u> credulous <u>as</u> we used to be.（原文同义换用）
  ┏ 他不像以前那么内向(introverted)了。
  ┗ He is <u>less</u> introverted <u>than</u> he used to be.
  ┗ He is <u>not so/ as</u> introverted <u>as</u> he used to be.
  ┏ 他英语说的不如以前好了。
  ┗ He speaks English <u>less</u> well <u>than</u> he used to.
  ┗ He does<u>n’t</u> speak English <u>so/ as</u> well <u>as</u> he used to.
+ **would 和 used to do 类似，都可以表示过去习惯性的动作，**
  如：One day in a week he <u>would</u> spend a whole day in silence.
  **但注意：would 不能用在故事开头，往往在故事开头用 used to do，而后面换为would do,**
  如：We <u>used to</u> work in the same office and we <u>would</u> often have coffee together.
+ **conclusion** n. 结束，结论，结果
  **bring sth. to a conclusion** 使某事结束，~~得出结论~~
  ✎ The two countries decided to <u>bring</u> the war <u>to a conclusion</u>. 两国决定停战/结束战争。
  **<u>come to/ arrive at/ reach/ draw</u> a conclusion** 得出结论
  **bring sth. to <u>a close/ an end</u>** 使结束，使终结
  ✎ The rally <u>was brought to a close/ an end</u> by the singing of the national anthem. 在国歌声中，大会落幕了。/大会是唱国歌的形式结束的。
  **end/ close/ conclude……** 结束……（及物动词表达）
  …… a novelist would <u>end/ close/ conclude</u> his story by……（原文同义换用）
+ **bring…… to……** 使……到达……状态
  ◇ It was the war that first **brought** him **to power**. 正是这场战争让他第一次掌权/当政。
  ◇ So far the US has been unable to **bring** him **to justice**. 到目前为止，美国一直未能将他绳之以法。
+ **present sb. with sth.** 把某物呈递给某人（L22）
  **present sth. to sb.**
  ✎ He entered the cell and <u>presented</u> the letter <u>to</u> the aristocrat.（L22）
+ **a series of** 一连串的（L33）
  ✎ …… <u>an unforeseen series of</u> catastrophes.（L33）
+ **coincidences** 巧合的事
  **by coincidence** 碰巧
  ✎ My mother is called Anna, and <u>by coincidence</u> my wife’s mother is called Anna too. 我的母亲叫安娜，巧合的是，我妻子的母亲也叫安娜。
  **coincide with sth.** ① 碰巧与某事同时发生；② 碰巧跟另外一个东西一样
  ✎ My arrival <u>coincided with</u> his departure. 我的到来恰逢他离开。
  ✎ If our schedules <u>coincide</u>, we’ll go to Shanghai together. 如果我们的日程安排一致，我们将一起去上海。
  ✎ His tastes and habits <u>coincide</u> with those of his wife.
  (A)combine；(B)compete；(C)coincide；(D)compromise（六级真题）
  ✎ It is fortunate for the old couple that their son’s career goals and their wishes for him <u>coincide</u>.
  (A)coincide；(B)comply；(C)conform；(D)collaborate（六级真题）
+ — most of them (being) wildly improbable.（原文-独立主格）
  【✘】— most of them were wildly improbable.（完整的主系表句，需用连词连接）
  【✔】— <u>and/ but</u> most of them were wildly improbable.（语法正确，但啰嗦，重点不够突出）
  【✔】— most of <u>which</u> were wildly improbable.（定语从句，简洁，但依然不如独立主格简洁）
  ┏ Apart from an interesting-looking carved dagger, the box was full of crockery, <u>much of it broken</u>.（L34）
  ┗ Apart from an interesting-looking carved dagger, the box was full of crockery, <u>and/ but much of it was broken</u>.（换用并列句）
  ┗ Apart from an interesting-looking carved dagger, the box was full of crockery, <u>much of which was broken</u>.（换用定语从句）
  ✎ 考古学家发现了十五尊雕像^主^，每一尊代表着一位女神^次^。
  The archaeologists found fifteen statues, each of them representing a goddess.
+ **be presumed <u>dead/ innocent</u>……** 被认为死了/是清白的（固定搭配）
  ✎ Their nephew was missing, <u>presumed dead</u>. 他们的侄子失踪了，被认为已经死亡。（作非谓语动词，be被删掉）
  ✎ In English law, an accused man <u>is presumed innocent</u> until he is proved guilty. 在英国法律中，一个被指控的人直到被证明有罪之前会假定是清白的。
+ **alive**（a开头的形容词，通常不能放在名词前作前置定语）
  ✎ He may hunt, beg, or steal occasionally to keep himself <u>alive</u>,……（L27）
  相关词：
  **living** 活着的（通常作前置定语）
  ✎ all <u>living</u> things 所有生物
  ✎ <u>living</u> proof 活生生的证据（L35）
  ✎ At such times, justice acts like a <u>living</u> force.（L35）
  **live** 活着的(通常作前置定语)；现场的；带电的
  ✎ experiments on <u>live</u> animals 活体动物实验
  ✎ be transmitted <u>live</u> 现场直播
  ✎ Is the wire <u>live</u>? 这个电线有电吗？
+ **plot**
  【✔】…… and wickedly <u>plotting to</u>……（原文）
  【✔】…… and wickedly <u>scheming to</u>……（同义换用）
  【✘】…… and wickedly <u>conspiring to</u>……（一个人无法合谋）
  ✎ a <u>plot</u> to assassinate the President 一个刺杀总统的阴谋（assassin 刺客）
  近义词：
  **scheme, intrigue** 阴谋
  **conspiracy** 合谋
  **schemes and intrigues** 阴谋诡计
  ✎ All the imperialist <u>schemes and intrigues</u> are doomed to failure. 所有帝国主义的阴谋诡计注定会失败。（毛泽东）
+ **downfall**
  +  n.1. fall from a position of prosperity or power 垮台
  ✎ Greed led to his <u>downfall</u>. 贪婪导致了他的垮台。
  + n.2. thing that causes this 引起垮台的事情，垮台的原因
  ✎ His vanity was his <u>downfall</u>. 他的虚荣心是他垮台的原因。/他的虚荣心导致了他的垮台。
    + 同义替换：
      **undoing** 垮台的原因
      ✎ The team’s weak defense was their <u>undoing</u>. 该队孱弱的防守是他们失败的原因。
      ✎ That proved to be my <u>undoing</u>, for I soon got back to my old bad habit of dozing off in front of the screen.（L50）
+ **and so on** 等等（L33）
  同义替换：
  **and so forth**
  **and the like**（口语）
  **and what not**（口语）
  **etc.** (et cetera)
+ **unacceptable** 不可接受的
  近义替换：
  **improbable** 不大可能的
  **incredible** 难以置信的
  **unbelievable** 难以置信的
  **inconceivable** 难以想象的
  **unconvincing** 令人难以相信的；没有说服力的
  **preposterous** 荒谬的

#### **用宾语补足语而非宾语从句，以使句子简洁。**
> 仿写第1段倒数第2句
  中国学生会觉得这么简单的考试是完全无法相信的。
  Chinese students would **find** <u>such easy examinations^宾^</u> <u>totally incredible^宾补^</u>.

✎ Though the crew were at first under the impression that the lost ship had been found, the contents of the chest **proved** <u>them^宾^</u> <u>wrong^宾补^</u>.（L32）
✎ 事实证明他们的担心是多余的。
The facts **proved** <u>their worries^宾^</u> <u>unnecessary^宾补^</u>.
✎ 事实证明他的指责毫无根据。
The facts **proved** <u>his accusation^宾^</u> <u>totally groundless^宾补^</u>.
✎ If you lived in the Mediterranean, for instance, you would **consider** <u>octopus^宾^</u> <u>a great delicacy^宾补^</u>.（L23）
✎ 如果你住在北京，你就会把豆汁儿(Douzhir)当作一道美味佳肴。
If you lived in Beijing, you would **consider** <u>Douzhir^宾^</u> <u>a great delicacy^宾补^</u>.（L23仿写）
✎ 如果你住在中国东北地区(the Northeast of China)，你就会非常喜欢滑冰。
If you lived in the Northeast of China, you would **consider** <u>skating^宾^</u> <u>a great pleasure^宾补^</u>.（L23仿写）

+ ┏ **in real life** 在现实生活中
  ┗ **in the real world**（同义替换）
+ **circumstances** n.[pl.] 情形，情况，状况
  **Under no circumstances** should you approach that man. 绝不要做某事
  **Due to circumstances beyond our control**,…… 由于出现了无法控制的情况
+ **do** 的确，确实（加强语气）
+ **conspire to do sth.** 密谋做某事（多指**合谋**坏事）
  ✎ Falling demand and high interest rates have <u>conspired to</u> produce a big drop in profits. 下降的需求和高利率共同导致利润大幅下降。
+ **but** prep. 除了……之外，~~conj. 但是~~
  ✎ Nobody <u>but</u> Robert would do such a thing. 除了罗伯特，没有人会做这样的事。
  ✎ Who <u>but</u> a fool would do such a thing? 除了傻瓜，谁会做这样的事？
  ✎ His house is **the last but one** in the street. 他的房子是街上倒数第二个。
  ✎ Take **the next turning but one** on your left. 在第二个路口左转。
  + **nothing but = only**（通常接名词）
    ✎ He is <u>nothing but</u> a thief. 他只不过是个小偷。
  + **anything but = not at all** 一点也不（通常接名词、形容词）
    ✎ He is <u>anything but</u> a hero. 他绝不是个英雄。
    ✎ He is <u>anything but</u> stupid. 他一点都不傻。
  + **all but = almost** ad.（修饰形容词、副词、动词）
    ✎ Britain’s coal industry has <u>all but</u> disappeared. 英国的煤炭工业几乎消失了。
    ✎ His left arm was <u>all but</u> useless. 他的左胳膊几乎没用了。
  + **but后可跟不定式(to) do**
  ┏ We have nothing to <u>do</u> **but** <u>wait</u> here. 除了等，我们没有任何事情可做。（前面出现实义动词do，则to省略）
  ┗ We have no choice **but** <u>to wait</u> here. 除了等，我们别无选择。（前面没有出现实义动词do，则to保留）
> 仿写第1段末句
  在现实生活中，有时确实很多情况会凑到一起导致一连串的大灾难，而这些事情除了受害者之外可能谁也不会相信。
  In real life, circumstances do sometimes conspire to bring about a series of catastrophes which anyone but the victims would find incredible.
+ 【✔】When I was a boy,……（原文）
  【✘】When a boy,……（状语从句主语和主句主语统一时，才可省略状语的主语和be动词）
  【✔】In my childhood,……
  【✔】In my early years,……
  【✔】In my teens,……
  【✔】In my adolescence,…… 青春期
  【✔】In my youth,…… 青年
+ was thought to have been killed
  ① be thought to do（固定搭配）
  ② 不定式的完成时：to have done
  ✎ Everyone went to the funeral, for the ‘ghost’ was none other than Eric Cox, a third brother who <u>was supposed to have died</u> as a young man.（L30）
+ ┏ **comment on……** 对……发表评论
  ✎ I don’t want to <u>comment on</u> other people’s views. 我不想评论别人的观点。
  **No comment.** 无可奉告。
  ┗ **comment that……**
  ┏ **remark on……**
  ┗ **remark that……**
+ close resemblance
  同义动词短语：
  **bear a close resemblance to……** 跟某人特别像
  **closely resemble……**
  ┗ Mrs. Bussman <u>commented/ remarked</u> that **the workman <u>bore a close resemblance to her husband</u>**.（原文换用）
  ┗ Mrs. Bussman <u>commented/ remarked</u> that **the workman <u>closely resembled her husband</u>**.（原文换用）
  更多同义表达：
  ✎ The workman and her husband **were <u>extraordinarily similar/ particularly alike</u>**.（借鉴自L1）
  ✎ The workman and her husband **had a lot in common**.
  ✎ **There <u>were striking similarities/ was considerable commonality</u> between** the workman **and** her husband.
+ **suggest** 暗示，~~建议~~
  表建议，后面必须用should do型的虚拟语气
+ **pour scorn on……** 对……嗤之以鼻/不屑一顾（**pour** 倒水；**scorn** 轻蔑，鄙视）
  + 同义替换：
    **pour contempt on……**
    **pour ridicule on……**
  + 类似搭配：
    **pour cold water on……** 打击某人的积极性
  + ✎ Franz didn’t take the idea seriously.（原文同义改写）
+ ┏ ……, <u>pointing out that</u> his brother had been killed……（原文）指出，提醒某人注意（that不用在介词后，此处out不作介词而作副词）
  ┗ ……, <u>reminding her that</u> his brother had been killed……（同义替换）
  ✎ I must <u>point out that</u> you are making a dangerous mistake. 我必须指出，你正在犯一个危险的错误。
  ✎ At this, the police <u>pointed out</u> ironically <u>that</u> this would hardly be necessary as the men were already under arrest.（L40）
+ …… his brother <u>had been killed in action</u> during the war. 在战斗中牺牲
  ✎ His father told everybody that Eric <u>had been killed in action</u>.（L30）
+ ┏ Though Mrs. Bussman <u>was fully acquainted with</u> this story,……（原文）
  ┗ Though Mrs. Bussman <u>was fully familiar with</u> this story,……
+ ┏ ……, she thought that there was <u>a chance in a million that</u> she might be right.（原文）
  **the <u>slightest/ remotest</u> chance** 微弱的可能性（固定搭配）
  ┗ ……, she thought there was <u>the slightest/ remotest chance that</u> she might be right.
> 仿写第2段第5句
  尽管这位侦探非常了解这位老太太对周围每一个人总是这么好，但他认为仍有一丝可能这位老太太就是谋杀犯。
  Though the detective was fully acquainted with the fact that the old lady was always so kind to everybody, he thought that there was a chance in a million that she might be the murderer.
+ **Needless to say** 不用说也能知道
  **= As you can imagine** 正如你能想象到的那样
  ✎ <u>Needless to say</u> our house is now surrounded by a jungle.（L46）
+ **how it was**: how it happened 这件事是如何发生的（宾语从句内嵌套主语从句）
  ✎ 当Eric回到农场后，他解释了他是怎么从团里逃出来的。
  When Eric returned to the farm, he explained how it was that he deserted his regiment.
+ ┏ After having been wounded……（after 作介词，后加动名词的完成时（强调动作先发生，L4））
  ┗ After he had been wounded……（after 作连词，后加过去完成时从句）
+ **towards/ toward** 临近某个时候（L35）
  ✎ <u>towards/ toward</u> midnight 快到午夜的时候
  ✎ <u>Towards midday</u>, a girl heard a muffled cry coming from behind one of the walls.（L35）
+ ┏ **send sb. to hospital** 送某人去看病
  ┗ **take sb. to hospital**
  **be taken to hospital** 被送到医院
  ✎ A man who had broken his right leg <u>was taken to hospital</u> a few weeks before Christmas.（L29）
  
  **be in hospital** 在住院
  **= be hospitalized**
  **be out of hospital** 出院
  **= leave hospital**
  ✎ To compensate for his unpleasant experiences <u>in hospital</u>, the man drank a little more than was good for him. 住院（L29）
  ✎ The following day, however, the doctor consoled him by telling him that his chances of being able to <u>leave hospital</u> in time for New Year celebrations were good. 出院（L29）
+ **separate…… from……** A和B隔离开，不能见面（se- 分离，分开；par: part）
  ✎ Theory should never <u>be separated from</u> practice. 理论永远不能脱离实践。
  同义替换：
  **cut…… off from……** 从……上把……切下来
  ✎ She realized that he was trying to <u>cut</u> her <u>off from</u> her friends. 她意识到他正试图切断她与她朋友的联系。
  **isolate…… from……**
  ✎ He <u>was isolated from</u> all the other prisoners. 他被与其他囚犯隔离开了。
  **segregate…… from……**（只能接人，多指因种族、宗教、性别等把人隔离）
  ✎ Blacks <u>were segregated from</u> whites in every area of life. 黑人在生活的各个领域都与白人隔离开了。
+ **make one’s way** 前往某地，去某地（常跟介词短语搭配）（L15）
  ✎ I <u>made my way</u> <u>to the house</u>. 我朝房子走了过去。
  ✎ I <u>made my way</u> <u>into the backyard</u>. 我走进了后院。
  ✎ I <u>made my way</u> <u>along the river</u>. 我沿着河走去。
  ✎ I <u>made my way</u> <u>up the stairs</u>. 我走上了楼。
  ✎ Turning back down the main street, we quickened our pace and <u>made our way</u> rapidly <u>towards the stream</u> where we hoped the boatman was waiting.（L48）
+ **v. + one’s way**（详见L15：find one’s way）
+ **family home** 老家（父母、兄弟姐妹一块住的那个家）
+ **become of <u>sb./ sth.</u>** 某人/某物现在情况如何（多用于What、Whatever引导的疑问句或从句）
  ✎ What has <u>become of</u> Jane? 简现在情况怎么样？
  ✎ Whatever <u>became of</u> the parcel you sent? 你寄的包裹到底怎么样了？
+ **whereabouts** n.[pl.] 下落
  ✎ No one in the neighborhood knew his family’s <u>whereabouts</u>. 附近没有人知道他家人的下落。
  ✎ Despite numerous searches and enquiries, her <u>whereabouts</u> are still unknown. 尽管进行了多次搜查和询问，但她的下落仍然未知。
+ **inhabitant** n. 居民（书面语）（字根 **habit**：居住，~~习惯~~）
  **inhabit** vt. 居住在某地
  ✎ In the future people may <u>inhabit</u> other planets. 在未来，人们可能会居住在其他行星上。
  **cohabit** vi.（未婚者）同居
  **cohabit with……** 与某人同居
  **cohabitant** n. 同居者
  **habitat** 栖息地
+ **assuming (that)……** 以为；假定，假如（本身可做复合连词）
  ✎ <u>Assuming (that)</u> the man was making a homosexual advance, he stormed out of the house angrily. 他<u>以为</u>那人是在对他进行同性恋示好，便怒气冲冲地冲出了屋子。
  ✎ <u>Assuming (that)</u> the house is for sale, would you buy it? <u>假如</u>这房子要出售，你会买吗？
  ✎ You can stretch your legs on the spacious decks, play games, swim, meet interesting people and enjoy good food — always <u>assuming</u>, of course, <u>that</u> the sea is calm. <u>假定</u>（L44）
  **even assuming (that)……** = even if…… 即使；就算
  ✎ <u>Even assuming (that)</u> smokers do see the health warnings, I doubt they’ll take any notice. 即使吸烟者确实看到了健康警告，我也怀疑他们会注意到。
+ **settle down** 定居，安顿下来（L14）
  ✎ He had often dreamed of retiring in England and had planned to <u>settle down</u> in the country.（B2L38）
+ ┏ Hans settled down in a village fifty miles away <u>**where** he had remained ever since</u>.（原文-定语从句，相当于并列句）
  ┗ ……, Hans settled down in a village 50 miles away <u>**and** he had remained there ever since</u>.（there指前文in a village 50 miles away）（还原为并列句）

---

## **Lesson 37 - The Westhaven Express**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>We have learnt to expect that trains will be punctual. After years of conditioning, most of us have developed an unshakable faith in railway timetables. Ships may be delayed by storms; flights may be cancelled because of bad weather; but trains must be on time. Only an exceptionally heavy snowfall might temporarily dislocate railway services. It is all too easy to blame the railway authorities when something does go wrong. The truth is that when mistakes occur, they are more likely to be *ours* than *theirs*.

After consulting my railway timetable, I noted with satisfaction that there was an express train to Westhaven. It went direct from my local station and the journey lasted a mere hour and seventeen minutes. When I boarded the train, I could not help noticing that a great many local people got on as well. At the time, this did not strike me as odd. I reflected that there must be a great many people besides myself who wished to take advantage of this excellent service. Neither was I surprised when the train stopped at Widley, a tiny station a few miles along the line. Even a mighty express train can be held up by signals. But when the train dawdled at station after station, I began to wonder. It suddenly dawned on me that this express was not roaring down the line at ninety miles an hour, but barely chugging along at thirty. One hour and seventeen minutes passed and we had not even covered half the distance. I asked a passenger if this was the Westhaven Express, but he had not even heard of it. I determined to lodge a complaint as soon as we arrived. Two hours later, I was talking angrily to the station master at Westhaven. When he denied the train’s existence, I borrowed his copy of the timetable. There was a note of triumph in my voice when I told him that it was there in black and white. Glancing at it briefly, he told me to look again. A tiny asterisk conducted me to a footnote at the bottom of the page. It said: ‘This service has been suspended.’</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **express** n. 快车；快递；a. 快速的
  n.
  **<u>express/ express train</u>** 快车
  ✎ the 8.00 am <u>express</u> to Edinburgh 上午8点开往爱丁堡的快车
  ✎ the Beijing to Shanghai <u>express</u> 北京至上海的快车
  ✎ send goods by <u>express</u> 用快递的方式发送货物
  a.
  ✎ an <u>express</u> <u>train/ coach/ bus</u> 快速列车/长途汽车/公共汽车
  ✎ <u>express</u> delivery services 快递服务
  **expressway [美], freeway [美], motorway [英]** 高速公路
  ✎ On <u>motorways</u> you can, at least, travel fairly safely at high speeds,……（L44）
+ **condition** v. 训练，影响，使习惯或适应……；决定……
  + v.1.
    英文释义：to train or influence a person or animal mentally so that they do or expect a particular thing without thinking about it 训练，影响，使习惯或适应……
    ✎ People <u>are conditioned by</u> the society in which they live. 人们受到他们所生活的社会的影响。
    **condition sb. to do sth.** 训练/影响某人使其做某事
    ✎ Pavlov <u>conditioned</u> dogs <u>to</u> salivate at the sound of a bell. 巴甫洛夫训练狗一听到铃声就会流口水。（at the sound of…… 一听到某个声音就……（L23：at…… of）；saliva 口水，唾液）
    ✎ Many women <u>are conditioned</u> from birth <u>to</u> be accepting rather than questioning. 许多女性从出生起就受到外界的规训，即她们倾向接受而不是质疑。
  + v.2. determine 决定……
    ✎ Environment <u>conditions</u> an animal’s development. 环境决定动物的发育。
    ✎ What I buy <u>is conditioned by</u> the amount I earn. 我买什么取决于我挣多少钱。
  + conditioning n. 潜移默化的影响（其实就是动名词直接当作名词用）
    ✎ <u>Conditioning</u> starts as soon as boys are given guns to play with and girls are given dolls. 一旦男孩拿到枪玩，女孩拿到娃娃，潜移默化的影响就开始了。
    **Social conditioning** [U] 社会对人的潜移默化的影响
    ✎ <u>Social conditioning</u> makes crying more difficult for men. 社会对人的潜移默化的影响使哭泣对于男性更困难。
+ **exceptionally** ad. 例外地，反常地；极其
  ✎ <u>Exceptionally</u>, students may be accepted without formal qualifications. 在特殊情况下，也可能接受无正式文凭的学生。
  ✎ an <u>exceptionally</u> talented player 一位极具天赋的运动员
  ✎ The weather was <u>exceptionally</u> cold. 天气特别寒冷。
  **exceptional** a. 反常的，例外的；非凡的，杰出的
  + a. 反常的，例外的
    ✎ This is an <u>exceptional</u> case; I’ve never seen anything like it before. 这是一个特例；我以前从未见过这样的东西。
  + a. 非凡的，杰出的（L14）
    ✎ The child had shown <u>exceptional</u> courage. 这个孩子展现出了非凡的勇气。
    ✎ Her scores are quite <u>exceptional</u>. 她的成绩相当地突出。
    同义词：
    **extraordinary**（L1，L14）
    ✎ her <u>extraordinary</u> beauty 她非凡的美貌
    ✎ Nelson Mandela is a truly <u>extraordinary</u> man. 纳尔逊·曼德拉是一位真正了不起的人。
    **remarkable**
    ✎ a <u>remarkable</u> feat 一个非凡的功绩
    ✎ a <u>remarkable</u> achievement 一个非凡的成就
  + **exception** n. 例外的情况，个案
    ✎ We all laughed, **with the exception of** Maggie. 除了麦琪之外，我们都笑了。（L27）
    ✎ Each plant, **without exception**, contains some kind of salt. 每种植物都无一例外地含有某种盐。
    ✎ Tramps seem to be the only **exception to** this general rule. ……的例外情况（L27）
+ **dislocate** v. 打乱，扰乱；使脱臼（locate 定位）
  ✎ Flights have been <u>dislocated</u> by the fog. 航班因大雾而打乱。
  ✎ Only an <u>exceptionally</u> heavy snowfall might temporarily dislocate railway services.（本文）
  ✎ <u>dislocate</u> one’s <u>ankle/ wrist</u>…… 脚踝/手腕脱臼
  ✎ a <u>dislocated</u> finger 一个脱臼了的手指（过去分词用作形容词）
  **dislocation** n. 混乱；脱臼
  ✎ These policies could cause severe economic and social <u>dislocation</u>. 这些政策可能引起严重的经济和社会混乱。
  ✎ a <u>dislocation</u> of the shoulder 肩膀的脱臼
+ **blame** v. to say or think that sb. or sth. is responsible for sth. bad 责备（L31-reprimand）
  ✎ A bad workman <u>blames</u> his tools. 拙劣的工匠总是归罪于他的工具。拙匠埋怨工具差（不承认错在自己）。
  ┏ **blame <u>sb./ sth.</u> for sth.** 把某事归罪到某人身上（L31）
  ┗ **blame sth. on <u>sb./ sth.</u>**
  ┏ They <u>blamed</u> George <u>for</u> the failure. 他们因这次失败而指责乔治。
  ┗ They <u>blamed</u> the failure <u>on</u> George. 他们把这次失利归咎到了乔治身上。
  **<u>sb./ sth.</u> is to blame (for sth.)** (某事)都怨某人（主动形式表达被动含义）
  ✎ George <u>is to blame for</u> the failure.
  **<u>reprimand/ rebuke</u> sb. for sth.** （多用于上下级之间的责备）
  ✎ I was <u>reprimanded/ rebuked</u> by my manager <u>for</u> being late.
  ✎ Recognizing who the customer was, the manager was most apologetic and <u>reprimanded</u> the assistant severely.（L31）
  **accuse sb. of sth.** （情绪化地）指责/指控某人
  ✎ Dimitri immediately went to Aleko’s house and angrily <u>accused</u> him <u>of</u> stealing the lamb.（L16）
  **criticize sb. for sth.** 因为某事而批评某人
  ✎ He <u>was criticized for</u> his delay in dealing with the matter. 他由于没有及时处理这件事而受到批评。
  **censure sb. for sth.** 严厉地指责
  ✎ Ministers <u>were censured for</u> their lack of decisiveness during the crisis. 因为在危机期间不够果断，部长们受到了严厉的指责。
  **scold sb. for sth.** 因为某事指责某人（多用于长辈对晚辈）
  ✎ His mother <u>scolded</u> him <u>for</u> breaking her favorite vase. 因为他打碎了妈妈最心爱的花瓶，他的妈妈批评了他。
  **reproach sb. for sth.** 强调因为没有做该做的事而指责（偏文言）
  ✎ He <u>reproached</u> me <u>for</u> not answering his letter. 他因为我没有回他的信而指责我。
  **condemn A <u>for/ as</u> B** 因为B而谴责A / 把A谴责为是B（大家一致地批评）
  ✎ The movie <u>was condemned for</u> its sexism. 这部电影因为性别歧视而受到谴责。
  ✎ The terrorist attack <u>was condemned as</u> an act of barbarism and cowardice. 这次恐怖袭击被谴责为是野蛮和懦弱的行径。
+ **consult** v. 向……请教；查阅
  + v. 向……请教
    ✎ <u>consult</u> <u>an expert/ a doctor/ a lawyer/ ……</u> 向一位专家/医生/律师……请教
    ✎ If symptoms persist, <u>consult</u> a doctor without delay. 如果症状持续，请立即咨询医生。
  + v. 查阅 **= refer to**
  ✎ <u>consult/ refer to</u> a <u>timetable/ map/ dictionary……</u> 查阅时刻表/地图/字典
  ✎ After <u>consulting</u> my railway timetable, I noted with satisfaction that there was an express train to Westhaven.（本文）
  ✎ Bruce <u>consulted</u> the map once more and told us that the village was now only fifteen miles away.（L39）
  ┏ 查字典
  ┗ <u>consult/ refer to</u> a dictionary <u>for</u> the word（宾语是“字典”）
  ┗ <u>look up</u> the word <u>in</u> a dictionary（宾语是“单词”）
+ **direct** ad. 中途不停地；不经中间环节地（= directly）
  + ad.1. without stopping or changing direction = directly
    ✎ The train goes there <u>direct/ directly</u>. 这辆火车直达那里。
  + ad.2. with no one in between = directly
    ✎ He decided to contact the manager <u>direct/ directly</u>. 他决定直接跟经理联系。
  + 除以上两种意思外，都只能用directly，如用其修饰形容词、副词、动词时；如其表示其它含义时。
    ✎ He’s <u>directly (~~direct~~)</u> responsible to the boss. 他直接对老板负责。
    ✎ The new property tax law won’t <u>directly (~~direct~~)</u> affect us. 新的物业税法并不会直接影响到我们。
    ✎ It was a small house, <u>directly (~~direct~~)</u> behind the church. 这是一座小房子，它就在教堂的后面。（就在，正在）
    ✎ She left <u>directly (~~direct~~)</u> after the show. 她在表演结束后立刻就走了。（立即，立刻）
  + 不加ly和加ly的副词
    ┏ **deep** 具象的，可丈量的
    ┗ **deeply** 抽象的，比喻义的
    ✎ He pushed the stick <u>deep</u> into the mud. 他把棍子深深地插进泥里。
    ✎ He was <u>deeply</u> moved. 他被深深地打动了。
    ┏ **high**
    ┗ **highly**
    ✎ He climbed <u>high</u> up the mountain. 他爬上了高山。
    ✎ It is <u>highly</u> confidential. 这是高度机密的。
    ┏ **wide**
    ┗ **widely**
    ✎ Open your mouth <u>wide</u>. 把嘴张大。
    ✎ He seems to be <u>widely</u> known here. 他似乎在这里名气很大。
    ┏ **sharp**
    ┗ **sharply**
    ◇ 只能用sharp的情况 ↓
    ✎ We’re meeting at one-thirty <u>sharp (~~sharply~~)</u>. 准时地
    **turn sharp (~~sharply~~) <u>left/ right</u>** 急转弯
    ✎ You <u>turn sharp right</u> at the crossroads. 你在路口向右急转弯。
    ◇ 只能用sharply的情况 ↓
    ✎ Interest rates have fallen <u>sharply (~~sharp~~)</u> over the last few weeks. 在过去的几周内，利率急剧下降。
    ✎ The government has been <u>sharply (~~sharp~~)</u> criticized for human rights violations. 政府因侵犯人权而受到严厉批评。
+ **triumph** n.[C]&[U] 胜利，成功（的喜悦）；v. 获得成功，取胜
  + n.[C]&[U] 胜利，成功（的喜悦）
    ✎ one of the <u>triumphs</u> of modern science 现代科学的胜利之一
    **do sth. in triumph** 带着成功的喜悦
    ✎ The winning team returned home <u>in triumph</u>. 获胜的队伍凯旋归来。
    **a note of triumph** 得意洋洋的语气/态度
    ✎ There was <u>a note of triumph</u> in her voice. 她言谈中透着一丝得意。
    ✎ Arch of <u>Triumph</u> 凯旋门（法国）（L6）
  + v. 获得成功，取胜
    **triumph over……** 战胜/击败某人
    ✎ In the end, good shall <u>triumph over</u> evil. 最终，善一定会击败恶。
  + **triumphant** a. 得胜的，凯旋的
    ✎ a <u>triumphant</u> cheer 一个胜利的欢呼
  + **triumphantly** ad. 得胜地，胜利地
    ✎ Who has not stood in awe at the sight of a spider pouncing on a fly, or a column of ants <u>triumphantly</u> bearing home an enormous dead beetle?（L54）
+ **asterisk** n. 星号（*）
  字根 **astr/ aster = star**
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onomy 天文学
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onomical 天文学的；天文数字的
  ◇ <u>astr</u>ology 占星术
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onautics 航天学（nau = ship；cs 表示某种学问）
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onaut 宇航员
  ◇ dis<u>aster</u> 大灾难；灾星，扫把星（dis 表示不好的，有灾的）
  ◇ <u>aster</u>oid 小行星


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **faith**
  + 搭配形容词
    ◇ <u>great/ enormous/ tremendous</u> <u>faith</u> 巨大的/强烈的信心
    ◇ <u>absolute/ implicit</u> <u>faith</u> 绝对的信心
    ◇ <u>complete/ total</u> <u>faith</u> 完全的信心
    ◇ unshakeable <u>faith</u> 不可动摇的信心
    ◇ blind <u>faith</u> 盲目的信心
  + 搭配动词
    ◇ **develop faith in……** 对……渐渐产生了信心
    ◇ **have faith in……** 对……有信心
    ◇ **<u>put/ place</u> faith in……** 对……倾注信心
    ◇ **<u>shake/ undermine</u> faith in……** 动摇/削弱对……的信心
    ◇ **destroy faith in……** 摧毁对……的信心
    ◇ **lose faith in……** 丧失对……的信心
    ◇ **restore faith in……** 恢复对……的信心
+ **timetable [BrE], schedule [AmE]** 时间表，日程表，课程表，行程表
  ✎ <u>train/ railway[BrE]/ railroad[AmE]</u> ~ 列车时刻表
  ✎ <u>college/ school</u> ~ 大学/学校课程表
  ✎ <u>exam/ examination</u> ~ 考试日程
+ on time = punctual（原文同义替换）
+ **snowfall** n.[C]&[U] 降雪；降雪量
  ✎ <u>heavy/ light</u> <u>snowfall</u> 大/小雪
  ✎ <u>annual/ average</u> <u>snowfall</u> 年/平均降雪量
+ **temporary** a. 临时的
  ✎ A <u>temporary</u> rudder was made on board from spare planks and it was fitted with great difficulty.（L25）
+ **too…… to……**
  + 太……而不会……
    ✎ He was <u>too</u> excited <u>to</u> say a word. 他激动得说不出话来。
  + 做某事非常……，做某事求之不得（too + 以下4种形容词时）
    ① glad/ pleased…… 高兴的
    ② ready/ willing…… 愿意的，乐意的
    ③ easy/ apt…… 容易的
    ④ eager/ anxious…… 迫切的
    ✎ It is all <u>too</u> **easy** <u>to</u> blame the railway authorities when something does go wrong.（本文）
    ✎ I’m <u>too</u> **pleased** <u>to</u> help you. 我非常高兴帮助你。
    ✎ She is <u>too</u> **willing** <u>to</u> marry him. 她非常原意嫁给他。
    ✎ He’s <u>too</u> **eager** <u>to</u> pass the exam. 他非常迫切地想通过这门考试。
    + **(only/ all/ but) too…… to……** 做某事非常……（添加副词，以强化语气，不翻译）
      ✎ It is **all** <u>too</u> easy <u>to</u> blame the railway authorities when something does go wrong.（原文）
      ✎ I’m **only** <u>too</u> **pleased** <u>to</u> help you. 我非常乐意帮助你。
      ✎ They’re **but** <u>too</u> **glad** <u>to</u> do so. 他们非常高兴这么做。
      ✎ ……, and the doctor in charge of the department is **only** <u>too</u> **ready** <u>to</u> provide them with these requirements. 非常乐意……（B4L28）
+ **the authorities** [pl.] 政府，当局（L30）
  ✎ the local authorities 地方政府
  ✎ the Chinese authorities 中国政府
  ✎ Fearing <u>the authorities</u>, Eric remained in hiding after the war as well.（L30）
  ✎ When the fire had at last been put out, <u>the forest authorities</u> ordered several tons of a special type of grass-seed which would grow quickly.（B2L62）
+ **go wrong** 出错，出问题，不顺利（L33）
  ✎ We have all experienced days when everything <u>goes wrong</u>.（L33）
> 仿写第1段倒数第2句
  当问题和困难确实出现(arise)的时候，我们很容易放弃自己的梦想。
  It’s all too easy to give up our dreams when problems and difficulties do arise.
+ **more…… than……** 更……而非……
  有时可译为“与其说 (后者) 不如说 (前者)”，特别是more和than后跟同样词性或结构时。
  ✎ It is <u>more</u> a poem <u>than</u> a picture. 与其说这是一幅画不如说这是一首诗。
  ✎ He is <u>more</u> diligent <u>than</u> clever. 与其说他聪明，不如说他勤奋。
  ✎ The present crisis in capitalist countries is <u>more</u> a political <u>than</u> an economic crisis. 资本主义国家目前的危机与其说是经济危机，不如说是政治危机。
+ “with + 名词”往往相当于“此名词同根的副词”，前者更正式（L3，L11）
  ◇ with satisfaction = satisfiedly 满意地
  ◇ with ease = easily 容易地
  ◇ with delight = delightedly 高兴地
  ◇ with pride = proudly 骄傲地，自豪地
  ◇ with a smile = smilingly 微笑地
  ◇ with attention = attentively 专心地，专注地
  ◇ with confidence = confidently 自信地
  ◇ with reluctance = reluctantly 勉强地，不情愿地
+ **a mere……** 仅仅……；只有……（L34）
  a mere 后跟单数名词时 = **only <u>a/ an</u>**
  在其他情况下 a mere = **only**
  ✎ …… and the journey lasted <u>a mere (= only an)</u> hour and seventeen minutes.
  ✎ He’s <u>a mere (= only a)</u> child. 他只是个孩子。
  ✎ He’s not <u>a mere (= only a)</u> boxer: he’s world champion. 他不仅仅是个拳击手，他是世界冠军。
  ✎ <u>A mere ( = Only)</u> 2% of their budget has been spent on publicity. 他们仅仅有2%的预算用于宣传。
  ✎ He has often described to me how he picked up a masterpiece for <u>a mere (= only)</u> £50.（L34）
  ✎ Glancing at his map, he informed us that the next village was <u>a mere (= only)</u> twenty miles away.（L39）
+ **board = get on** 上（车、船、飞机）（原文同义替换）（L28）
  使用条件：该交通工具需够大，至少人能站得起来。
  + board
    ✎ <u>board</u> a <u>bus/ train/ ship/ plane</u>
    ✎ The couple <u>boarded</u> the train for New York. 这对夫妇登上了火车赴纽约。（及物）
    ✎ Flight No.714 for Paris is now <u>boarding</u> at Gate 8. 飞往巴黎的714号航班正在8号门登机。（不及物）
  + get on
    ┏ <u>get on</u> a <u>bus/ train/ ship/ plane</u>
    ┗ <u>get off</u> a <u>bus/ train/ ship/ plane</u>
    ✎ I had no sooner <u>got off</u> the ship than I was assailed by a man who wanted to sell me a diamond ring.（L28）
  + 小型交通工具：
    不加宾语
    ┏ **get in**
    ┗ **get out**
    加宾语
    ┏ **get into** a <u>car/ taxi</u>
    ┗ **get out of** a <u>car/ taxi</u>
  + 专指上船、飞机
    不加宾语
    ┏ **embark**
    ┗ **disembark**
    加宾语
    ┏ **embark on** a <u>ship/ plane</u>
    ┗ **disembark from** a <u>ship/ plane</u>
+ **can’t help (doing) sth. ……** 不禁/忍不住……（help 避免）
  ✎ I <u>couldn’t help</u> <u>thinking</u> about the past. 我不禁想起了过去。
  ✎ ‘Stop biting your nails.’‘I <u>can't help</u> <u>it</u>.’ 不要咬指甲。 我忍不住。
  **can’t help but do……** 忍不住而只能做……
  ✎ Her evidence was so convincing that I <u>could not help but</u> <u>agree</u> with her. 她的证据如此有说服力，以至于我忍不住同意她的观点。
  **sth. can’t be helped** 某事不能被避免
  ✎ I really don’t want to go this weekend, but <u>it</u> <u>can’t be helped</u>. 这个周末我真的不想走，但没办法。
  ✎ M: I don’t know how I managed to break that platter. I’ll be more than happy to buy you a new one.（more than 修饰形容词：极其 = extremely，~~比……多~~）
  W: Forget about it. <u>Some things</u> just <u>can’t be helped</u>. 算了吧。有些事情是不能被避免的。
  Q: What does the woman mean?
  Answer: She doesn’t want the man to replace the platter.（托福听力真题）
  **not if I can help it** 不想做某事，能不做就不做
  ✎ ‘Are you going to watch the school play?’ ‘<u>Not if I can help it</u>.’
  ✎ M: Will you be living in the dormitory this year?
  W: <u>Not if I can help it</u>. I’ve been thinking of renting an apartment off campus with some friends of mine.
  Q: What does the woman imply?
  Answer: She doesn’t want to live in university housing.（housing [U] 住处）（托福听力真题）（L6）
  **help oneself to sth.**
  ✎ One of the thieves was struck by a heavy statue, but he was too busy <u>helping himself to</u> <u>diamonds</u> to notice any pain.（L6）
+ ┏ At the time, this did not strike me as odd.（原文）
  ┗ At the time, I didn’t think this was odd.（太通俗）
+ **strike sb. as……** 给某人某种印象，某人感到，觉得……
  ✎ The idea <u>struck</u> me <u>as</u> stupid. 我觉得这个想法很愚蠢。/这个想法给我的印象是愚蠢的。
  ✎ The request <u>struck</u> me <u>as</u> comic. 我觉得这个请求非常可笑。
  ✎ He <u>struck</u> them <u>as</u> an honest man. 他们觉得他是一个诚实的人。/他给他们的印象是个诚实的人。
+ **reflect** v. 心想，考虑；反射(本义)
  **reflect on……** 心想……，考虑……
  ✎ I need time to <u>reflect (on</u> what to do). 我需要时间考虑（我该做什么）。
  **reflect that……** 心想……，考虑……
  ✎ She <u>reflected that</u> his argument was probably true. 她想他的论证可能是正确的。
  **take advantage of sth.** 利用某物
  ✎ I <u>took advantage of</u> the good weather to paint the shed. 我利用好天气粉刷了棚屋。
  ✎ Many schools don’t <u>take full advantage of</u> the Internet. 许多学校没有充分利用互联网。
  **take advantage of sb.** 利用某人，占某人的便宜（贬义）
  ✎ Don’t lend them the car — they’re <u>taking advantage of</u> you! 别把车借给他们，他们在占你便宜！

#### 👾 **部分倒装（复制自L5）**
+ **形式：只把助动词、be动词（之前没有其它助动词的情况下）或情态动词置于主语之前，中心谓语动词保持在主语后面不动。**
+ **目的：突出句首的状语。**
适用情况：
1. **否定词位于句首** （如本文）
（否定词举例：not only, not until, neither, nor, never, hardly, barely, scarcely, few, little, rarely, seldom, under no circumstances, in no way, ……）
  ✎ <u>Not only</u> **had** the poor man been arrested, but he had been sent to prison as well.（L5）
  ✎ <u>Nor</u> **is** the city without its moments of beauty.（L41）
  ✎ <u>Neither</u> **was** I surprised when the train stopped at Widley, a tiny station a few miles along the line.（本文）
  ✎ <u>Never</u> **have** I seen such a good movie. 我以前从来没有看过这么好看的电影。
  ✎ <u>Not until</u> yesterday **did** little John change his mind. 直到昨天小约翰才改变他的注意。
  ✎ <u>Under no circumstances</u> **should** you lend Paul any money. 你绝不要借给保罗一分钱。
2. **“only + 状语”位于句首**
意为：只有……才……；直到……才……
  ✎ <u>Only</u> <u>then</u> **did** he realize that he was mistaken. 直到那时，他才明白他错了。（副词作状语）
  ✎ <u>Only</u> <u>by working hard</u> **can** we succeed in doing anything. 只有通过努力工作，我们才能成功地完成任何事情。（介词短语作状语）
  ✎ <u>Only</u> <u>after a baby seal is pushed in to the sea by its mother</u> **will** it learn how to swim. 直到一直小海豹被它的妈妈推到大海里之后，它才能学会如何游泳。（状语从句）
  ✎ <u>Only</u> <u>when he saw that the man was actually telephoning the police</u> **did** he realize that they had all been the victims of a hoax.（状语从句）（L40）
3. **such, so, well, often, many a time 等表示程度、频率的副词位于句首**
  ✎ <u>Such</u> **is** human nature, that a great many people are often willing to sacrifice higher pay for the privilege of becoming white-collar workers.（L4）
  ✎ <u>So</u> great **is** our passion for doing things for ourselves, that we are becoming increasingly less dependent on specialized labour.（L46）
  ✎ <u>Well</u> **did** I know him and <u>well</u> **did** he know me. 我很了解他，他也很了解我。
  ✎ <u>Often</u> **did** it snow there. 那里经常下雨。
  ✎ <u>Many a time</u> **has** he given me good advice. 他经常给我一些好的建议。
+ 造句应用：
  ✎ 你不但吓了我一跳，而且可能把村子里所有人都吵醒了。
  **Not only** <u>did</u> you give me a surprise, **but** you’ve probably woken up everyone in the village **as well**.
  ✎ 不但有几个人抱怨说在夜里听见了“像猫一样的噪音”，而且一位钓鱼途中的商人还看见那只美洲狮在树上。
  **Not only** <u>did</u> several people complain of ‘cat-like noises’ at night, **but** a businessman on a fishing trip saw the puma up a tree **as well**.

+ **mighty**（书面语、正式语）
  + a.1. very strong and powerful
    ✎ a <u>mighty</u> warrior 一名强悍的的战士
    ✎ a <u>mighty</u> empire 一个强大的帝国
    ✎ With a <u>mighty</u> kick, he broke down the door. 他一脚猛踢，把门踢开了。
  + a.2. large and impressive
    ✎ <u>mighty</u> mountain peaks 雄伟的山峰
    ✎ <u>mighty</u> oak trees 高大的橡树
+ **hold <u>sb./ sth. 🗘 up</u>**: to delay sb. or sth. 延误/耽搁某人/某事
  ✎ Our flight <u>was held up</u> by fog. 我们的航班因大雾而延误。
  ✎ My application <u>was held up</u> by the postal strike. 我的申请因邮政罢工而被延误/耽搁。
  ✎ Road-works on the motorway are <u>holding up</u> traffic. 高速公路上的道路施工延误了路上的车辆。
+ **dawdle** v. to take a long time to do sth or go somewhere 磨蹭
  ✎ Stop <u>dawdling</u> and hurry up: we’re late. 别再磨蹭了，快点：我们迟到了。
  ✎ Eleanor will be back any moment, if she doesn’t <u>dawdle</u>. 如果埃莉诺不磨蹭的话，她随时都会回来的。
+ **sth. after sth.** 一个又一个地（固定搭配）
  ✎ day <u>after</u> day 一天又一天地
  ✎ week <u>after</u> week 一周又一周地
  ✎ year <u>after</u> year 一年又一年地
  ✎ time <u>after</u> time 一次又一次地
  ✎ He fired <u>shot after shot</u>. 他开了一枪又一枪。
  ✎ Shelley sent him <u>letter after letter</u> to explain the delay. 雪莉一封又一封地给他写信，解释延误的原因。
  ✎ They sent <u>regiment after regiment</u> to attack us. 他们派了一个又一个团来攻击我们。
  ✎ In <u>factory after factory</u> we were shown machines built by the workers themselves. 在一家又一家工厂里，我们看到了工人自己制造的机器。
+ **sth. dawn on sb.** 某人想到某事（物作主语）
  **= sth. occur to sb.**
  **= sth. strike sb.**
  **= sth. cross one’s mind**
  ✎ It <u>dawned on</u> me that Joanna had been right all along. 我意识到乔安娜一直都是对的。
  ✎ It suddenly <u>occurred to</u> one of the workers to open up the box.（B2L46）
  ✎ It suddenly <u>struck</u> me how we could improve the situation. 我一下子明白我们如何能改善局面了。
  ✎ It didn’t <u>cross her mind</u> that she might be doing something illegal. 她没有想到她可能在做违法的事情。
  **sb. realize that……** 某人明白/想到……（人作主语）
  **sb. become aware (of the fact) that……**
  **sb. wake up to the fact that……**
+ **roar down……** 沿着……呼啸而下（L6）
  ✎ The silence was suddenly broken when a large car, with its headlights on and its horn blaring, <u>roared down</u> the arcade.（L6）
+ **chug** v. if a car, train etc. chugs somewhere, it moves there slowly, with the engine making a repeated low sound (发动机缓慢运转时)发出突突声
  **chug <u>along/ down/ up etc.</u>** 吭哧吭哧前进/下来/上去(反方向)
  ✎ An old car <u>chugged down</u> the road. 一辆旧车在路上吭哧吭哧走了下来/前进。
+ **cover** v. travel (a certain distance) 行走（一段路程）（不强调交通方式）
  ✎ By sunset we had <u>covered</u> thirty miles. 到日落时分，我们已经走了三十英里的路程。
  ✎ A week before, he had completed a successful overland flight during which he <u>covered</u> twenty-six miles.（L20）
  ✎ The bird <u>covered</u> the distance in three minutes.（B2L9）
+ **听说，获悉**（L30）
  **learn <u>of/ about</u>**
  **know <u>of/ about</u>**
  **hear <u>of/ about</u>**
  后接that从句时，须删掉介词。that从句不用在介词后。
+ **<u>determine/ resolve</u> to do sth.** (fml.) 决意做某事（比 **decide to do** 更正式、坚决）
  ✎ After the divorce she <u>determined/ resolved</u> never <u>to</u> marry again. 离婚后，她决定再也不结婚了。
  **choose to do sth.** ① 选择去做某事；② 决定去做某事（表示出乎意料的决定）（L33）
  ✎ What invariably happens is that a great number of things <u>choose to</u> go wrong at precisely the same moment.（L33）
  ✎ She <u>chose to</u> ignore my advice. 她决定不理睬我的建议。
  ✎ More young couples are <u>choosing</u> not <u>to</u> marry. 更多的年轻伴侣决定不结婚。
+ **<u>lodge/ bring/ file</u>** a complaint 发起投诉
  **<u>get/ receive</u>** a complaint 收到投诉
  **<u>deal with/ handle</u>** a complaint 处理投诉
  **investigate** a complaint 调查投诉
  **resolve** a complaint 解决投诉
  **reject** a complaint 驳回投诉
+ **<u>stationmaster/ station master</u>**
  an official in charge of a railroad or bus station 火车站/汽车站站长
+ ┏ **deny + <u>sth./ doing/ that……</u>** 否认某事（L16）
  ┗ **<u>admit/ acknowledge</u> + <u>sth./ doing/ that……</u>** 承认某事
  ┏ He <u>denied</u> <u>the charge. knowing about it. that he had stolen the sheep.</u> 他否认这项指控。/他否认知道这个事情。/他否认他偷了这只羊。
  ┗ He <u>admitted/ acknowledged</u> <u>the charge./ knowing about it./ that he had stolen the sheep.</u>
  **deny <u>the existence of sth./ sth.’s existence</u>** 否认某物的存在（固定搭配）
  ✎ When he <u>denied the train’s existence</u>, I borrowed his copy of the timetable.（原文）
  ✎ Atheists <u>deny the existence of God</u>. 无神论者否认上帝的存在。（atheistm 无神论）
  ✎ Officials have repeatedly <u>denied the existence of a secret report</u>. 官员们反复地否认了秘密报告的存在。
+ **copy** 一张，一份，一本，~~复印件，拷贝~~
  ✎ But the <u>copy</u> he gave him had not been written out in full as usual.（L22）
+ **note** n. a way of speaking or writing that shows what someone’s feelings are 语言文字中带有某种感情
  **there <u>is/ was</u> a note of…… in……** （某人的语言/文字）中带有一种……的感情
  ✎ <u>There was a note of</u> triumph <u>in</u> my voice when I told him that it was there in black and white.（本文）
  ✎ <u>There was a note of</u> doubt <u>in</u> her voice. 她的语气里透着一丝怀疑。
  ✎ <u>There was a note of</u> self-satisfaction <u>in</u> his speech. 他的讲话中有一种自得的意味。
  ✎ <u>There was a note of</u> sadness <u>in</u> her letter. 她的信中流露着一丝悲伤。
+ **in black and white** ad. in writing or in print 白纸黑字（书写的或印刷的）
  ✎ I want the contract <u>in black and white</u>. 我要这份合同见诸文字。/我想要一份白纸黑字的合同。
  ┏ **black-and-white** 黑白的
  ✎ a <u>black-and-white</u> <u>photograph/ television/ printer</u> 黑白照片/电视/打印机
  ┗ **color** 彩色的
  ✎ a <u>color</u> <u>photograph/ television/ printer</u>
  **black and blue** 鼻青脸肿 **beat sb. black and blue** 打得某人鼻青脸肿
  **be in the black** 账户有盈余
  ✎ We’ve managed to stay <u>in the black</u> for over a year now. 我们已经设法保持盈利一年多了。
  **be in the red** 赤字/欠债状态
  ✎ This is the airline’s fourth straight year <u>in the red</u>. 这家航空公司已连续第四年出现亏损。（straight 连续）
+ **glance at……** 匆匆地看，浏览一遍（动词搭配）
  ✎ <u>Glancing at</u> it briefly, the dealer told him that it was worth £50.（L34）
  ✎ <u>Glancing at</u> his map, he informed us that the next village was a mere twenty miles away.（L39）
  **<u>take/ have/ shoot/ throw/ cast</u> a glance (at……)** 匆匆扫了一眼（名词搭配）
  ✎ The couple at the next table <u>cast quick glances</u> in our direction. 邻桌的那对夫妇匆匆朝我们的方向瞥了一眼。
  ✎ So I drove back to the town and began to retrace the route, <u>taking frequent glances at</u> the map.（L57）
+ **conduct sb. to……** 引导/指引/带领某人到某地
  ✎ I asked the attendant to <u>conduct</u> him <u>to</u> the door. 我让服务员领他到门口。
+ **footnote** n. a note at the bottom of the page in a book, which gives more information about something 脚注
+ **say** v. 上面写着……（L18）
  ✎ The sign <u>says</u> ‘Keep Out’. 标牌上写着“请勿入内”。
  ✎ What did the letter <u>say</u>? 信上说了什么？
  ✎ The first thing I saw when I entered the art gallery was a notice which <u>said</u>: ‘Do not touch the exhibits. Some of them are dangerous!’（L18）
+ **suspend** 悬，挂；临时中止；停职（详见L17）
  ✎ The ferry service has <u>been suspended</u> for the day because of bad weather. 由于天气不好，渡轮服务今天被暂停。
  ✎ The policeman <u>was suspended</u> while the complaint was investigated. 当投诉在被调查期间，这位警察被停职了。
  ✎ Dave <u>was suspended from</u> school for a week. 戴夫被学校停课一周。

---

## **Lesson 38 - The first calendar**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>Future historians will be in a unique position when they come to record the history of our own times. They will hardly know which facts to select from the great mass of evidence that steadily accumulates. What is more, they will not have to rely solely on the written word. Films, videos, CDs and CD-ROMs are just some of the bewildering amount of information they will have. They will be able, as it were, to see and hear us in action. But the historian attempting to reconstruct the distant past is always faced with a difficult task. He has to deduce what he can from the few scanty clues available. Even seemingly insignificant remains can shed interesting light on the history of early man.

Up to now, historians have assumed that calendars came into being with the advent of agriculture, for then man was faced with a real need to understand something about the seasons. Recent scientific evidence seems to indicate that this assumption is incorrect.

Historians have long been puzzled by dots, lines and symbols which have been engraved on walls, bones, and the ivory tusks of mammoths. The nomads who made these markings lived by hunting and fishing during the last Ice Age which began about 35,000 B.C. and ended about 10,000 B.C. By correlating markings made in various parts of the world, historians have been able to read this difficult code. They have found that it is connected with the passage of days and the phases of the moon. It is, in fact, a primitive type of calendar. It has long been known that the hunting scenes depicted on walls were not simply a form of artistic expression. They had a definite meaning, for they were as near as early man could get to writing. It is possible that there is a definite relation between these paintings and the markings that sometimes accompany them. It seems that man was making a real effort to understand the seasons 20,000 years earlier than has been supposed.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **calendar** n. 日历
  ◇ solar <u>calendar</u> 阳历
  ◇ lunar <u>calendar</u> 阴历
  ◇ Chinese <u>calendar</u> 农历（阴历的一种）
  ◇ perpetual <u>calendar</u> 万年历（**perpetual** a. 永久的）
  ◇ desk <u>calendar</u> 台历
  ◇ wall <u>calendar</u> 挂历
+ **unique** a. 唯一的，独一无二的
  ✎ a <u>unique</u> position 独一无二/得天独厚的地位
  ✎ Each person’s DNA is <u>unique</u>. 每个人的DNA都是独一无二的。（作表语）
  **be unique to……** 对……来说是独有的
  ✎ Fingerprints <u>are unique to</u> every individual. 指纹对每个人来说都是独一无二的。
  **be peculiar to……** 是……所独有的（L18）
  ✎ Pandas <u>are peculiar to</u> China. 大熊猫是中国特有的动物。
  **be confined to……** 仅仅局限在某地
  ✎ ……, for collectors <u>are</u> not <u>confined to</u> any one country.（L59）
  **be limited to……** 限制在……范围之内
  ✎ The air strikes <u>are limited to</u> military targets. 空袭仅限于军事目标。
  **be restricted to……** 限制在……范围之内（**restrict** vt. 限制）
  ✎ Access to the company files <u>is restricted to</u> management. 对公司文件的访问仅限于管理层。
+ **solely** ad. 唯一地
  **sole** a. 唯一的
  ✎ He is the <u>sole</u> survivor of the car accident. 他是车祸中唯一的幸存者。
  同义词：
  **only, single**
  ✎ …… to this day it has never written a <u>single</u> word!（L28）
  **lone, solitary**（更文言）
  ✎ Owen scored the <u>lone</u> goal of the match. 欧文打进了这场比赛的唯一一个进球。
  ✎ They had a <u>single</u> aim, a <u>solitary</u> goal, the top.（B4L3）
+ **bewilder** v. 令人眼花缭乱，晕头转向
  ✎ Big city traffic <u>bewildered</u> the country girl. 大城市的车水马龙让这个乡下女孩眼花缭乱。
  **bewildering** a. 令人晕头转向的，令人迷惑的（分词作形容词）
  （**ing形容词**，多表示“令人……样的”，形容事物的特征；**ed形容词**，通常表示人的感受）
  ✎ the <u>bewildering</u> amount of information（本文）
  **confuse** vt. (由于事物或选择太多而)令人迷惑
  ✎ They <u>confused</u> me with their conflicting advice. 他们那些相互矛盾的建议把我弄糊涂了。
  **confusing** a. 令人眼花缭乱的，令人晕头转向的
  ✎ Many tourists were <u>bewildered</u> by the city’s complicated traffic system.
  (A) degraded 使降级，使恶化；(B) bewildered；
  (C) evoked 唤起(某种感情)；(D) diverted 使拐弯（六级单选）
  ✎ As an increasing number of traffic regulation schemes are devised, the poor <u>bewildered</u> driver finds himself diverted and forced into one-way systems which cause even greater delays than the traffic jams they are supposed to prevent.
  随着/因为越来越多的交通规则的计划被设计出来，可怜的、被搞得晕头转向的司机发现自己必须不停地拐弯并被迫进入单行系统，这导致的延误甚至比他们应该防止的交通堵塞更大。（考研阅读真题节选）
  近义词：
  **puzzle, perplex, baffle** 使迷惑（强调事物本身难度大、复杂，而导致迷惑不解，不一定指事物很多）
  ✎ The murder case still <u>puzzled/ perplexed/ baffled</u> the police. 这起谋杀案依然令警方困惑。
  **puzzling, perplexing, baffling** a. 令人迷惑不解的（同样强调事物本身难度大、复杂，而令人迷惑）
+ **deduce** v. 推理，推断
  **deduce…… from……** 由 (后者) 推断出 (前者)
  ✎ I can <u>deduce</u> his motives <u>from</u> his behavior. 我可以从他的行为推断出他的动机。
  **deduction** n. 推理，得出的结论
  + 同义替换：
    **conclude…… from……**
    ✎ What do you <u>conclude from</u> the evidence? 从证据中，你能得出什么结论？
    **conclusion** n. 得出的结论；事情的结束
    **infer…… from……**
    ✎ What can we <u>infer from</u> the passage? 从文章我们可以推断出什么？
    **inference** n. 推理，推断；推论，结论
+ **scanty** a. 不足的，匮乏的
  ✎ <u>scanty</u> clues 匮乏的线索 ✎ <u>scanty</u> evidence 不足的证据
  + 同义替换：
    **scant, insufficient, inadequate**
    **scarce** a. 不足的；难以得到的（多指日用品）
    ✎ Food and clean water were becoming <u>scarce</u>. 食物和干净的水变得越来越匮乏。
  + 反义词：
    **sufficient, adequate**
  + 近义词：
  **rare** 稀罕的，罕见的 ✎ a <u>rare</u> <u>disease/ species</u> 罕见的疾病/物种
  **sparse** 稀疏的 ✎ a <u>sparse</u> population 稀疏的人口 ✎ <u>sparsely-populated</u> regions 人口稀少的地区

  **be deficient in……** （某种物质）匮乏的
  ✎ a diet <u>deficient in</u> vitamin C 一种缺乏维生素C的饮食
  **be few and far between**（某人某物）比较少见的（习语）
  ✎ People like John <u>are few and far between</u>. 像约翰这样的人很少。
  ✎ Thank God people like John <u>are few and far between</u>. 谢天谢地，像约翰这样的人真是少之又少。
+ **engrave** v. 雕刻（指二维雕刻，表层的花纹、图案）
  ✎ Historians have long been puzzled by dots, lines and symbols which have <u>been engraved</u> on walls, bones, and the ivory tusks of mammoths.（原文）
  **inscribe** 刻字（L28）
  ✎ At the base of the gold cap, the words ‘made in the U.S.A.’ had been neatly <u>inscribed</u>.（L28）
  **sculpt** v. 雕刻 **sculpture** n. [U]雕刻艺术；[C]雕塑品（指三维立体雕刻）（L18）
  **etch** 蚀刻
  **be <u>etched/ engraved</u> <u>on/ in</u> one’s memory** 某人永远不能忘记某事
  ✎ The scene will <u>be etched/ engraved on/ in my memory</u> forever. 这个情景我一辈子也不会忘记。
+ **correlate** v. 使相互联系（动态关联）
  ✎ Stress levels and heart disease **are strongly correlated**. 压力程度和心脏病密切相关。
  **relate** 使联系，使关联（静态关联）
  ✎ Cancer cases in the area **are directly related to** the new nuclear power station. 该地区的癌症病例与新的核电站直接相关。
  **correlation** n. 相互关联，相互关系
  ✎ **There’s a high correlation between** smoking **and** lung cancer. 吸烟和肺癌之间有很高的相关性。（固定句型）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **未来**
  ┏ **husband-to-be, fiancé** 未婚夫
  ┗ **bride-to-be, fiancée** 未婚妻
  **posterity** n.[U] 后代，子孙
  **do sth. for posterity**
  ✎ These works of art are preserved for <u>posterity</u>. 这些艺术品是为后代而保存下去的。
  **in the <u>near/ not-too-distant</u> future** 在不远的将来
  **in the foreseeable future** 在可预见的将来
  ┏ **in the long run** 从长远来看
  ┗ **in the short run** 从短期来看
  ✎ Taking this decision will cost us more <u>in the short run</u>, but will be beneficial <u>in the long run</u>. 做出这一决定在短期内会让我们付出更多的代价，但从长远来看是有益的。
  + **当代**
    ┏ 当代的历史学家
    ┗ <u>modern</u> historians
    ┗ <u>today’s</u> historians
    ┗ historians <u>of today</u>
    ┗ <u>contemporary</u> historians
+ **position**: situation 地位，状况，处境，~~位置~~
  ◇ She’s **in the enviable position** of being able to choose who she works with. 她处于一个令人羡慕的处境，可以选择和谁一起工作。
  ◇ When two of your best friends argue it **puts** you **in a very awkward position**. 当你最好的两个朋友吵架时，你会处于一个非常尴尬的境地。
  ◇ **in a delicate position** 处于微妙的境地
  ◇ **in a dominating position** 处于统治地位
  ◇ **in a favorable position** 处于有利地位
