  ◇ **in an adverse position** 处于不利地位
  ◇ **China’s world position** 中国的世界地位
+ **come to do sth.** ① 开始做某事；② 偶然地做某事；③ 逐渐地/慢慢地就……
  ✎ I’ve <u>come to</u> like her over the months. 经过几个月来，我已经开始喜欢她了。
  ✎ A body <u>came to</u> be found under the bridge. 有人无意中在桥下发现了一具尸体。
> 仿写
  在计算机的帮助下，当代的科学家在开始进行复杂运算的时候处于得天独厚的地位。
  With the assistance of computers, contemporary scientists are in a unique position when they come to make complicated calculations.

#### 👾 **“疑问词 + to do” 可以视为名词性从句的缩略形式**
1. 相当于宾语从句
  ↓ They will hardly know <u>which facts to select from……</u>（原文）
  ↳ They will hardly know <u>which facts they should select from……</u>
  ↓ I don’t know <u>what to do</u>. 我不知道该做什么。
  ↳ I don’t know <u>what I should do</u>.
  ↓ I haven’t decided <u>whether to sell it or not</u>. 我还没有决定是否卖掉它。
  ↳ I haven’t decided <u>whether I should sell it or not</u>.
  ↓ Have you settled <u>where to go</u>? 你决定要去哪里了吗？
  ↳ Have you settled <u>where you should go</u>?
2. 相当于主语从句
  ↓ <u>Who to turn to</u> is what she wants to know. 她想知道该向谁求助。
  ↳ <u>Who she should turn to</u> is what she wants to know.
3. 相当于表语从句
  ↓ The problem she faces is <u>which way to take</u>. 她面临的问题是该走哪条路。
  ↳ The problem she faces is <u>which way she should take</u>.
4. 相当于同位语从句
  ↓ The problem <u>which course to take</u> worried Lucy for hours. 选哪门课的问题让露西忧虑了好几个小时。
  ↳ The problem <u>which course she should take</u> worried Lucy for hours.

+ **mass**
  + a large quantity or number 大量
    ┏ **<u>a mass of…… / masses of……</u>** 大量的……（书面）
    ┗ **<u>a lot of…… / lots of……</u>**（口语）
    ✎ the great <u>mass of</u> evidence（本文）
    ✎ Traditional custom, taken the world over, is <u>a mass of detailed behavior</u> more astonishing than what any one person can ever evolve in individual actions, no matter how aberrant.（B4L44）
    ✎ This caused the construction of gigantic buildings where too <u>large masses of human beings</u> are crowded together.（B4L16）
    **the masses** 人民群众（固定短语）
    ✎ It is an entertainment that will appeal to <u>the masses</u>. 这是一种能吸引大众的娱乐活动。/这是一种人民群众喜闻乐见的娱乐形式。
  + a. 人数众多的，大规模的
    ✎ <u>mass</u> education 群众性的教育
    ✎ the problem of <u>mass</u> unemployment 大规模失业问题
    ✎ weapons of <u>mass</u> destruction 大规模杀伤性武器
    ✎ <u>mass</u> communication 大众传播
+ **ever-doing结构** a. 不断……的
  ✎ We have to ask ourselves very seriously what will happen if this two-fold use of knowledge with its <u>ever-increasing</u> power continues.
  ┏ evidence that steadily accumulates 稳定地/不断地积累（原文-定语从句）
  ┗ the **ever-accumulating** evidence（前置定语）
  ┏ the world that steadily changes 不断变化的世界
  ┗ the **ever-changing** world
  ┏ the knowledge that steadily grows 不断增长的知识
  ┗ the **ever-growing** knowledge
  ┏ the economy that steadily develops 不断发展的经济
  ┗ the **ever-developing** economy
  ┏ the market that steadily expands 不断扩张的市场
  ┗ the **ever-expanding** market
  ┏ the reform that steadily deepens 不断深化的改革
  ┗ the **ever-deepening** reform
  ┏ the resources that steadily dwindle 不断缩减的资源（**dwindle** vi.(fml.) 缩减，慢慢变少）
  ┗ the **ever-dwindling** resources
+ **<u>what is more/ what’s more</u>** 此外，而且，更好/糟的是（表递进）
  ✎ He could not find his fifty pence piece anywhere, and <u>what is more</u>, he could no get his arm out.（L15）
  同义替换：
  **furthermore, moreover, besides**
  **in addition, additionally**
  近义词：
  ┏ **better still** 更好的是（通常用于句首(加逗号)，句中则变为 still better）
  ┗ **worse still** 更糟的是
  ┗ **to make things worse**（尽管是动词不定式，但由于是习语，故可直接作副词短语使用）
  ┗ **to make matters worse**
  **stranger still** 更奇怪的是（通常用于句首(加逗号)）
✎ During these tests she was able to read a newspaper through an opaque screen and, <u>stranger still</u>, by moving her elbow over a child’s game of Lotto she was able to describe the figures and colours printed on it;…… 位于分句句首（B4L4）
+ **solely** ad. 仅仅 = only
  **sole** a. = only
+ **rely on……** 依赖，依靠，取决于……（L3，L29）
  同义替换（以下的on都可以换成upon）：
  **depend on……**
  **bank on……**
  **count on……** 指望……
  **hinge on……** （hinge 铰链，合叶）
  **rest on……** 搭在……上
  **build on……**
  **ride on……**
  **reliance on……** 对……的依赖（reliance n.）
+ **written** a. 书面的，~~被写出来的~~
  ✎ the <u>written</u> word = <u>written</u> language 书面语
  ✎ a <u>written</u> <u>agreement/ statement</u> 一个书面的协议/声明
  ✎ the <u>spoken</u> word = <u>spoken</u> language 口语
  **oral/ verbal** 口头的
  ✎ an <u>oral</u> exam 一项口试
  ✎ a <u>verbal</u> agreement 一个口头协议
+ **as it were** 可以说是，仿佛是，真可谓是（常作插入语）（虚拟语气）
  ✎ He is, <u>as it were</u>, a walking dictionary. 他真可谓是一部活字典。
  ✎ Reading is thought to be a kind of conversation between the reader and the text. The reader puts questions, <u>as it were</u>, to the text and gets answers. In the light of these he puts further questions, and so on.
  阅读被认为是类似于读者与文本之间的一种对话。读者好像是在向文本提问并得到答案。根据这些答案，他再提出更深入的问题，等等。（四级阅读真题）
  ✎ The Han nationality and the minority nationalities are all, <u>as it were</u>, members of the same family. 汉族和少数民族真可以说是一家人一样。
  同义替换：
  **so to speak**
  ✎ He is, <u>so to speak</u>, a walking dictionary.
  ✎ The Han nationality and the minority nationalities are all, <u>so to speak</u>, members of the same family.
  辨：
  **as it is** 看样子，照目前情况来看（真实语气）
  ✎ I thought things would get better, but <u>as it is</u> they are getting worse. 我原以为事情会好转，但照目前情况来看它们正在恶化。
+ **in action** ① 在做事情，在行动中（字面义）；② 在战斗中牺牲/负伤（搭配义）
  ✎ His father told everybody that Eric had been killed <u>in action</u>. 在战斗中牺牲（L30）
+ the historian
  the + 单数名词：既可表示特指，也可表示类指。本文上文没有出现某一位特定的历史学家，所以不是特指。
+ **reconstruct** 使恢复原状
  ✎ When the archaeologists <u>reconstructed</u> the fragments, they were amazed to find that the goddess turned out to be a very modern-looking woman.（L3）
  同义表达：
  **piece together** 拼起来
  ✎ From this the captain was able to <u>piece together</u> all the information that had come to light.（L32）
  ✎ But the historian attempting to <u>piece together</u> the distant past……（原文换用）
  **be faced with……** 面临（某个棘手的问题）
  ✎ …… for then man <u>was faced with</u> a real need to understand something about the seasons.（本文）
  ✎ They were expecting their sixth child and <u>were faced with</u> even more pressing economic problems.（L45）
  ✎ After buying a new chain I <u>was faced with</u> the insurmountable task of putting the confusing jigsaw puzzle together again.（L46）
  **= be confronted with……**
  ✎ But if the animals <u>are confronted with</u> situations they have no control over, they later behave passively when <u>faced with</u> experiences they can control.（六级真题阅读节选-邻近替换）
+ available
  able、ible结尾的形容词，位置灵活，既可以放在名词之前，也可以放在名词之后。当名词前有其他的形容词（尤其是最高级）修饰时，此类形容词通常后置。
  ✎ the most democratic form of ‘college’ <u>imaginable</u>（B4L33）
  ✎ the most civilized society <u>conceivable</u> 可以想象到的最文明的社会
  ✎ the most talented person <u>available</u> 能找到的最有才华的人
  ✎ the farthest star <u>visible</u> 能看得到的最远的星星
+ **seemingly** ad. 表面上（暗示其实不是这样）
  ✎ We often read in novels how a <u>seemingly</u> respectable person or family has some terrible secret which has been concealed from strangers for years.（L24）
+ **<u>shed/ throw/ cast</u> light on sth.** 揭示……
  ✎ Figuring out how humans acquire language may <u>shed light on</u> why some children learn to read and write later than others. 弄清楚人类是如何习得语言的，可能会揭示出为什么有些孩子学习读书和写字比其他孩子晚。（六级听力真题）
  ✎ Groundbreaking research by two French geophysicists promises to <u>shed some light on</u> the mystery. 两位法国地球物理学家的突破性研究有望揭开这一谜团。（六级阅读真题）
  + 更多视觉原理搭配：
    **come to light** 被发现，被了解（L32）
    ✎ From this the captain was able to piece together all the information that had <u>come to light</u>.（L32）
    **colourful** 多姿多彩的，引人注目的
    ✎ One of the most <u>colourful</u> figures in boxing history was Daniel Mendoza, who was born in 1764.（L21）
    **pale in comparison with** 相形见绌，小巫见大巫（贬义）（**pale** vi. 变苍白；a. 苍白的）
    ✎ The devastating floods of two years ago <u>pale in comparison with</u> last week’s storms. 与上周的风暴相比，两年前的毁灭性洪水相形见绌。
+ **assume** v. 假定（贬义，通常指没有证据，暗示是错的、不合理的）
+ **come into being** 开始存在/产生
  + **being** ① 作系动词：是……；② 作普通动词：存在，活着（L1）
    ✎ alien <u>being</u> 外星生物 ✎ intelligent <u>being</u> 智慧生物
    ✎ To <u>be</u>, or not to <u>be</u>: that is the question. 生存还是死亡，这是一个问题。活着（《哈姆雷特》）
    ✎ I think therefore I <u>am</u>. 我思故我在。存在（笛卡尔）
  + 同结构搭配（L29）：
    **come into fashion** 开始流行
    **come into use** 开始得到使用
    **come into effect** 开始生效
    **come into blossom** 开花
+ **the advent of <u>sth./ sb.</u>** 重大人物/事件的到来（advent n. 到来，耶稣降临节）
  ✎ <u>The advent of</u> the steam engine heralded the beginning of a new era. 蒸汽机的出现宣告了一个新时代的开始。（herald vt. 宣告）
  ✎ With <u>the advent of</u> the new chairman, the company began to prosper. 随着新主席的到来，公司开始繁荣起来。
  + with the <u>advent</u> of……（本文）
    同义替换：
    with the <u>coming/ arrival</u> of……
    with the <u>birth</u> of……
    with the <u>genesis</u> of……（genesis 起源；《圣经(旧约)》的开篇《创世记》）
  + 随着……的……（L22）
    ✎ <u>with</u> the coming of spring 随着春天的到来
    ✎ <u>with</u> the approach of Christmas 随着圣诞节的临近
    ✎ <u>with</u> the outbreak of war 随着战争的爆发
    ✎ <u>with</u> the progress of science 随着科学的进步
    【✘】<u>with</u> the evidence began to accumulate（began是谓语动词，所在的句子是个从句，而从句需要连词衔接）
    【✔】<u>As</u> the evidence began to accumulate, experts from the zoo felt obliged to investigate,……（L1，评价：as是连词，也表示“随着”）
+ **indicate** 表明，表示（强调用语言、文字之外的方式）（L28）
  ✎ I shook my head and held up five fingers <u>indicating</u> that I was willing to pay £5.（L28）
+ **be puzzled by……** 对……感到很迷惑
  **= be perplexed by……**
  **= be baffled by……**
+ **long** ad. 长久以来
  ✎ Doctors **have long been puzzled by** the rare skin condition. 医生们长久以来对这种罕见的皮肤病感到很困惑。
  ✎ **It has long been known that** the hunting scenes depicted on walls were not simply a form of artistic expression. 人们长期以来就知道（本文）
  ✎ **It has long been believed that** cats have nine lives. 人们长期以来都相信猫有九条命。
  ✎ **There has long been a superstition** among mariners **that** porpoises will save drowning men by pushing them to the surface, or protect them from sharks by surrounding them in defensive formation.（B4L18）
> 仿写
  中国人长久以来迷信看见喜鹊会有好运气。
  <u>There has long been a superstition</u> among the Chinese <u>that</u> seeing a magpie <u>will bring you good luck./ is a good omen./ is an auspicious omen.</u>

+ **ivory** n.[U] 象牙；a. 象牙制的
  **ivory tusks** 象牙（tusk n.[C] 动物的长牙或獠牙）
  **ivory tower** 象牙塔
  英文释义：a place or situation where you are separated from the difficulties of ordinary life and so are unable to understand them, used especially to describe a college or university
+ **live by doing sth.** 靠某种职业为生（固定搭配）（L27）
  ✎ It has been said that everyone <u>lives by</u> selling something.（L27）
+ **age** 时代，时期（L3）
  ✎ the <u>Ice/ Stone</u> <u>Age</u> 冰川/石器时代
  ✎ the modern <u>age</u> 当代
  ✎ the computer <u>age</u> 计算机时代
  **times** 时代，时期
  ✎ Roman <u>times</u> 罗马时代（L3）
  ✎ in <u>modern/ recent/ ancient/ prehistoric</u> times 在当代/近代/古代/史前时代
  **era/ epoch** 时代，时期
  ✎ the steam-engine <u>era/ epoch</u> 蒸汽时代
  ┏ **the end of an <u>era/ epoch</u>** 某个时代的结束
  ✎ His death <u>marked the end of an era</u>.
  ┗ **the beginning of a new <u>era/ epoch</u>** 某个时代的开始
  ✎ The foundation of the People’s Republic of China <u>marked</u> the beginning of a new historical period in China. 中华人民共和国的成立标志着在中国新的历史阶段的开始。
+ ┏ **B.C./ BC** Before Christ（L3）
  ┗ **A.D./ AD** Anno Domini
> 仿写第3段第2句
  传说中道教的创始人老子，生活在大约公元前6世纪至公元前5世纪春秋时代的晚期，靠掌管国家图书馆为生。
  Laozi, legendary founder of Daoism, lived by taking charge of the royal library during the late Spring and Autumn Period which began about 600 B.C. and ended about 500 B.C.
+ **in various parts of the world** 在世界各地（固定搭配）
  ✎ Cooked in wine, snails are a great luxury <u>in various parts of the world</u>.（L23）
+ **the phases of the moon** 月象
  **wax and wane** 月亮的圆缺（固定搭配）
  **ebb and flow** 潮水的涨落
  **up and down** 人生的起落/沉浮
  **to and fro** 来来回回地
  **on and off** 断断续续地
  ✎ 人有悲欢离合 With joy and woe people meet and part/
  月有阴晴圆缺 With light and shade the moon waxes and wanes/
  此事古难全 Since time immemorial it’s been unchanged（time immemorial 远古时代）/
  但愿人长久 Would that we could live a long life/
  千里共婵娟 And together share the moonlight though thousands of miles apart
+ **depict** vt.1. 描绘，描画；2. 描写(= describe)
  ✎ a picture <u>depicting</u> him as a clown 一幅把他描绘成小丑的画
  ✎ The novel <u>depicts</u> French society in the 1930s. 这部小说描写的是20世纪30年代的法国社会。
+ **definite** a. 明确的，确切的
  ✎ a <u>definite</u> meaning 一个确切的含义
  ✎ a <u>definite</u> answer 一个明确的回答
  ✎ <u>definite</u> article 定冠词
  **indefinite** a. 不明确的，无期限的
  ✎ <u>indefinite</u> article 不定冠词
  ✎ an <u>indefinite</u> prison term 无期徒刑
  + 易混词：
    **definitive** a. 最终的，最好的
    ✎ a <u>definitive</u> judgment 终审裁决
    ✎ a <u>definitive</u> diagnosis 最终诊断
    ✎ a <u>definitive</u> guide book 一本最好的导游书
    ┏ **finite** a. 有限的，有边界的
    ✎ Human knowledge is <u>finite</u>.
    ┗ **infinite** a. 无限的，没有边界的
    ✎ The universe is <u>infinite</u>.
    **infinitive** n. 动词不定式
+ **get to doing sth. = start doing sth.** 开始做某事（to 是介词）
✎ He <u>got to thinking</u> that it was all his fault. 他开始认为这都是他自己的错。
+ **accompany** vt. 陪伴，伴随
  ✎ Having left the bag in the hall, I <u>accompanied</u> Robert into the living room.（主动）（L23-课后题）
  ✎ The disease <u>is accompanied by</u> sneezing and fever. 这种疾病常伴有打喷嚏和发烧的症状。（被动）
  ✎ Chinese President Xi Jinping, <u>accompanied by</u> his wife Peng Liyuan, is undertaking a state visit to the United Sates. 中国国家主席习近平携夫人彭丽媛正在对美国进行国事访问。
+ **make an effort to do sth.** 努力去做某事
  **spare no effort to do sth.** 不遗余力去做某事
  ✎ China will <u>spare no effort to</u> realize peaceful reunification. 中国将不遗余力地实现和平统一。
+ …… than (what) has been supposed.
  than + 宾语从句时，后者主语往往是what，通常可省略（详见L29）
  ✎ To compensate for his unpleasant experiences in hospital, the man drank a little more <u>than was good for him</u>.（L29）

---

## **Lesson 39 - Nothing to worry about**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>The rough road across the plain soon became so bad that we tried to get Bruce to drive back to the village we had come from. Even though the road was littered with boulders and pitted with holes, Bruce was not in the least perturbed. Glancing at his map, he informed us that the next village was a mere twenty miles away. It was not that Bruce always underestimated difficulties. He simply had no sense of danger at all. No matter what the conditions were, he believed that a car should be driven as fast as it could possibly go.

As we bumped over the dusty track, we swerved to avoid large boulders. The wheels scooped up stones which hammered ominously under the car. We felt sure that sooner or later a stone would rip a hole in our petrol tank or damage the engine. Because of this, we kept looking back, wondering if we were leaving a trail of oil and petrol behind us.

What a relief it was when the boulders suddenly disappeared, giving way to a stretch of plain where the only obstacles were clumps of bushes. But there was worse to come. Just ahead of us there was a huge fissure. In response to renewed pleadings, Bruce stopped. Though we all got out to examine the fissure, he remained in the car. We informed him that the fissure extended for fifty yards and was two feet wide and four feet deep. Even this had no effect. Bruce went into a low gear and drove at a terrifying speed, keeping the front wheels astride the crack as he followed its zigzag course. Before we had time to worry about what might happen, we were back on the plain again. Bruce consulted the map once more and told us that the village was now only fifteen miles away. Our next obstacle was a shallow pool of water about half a mile across. Bruce charged at it, but in the middle, the car came to a grinding halt. A yellow light on the dashboard flashed angrily and Bruce cheerfully announced that there was no oil in the engine!</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ 各种石头
  **boulder** n.（风化的）大圆石头
  **stone** 石头，石块（可手握，可投掷）
  **rock** 岩石（英：大块岩石；美：类似于stone，可投掷）
  **pebble** 卵石
  **fossil** 化石
+ **perturb** v. 使不安（类似于L1的**disturb**，但更文气）
  ✎ The letter shocked and <u>disturbed/ perturbed</u> me. 这封信使我震惊和不安。
  ✎ It is <u>disturbing/ perturbing</u> to think that a dangerous wild animal is still at large in the quiet countryside. 令人不安的（L1）
  ✎ Ministers declared themselves profoundly <u>disturbed/ perturbed</u> by the violence. 部长们声称他们对暴行深感不安。
  + 字根 **turb = stir** 搅拌
    **dis<u>turb</u>**（dis 由中间向四面散开）
    **per<u>turb</u>**（per 彻底地）
    **<u>turb</u>ine** n. 涡轮机
    **<u>turb</u>id** a. 浑浊的 （id 形容词字根） ✎ <u>turbid</u> water 浑水
    **<u>turb</u>ulent** a. 汹涌的；动荡不安的（ulent 多……的） ✎ <u>turbulent</u> waves 汹涌的波浪
    ✎ the <u>turbulent</u> times of the French Revolution 法国大革命的动荡时期
+ ┏ **underestimate** v. 低估（**estimate** 估计）
  ┗ **overestimate** 高估
  ✎ Never <u>underestimate</u> the power of the press. 不要低估新闻报道的力量。
  ✎ He tends to <u>overestimate</u> his own abilities. 他往往会高估自己的能力。
  同近义词：
  ┏ **underrate** 对……评价过低
  ┗ **overrate** 对……评价过高
  ✎ As an actor, he is seriously <u>underrated</u>. 作为一名演员，他被严重低估了。
  ✎ In my opinion, she is a hugely <u>overrated</u> singer. 在我看来，她是一个被高估的歌手。
  ┏ **understate** 对……轻描淡写（**state** 说明，声明）
  ┗ **overstate** 对……过分夸张
  ✎ It would be a mistake to <u>understate</u> the seriousness of the problem. 如果对该问题的严重性轻描淡写，那恐怕是错误的。
  ✎ He may have <u>overstated</u> his ability in the interview. 在面试期间，他可能对自己的能力过分夸大了。
  ┏ **underplay** 贬低
  ┗ **overplay** 过分强调
  ✎ She <u>underplays</u> her achievements. 她贬低了自己的成就。
  ✎ You must not <u>overplay</u> his part in the negotiations. 你绝不要过分强调他在谈判中的作用。
+ **swerve = turn = veer** v. 突然转向（L10）
  ✎ As we bumped over the dusty track, we <u>swerved</u> to avoid large boulders.（本文）
  ✎ The lorry <u>swerved</u> sharply to avoid the child. 卡车为了躲避孩子来了个急转弯。
  ✎ He <u>swerved</u> suddenly, narrowly missing a cyclist. 他突然拐弯，勉强躲过了一个骑车的人。
  ✎ After the alarm had been given, the great ship <u>turned</u> sharply to avoid a direct collision.（L10）
  ✎ Moments before crashing, the jet was seen <u>veering</u> sharply to the right. 在坠毁前的时刻，人们看到这架喷气式飞机突然向右转向。
  **change course** 改变航向（专指船或飞机）
  ✎ The plane <u>changed course</u> to avoid the storm. 这架飞机改变了方向以躲避暴风雨。
  **unswerving** a. 坚定不移的
  ✎ <u>unswerving</u> <u>loyalty/ belief/ support……</u> 坚定的忠诚/信仰/支持……
+ **ominously** ad. 不吉利地，不祥地
  ✎ I went into the kitchen and found him lying <u>ominously</u> still on the floor. 我走进了厨房，发现他不祥地躺在地板上。
  **ominous** a. 不吉利的，有凶兆的
  ✎ There was an **ominous silence** at the other end of the phone. 电话那头出现了不祥的沉默。
  **omen** n. 兆头
  ✎ a <u>good/ bad</u> <u>omen</u> 吉兆/凶兆
  ✎ He was convinced that seeing the black cat was a <u>bad omen</u>. 他确信看到黑猫是个不祥之兆。
  ┏ **auspicious** a. 吉利的
  ✎ It was an **auspicious date** for a wedding. 这是一个举行婚礼的吉日。
  ✎ They won their first match of the season which was an **auspicious <u>start/ beginning</u>**. 他们赢得了本赛季的第一场比赛，这是一个吉利的开始。
  ┗ **inauspicious** a. 不吉利的
  ✎ He made an **inauspicious start** to his career by breaking a leg in his first race. 他在第一场比赛中摔断了一条腿，这是他的职业生涯不吉的开端。
  ✎ There has long been a superstition among the Chinese that seeing a magpie is an **auspicious omen**. 中国人长久以来迷信看见喜鹊是个吉利的兆头。
  ✎ There has long been a superstition among the Chinese that hearing the crowing of a crow is an **ominous omen**. 中国人长久以来迷信听见乌鸦是个不吉利的兆头。
+ **rip** v. 撕破，扯破（**≈ tear**）
  ✎ I <u>ripped</u> my jeans on the fence. 我的牛仔裤在栅栏上撕破了。
  ✎ The flags had **been ripped in two**. 旗帜都被撕成了两半。
  ✎ The nail **ripped a hole** in my jacket. 钉子在我的夹克上撕了个洞。
  ✎ She **ripped** the letter **open**. 她撕开了那封信。
  ✎ Be careful with that dress; it <u>rips</u> easily. 小心那件裙子；它很容易撕破。
  同义替换：
  **tear** (tore torn tearing)
  ✎ She realized she had <u>torn</u> her jacket on a nail. 她意识到一颗钉子把自己的夹克衫撕破了。
  ✎ I **tore a hole** in my jeans. 我在牛仔裤上扯了一个洞。
  ✎ He **tore** the letter **in two**. 他把信撕成了两半。
  ✎ I **tore open** the package. 我撕开了包裹。
  ✎ Careful, the fabric <u>tears</u> very easily. 小心，这种织物很容易撕破。
  近义词：
  **split** (split split splitting) 裂开，分裂
  ✎ One of the boxes had **split open**. 一个箱子已经裂开了。
  ✎ Her dress had <u>split</u> along the seam. 她的连衣裙顺着接缝裂开了。
  ✎ Don’t tell me you’ve <u>split</u> another pair of pants! 别告诉我你又扯破了一条裤子！
+ 英 | 美 | 译 
  ---- | ---- | ---- 
  petrol | gasoline/ gas | 汽油
  petrol tank | gas tank | 油箱
  <u>petrol/ service</u> station | gas station | 加油站

  **petroleum** 石油；**crude oil** 原油
  OPEC: Organization of Petroleum Exporting Countries 石油出口国组织
+ **obstacle** n. （道路上的）障碍物
  ✎ The area was full of streams and bogs and other natural <u>obstacles</u>. 此地遍布小溪、沼泽和其他天然障碍。
  **obstacle to……** 通向……的障碍
  ✎ <u>obstacles to</u> world peace 世界和平的障碍
  ✎ The tax **puts obstacles in the way of** companies trying to develop trade overseas. 这项税阻碍了试图发展海外贸易的公司。
  **block** n. 阻塞物
  ✎ a <u>block</u> in the <u>pipe/ drain</u> 水管/下水道里的一个阻塞物
  **block to……** 通往……的障碍
  ✎ The government’s stubborn attitude was a <u>block to</u> further talks. 政府固执的态度是进一步谈判的障碍。
  **hindrance to……** 通向……的障碍（**hinder** v. 阻碍）
  ✎ The higher interest rates have been a <u>hindrance to</u> economic recovery. 更高的利率是经济复苏的障碍。
  ✎ To be honest, she was **more of a hindrance than a help**. 说实在的，她不但没帮上忙，反而是个累赘。
  **barrier** n. 路障
  ✎ The crowd had to stand behind <u>barriers</u>. 人群不得不站在路障后面。
  ✎ the **language barrier** 语言障碍
  **barrier to……** 通往……的障碍
  ✎ Lack of confidence is a psychological <u>barrier to</u> success. 缺乏信心是通往成功的心理障碍。
  **impediment** （身体上的）障碍，残障
  ✎ a **speech impediment** 言语障碍（如口吃、大舌头）
  **impediment to……** 通往……的障碍
  ✎ War is one of the greatest <u>impediments to</u> human progress. 战争是人类进步的最大障碍之一。
+ **renew** v. 更新，换新；继续；延期
  ✎ <u>renew</u> the water in the goldfish bowl 给金鱼缸换水
  ✎ The window frames need to <u>be renewed</u>. 窗框需要换新的了。
  ✎ We <u>renewed</u> our journey the next day. 第二天我们继续旅行。
  ✎ I need to <u>renew</u> my passport this year. 我今年需要延期我的护照。
  **renewed** a. happening again with increased interest or strength [only before noun] 更强烈的……
  ✎ <u>renewed</u> <u>determination/ enthusiasm</u> 更坚定的决心/更强烈的热情
  ✎ <u>Renewed</u> fighting has been reported on the border. 据报道，边境爆发了更激烈的战斗。
  ✎ In response to <u>renewed</u> pleadings, Bruce stopped.（本文）
+ **pleading** n. 恳求；a. 恳求的
  n.
  an act of asking for sth. that you want very much, in an emotional way
  ✎ He simply ignored my <u>pleading</u>. 他干脆不理会我的恳求。
  ✎ <u>pleading</u> eyes 恳求的双眼
  ✎ a <u>pleading</u> tone of voice 一种恳求的语气
  **plead** v.
  + ① vi. 恳求，请求
    **plead for……** 恳求得到某物
    ✎ Civil rights groups <u>pleaded for</u> government help. 人权组织恳求得到政府的帮助。
    ✎ He was on his knees, <u>pleading for</u> forgiveness. 他跪在地上，恳求得到原谅。
    **plead with sb. to do sth.** 恳求某人去做某事
    ✎ Moira <u>pleaded with</u> him <u>to</u> stay. 莫伊拉恳求他留下来。
    ✎ She <u>pleaded with</u> him not <u>to</u> leave her alone. 她恳求他不要丢下她一个人。
  + ② vt. 以某事作为借口
    ✎ <u>plead</u> <u>ignorance/ illness/ a headache/ tiredness/ insanity</u> 以无知/得病/头疼/疲劳/精神失常为借口
    ✎ Ellie <u>pleaded</u> <u>tiredness</u> and went to bed very early. 艾莉以疲倦为借口，很早就上床睡觉了。
    ✎ She stayed home from work, <u>pleading</u> <u>illness</u>. 她因病待在家里没去上班。
    ✎ No one can <u>plead</u> <u>ignorance</u> of a subject any longer, for there are countless do-it-yourself publications.（L46）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **get sb. to do** 说服某人去做某事
  ✎ He <u>got</u> his sister <u>to</u> help him with his homework. 他说服他姐姐帮他做家庭作业。
  ✎ We couldn’t <u>get</u> him <u>to</u> sign the agreement. 我们无法说服他签署协议。
  同义搭配：
  **persuade sb. <u>to do/ into doing</u>**（后者更正式）
  ✎ I finally managed to <u>persuade</u> her <u>to</u> go out for a drink with me. 我终于说服她和我出去喝一杯。
  ✎ Don’t let yourself <u>be persuaded into</u> buying things you don’t want. 不要让自己被说服去买你不想要的东西。
  ✎ In their efforts to <u>persuade</u> us <u>to</u> buy this or that product, advertisers have made a close study of human nature and have classified all our little weaknesses.
  **talk sb. into doing**
  ✎ We finally <u>talked</u> Father <u>into</u> buying the new car. 我们终于说服爸爸买下了这辆新车。（Father 表示称谓，可单独使用，无须加冠词或属格，但首字母必须大写）
  反义搭配：
  **get sb. not to do** 劝阻某人不让其做某事
  **persuade sb. <u>not to do</u>/ <u>out of doing</u>**
  **talk sb. out of doing**
  **dissuade sb. from doing**
+ **满**
  **be littered with……** 杂乱地堆满了某物
  ✎ The garden <u>was</u> soon <u>littered with</u> chunks of metal which had once made up a lawn mower.（L46）
  **litter** vt. 杂乱地布满某地
  ✎ There is always hope that in its labyrinth of musty, dark, disordered rooms a real rarity will be found amongst the piles of assorted junk that <u>litter</u> the floors.（L34）
  **be pitted with……** 满是坑洞
  ✎ The road <u>was pitted with</u> holes.（本文）
  ✎ His face <u>is pitted with</u> smallpox. 他的脸布满因天花而留下的麻坑。
  **be <u>dotted/ scattered</u> with……** 散乱地分布着……
  ✎ The sky <u>is ~ with</u> stars. 天上繁星点点。
  ✎ The lawn <u>is ~ with</u> pine trees. 草坪上散乱地分布着一些松树。
  **be covered with……** 盖满了某物（L28）
  ✎ Before she had anchored, the men from the boats had climbed on board and the decks <u>were</u> soon <u>covered with</u> colourful rugs from Persia, silks from India, copper coffee pots, and beautiful handmade silverware.（L28）
  **be loaded with……**（交通工具）满载着……
  ✎ Small boats <u>loaded with</u> wares sped to the great liner as she was entering the harbour.（L28）
  **be filled with……** 装满了某物/某种情绪
  ✎ …… it <u>is filled with</u> what looks like a thick, greyish substance.（L52）
  ✎ All at once, I noticed that my wife seemed to <u>be filled with</u> alarm.（L48）
  **be <u>packed/ crammed</u> with……** 挤满了某物
  ✎ The streets <u>were packed/ crammed with</u> Christmas shoppers. 街上挤满了圣诞购物者。
  ✎ It has been estimated that if the bridge <u>were packed with</u> cars, it would still only be carrying a third of its total capacity.（L17）
  **be stuffed with……** （内部/中间）填满了……
  ✎ a pillow <u>stuffed with</u> feathers 一个羽毛枕头
  ✎ duck <u>stuffed with</u> ‘eight treasures’ 八宝鸭
  ✎ <u>stuffed</u> birds 鸟标本（L59）
  ✎ I’m <u>stuffed</u>. = I’m full. 我吃饱了。
+ **一点也不/绝不**（复习L17）
  置于句首时，须部分倒装。
  ~ | ~
  ---- | ----
  **by no means** | **not by any means**
  **not at all** | **in no way**
  **be no……** | **not remotely**
  **on no account** | **not on any account**
  **not a bit** | **not in the least**
  **on no condition** | **under no circumstances**
  
  ✎ Though Verrazano is <u>by no means</u> considered to be a great explorer, his name will probably remain immortal, for on November 21st, 1964, the longest suspension bridge in the world was named after him.
  ✎ She is <u>by no means</u> pretty. 她一点也不好看。
  ✎ She’s <u>not</u> a bad kid, <u>by any means</u>. 她绝对不是一个坏孩子。
  ✎ <u>By no means **can**</u> theory be separated from practice. 理论绝对不能与实践相分离。
  ✎ She’s <u>not at all</u> happy about the current situation. 她对目前的情况非常不高兴。
  ✎ This will <u>in no way</u> influence our original decision. 这绝对不会影响我们最初的决定。
  ✎ I <u>am no</u> expert. 我绝对不是个专家。
  ✎ That girl <u>is no</u> fool. 那个女孩一点也不傻。
  ✎ Larry <u>is no</u> friend of mine. 拉瑞绝对不是我的朋友。
  ✎ His arguments are <u>not remotely</u> convincing. 他的这些论断一点也没有说服力。
  ✎ <u>On no account **must**</u> you disturb me when I'm working. 在我工作的时候你绝对不要打扰我。
  ✎ Do <u>not on any account</u> leave the prisoner unguarded. 绝对不要让囚犯处于无人看管的状态。
  ✎ I tried to convince them, but they were<u>n’t in the least</u> interested. 我试图说服他们，但是他们一点也没有兴趣。
  ✎ ‘Was she annoyed?’ ‘<u>Not a bit</u>! She was delighted.’ “她是不是有点不高兴？”“一点也没有，她非常开心。”
  ✎ <u>On no condition **should**</u> untrained personnel use the equipment. 绝不能让没有受过训练的人使用这个设备。
  ✎ <u>Under no circumstances **will**</u> we agree to splitting up the company. 在任何情况下，我们都不会同意去分裂我们的公司。
  辨：
  **not a little = more than a little = very** 特别地，非常地
  ✎ Graham was <u>not a little/ more than a little</u> frightened by what he had seen. 格雷厄姆对他所看到的景象大为恐惧。
+ **perturbed = disturbed = worried** 担忧的
+ **glance at……** 匆匆地看，扫视一眼（L37）
+ ┏ **inform sb. <u>of/ about</u> sth.** 通知某人某事
  ┗ **inform sb. that……**（从句形式）
  ┏ **convince sb. of sth……** 使某人相信某事
  ┗ **convince sb. that……**（从句形式）
+ **a mere……** 仅仅……（L37）
  ① a mere 后跟单数名词时 = **only <u>a/ an</u>**
  ② 在其他情况下 a mere = **only**
  ✎ Glancing at his map, he informed us that the next village was <u>a mere (= only)</u> twenty miles away.（本文）
  ✎ It went direct from my local station and the journey lasted <u>a mere (= only an)</u> hour and seventeen minutes.（L37）
+ **It <u>is/ was</u> not that……, but (that)……** 不是因为……，而是因为……（固定句型）
  ┏ It was not that Bruce always underestimated difficulties. He simply had no sense of danger at all.（原文）
  ┗ <u>It was not that</u> Bruce always underestimated difficulties, <u>but (that)</u> he simply had no sense of danger at all.（合并为一句）
  ✎ <u>It was not that</u> I actually remembered anything at all. <u>But</u> my father had described over and over again what we should see at every milestone, after leaving the nearest town, so that I was positive I should recognize it as familiar territory.（L57-第1句的句号可改成逗号，并为一句）
  ✎ <u>It is not that</u> the scales in the one case, and the balance in the other, differ in the principles of their construction or manner of working; <u>but that</u> the latter is a much finer apparatus and of course much more accurate in its measurement than the former.
  这并不是因为在第一种情况中磅秤和在另一种情况中的天平在结构原理或工作方式上有什么不一样；而是因为后者是一种更精密的设备，当然其测量精度也比前者高得多。（考研英语英译汉）
  **not that……, but that……**（简化版-前提是前后结构一致，且为了对仗工整that不能去掉）
  ✎ <u>Not that</u> I love Caesar less, <u>but that</u> I love Rome more. 不是我不爱凯撒，而是我更爱罗马。/ 不是因为我爱凯撒爱得更少，而是因为我爱罗马爱得更多。（Shakespeare ‘Julius Caesar’）
  ✎ <u>Not that</u> I love you less, <u>but that</u> I love liberty more. 不是我不爱你，而是我更爱自由。/ 不是因为爱你爱得更少，而是因为爱自由爱得更多。
  ✎ <u>Not that</u> I love my teacher less, <u>but that</u> I love truth more. 吾爱吾师，吾更爱真理。
+ **simply** ad. used to emphasize what you are saying （用以加强语气）简直，实在，根本，就是
  ✎ He <u>simply</u> had no sense of danger at all.（本文）
  ✎ His pronunciation is <u>simply</u> terrible. 他的发音简直太糟糕了。
  ✎ That is <u>simply</u> not true! 这根本就不是真的！
  ✎ I <u>simply</u> refuse to go! 我就是不想去！
  ✎ He <u>simply</u> won’t accept the committee’s decision. 他就是不愿接受委员会的决定。
+ ┏ <u>No matter what</u> the conditions were,……（原文）
  ┗ <u>Whatever</u> the conditions were,……
+ **possibly 经常与can/ could连用以表示“尽全力”的意思，**
  **后跟动词时，结构为：<u>can/ could</u> possibly + 动词；**
  **后省略动词时，结构为：possibly <u>can/ could</u>。**
  ✎ No matter what the conditions were, he believed that a car should <u>be driven</u> as fast as it <u>**could possibly** go</u>.（本文-前后动词不一样，无法省略）
  ✎ She’s <u>done</u> everything she <u>**could possibly** think of</u> to help. 她为了帮忙，已经做了一切她能想到的事情。
  ✎ We shall be <u>contributing</u> as much as we <u>**possibly can**</u> to the campaign. 我们应该尽我们所能为这场运动做出贡献。（省略了动词contribute）
  ✎ Doctors <u>did</u> everything they <u>possibly could</u> to save his life. 医生们为挽救他的生命，竭尽了全力。（省略了动词do）
> 仿写第1段末句
  无论在任何情况下，雷锋都认为一个人应该尽可能地为社会做出贡献。
  No matter what the conditions were, Lei Feng believed that a person should <u>contribute</u> as much as he <u>possibly could</u> to society.（前后动词一致，进行省略）
  无论在任何情况下，雷锋都认为一个人应该为社会做出他能想到的尽可能多的贡献。
  No matter what the conditions were, Lei Feng believed that a person should <u>make</u> as many contributions as he <u>could possibly think of</u> to society.（前后动词不一致，无法进行省略）
+ **bump** v. 碰撞；（拟声词）碰
  ✎ Be careful not to <u>bump</u> your head. 小心别撞到头。（vt.）
  ✎ In the dark I <u>bumped into</u> a chair. 在黑暗中，我撞到了一把椅子上。（vi.）
  ✎ The car <u>bumped against</u> the curb. 汽车撞到了路边。（vi.）
  **bump <u>over/ across/ along/ down……</u>** 颠簸前进
  ✎ As we <u>bumped over</u> the dusty track, we swerved to avoid large boulders.（本文）
  ✎ A police car <u>bumped down</u> the track. 一辆警车沿着这条小路颠簸地驶了过来。
  ✎ The old bus <u>bumped along</u> the mountain road. 旧公共汽车沿着山路颠簸行驶。
  ✎ The airplane <u>bumped across</u> a field before finally coming to a stop. 飞机颠簸着穿过了一片田野，最后停了下来。
+ **track** n. a narrow path or road with a rough uneven surface, esp. one made by vehicles, people or animals
+ **scoop**
  + n. a tool with a deep bowl-shaped end which is used to dig out and move a soft or powdery substance
    ✎ a measuring <u>scoop</u> 量勺
    ✎ an ice-cream <u>scoop</u> 冰淇淋勺
    ✎ a <u>scoop</u> of ice-cream 一勺冰淇淋（作量词）
  + vt. 
    **scoop (up/ out) sth.** 舀出/抱起某物
    ✎ He <u>scooped</u> water from the stream and splashed it on his face. 他从溪边捧水，泼在脸上洗。
    ✎ She bent down and <u>scooped up</u> the little dog. 她弯下腰，抱起了小狗。
    ✎ Carefully <u>scoop out</u> the pulp with a small spoon. 用小勺子小心地舀出果肉。
+ **hammer/ thunder** v. 重击（名词动用）
  ✎ He <u>hammered/ thundered</u> at the door. 他用力捶门。
  名词动用举例：
  ✎ It immediately ran away when she saw it, and experts confirmed that a puma will not attack a human being unless it is <u>cornered</u>. （角落 → 把某人逼入绝境）（L1）
  ✎ He <u>elbowed</u> his way through the crowd. 他挤过人群。（胳膊肘 → 用肘推，用肘挤）
  ✎ I am <u>fogged</u> by the issue. 我被这个问题弄迷糊了。（雾 → 使迷糊）
  ✎ The lady <u>housed</u> the homeless. 这位女士收容那些无家可归的人。（房子 → 住在房子里）
+ **sooner or later** 迟早，早晚有一天
  ✎ You should tell her, because she’ll find out <u>sooner or later</u>. 你应该告诉她，因为她迟早会发现的。
+ **<u>rip/ tear</u> a hole**
+ **leave a trail of…… behind……**
  ✎ The hurricane <u>left a trail of</u> destruction <u>behind</u> it. 飓风在身后留下了一串的废墟。
  ✎ The bus <u>left a trail of</u> black smoke <u>behind</u> it. 公共汽车在后面留下了一道黑烟。
  ✎ He <u>left a trail of</u> muddy footprints <u>behind</u> him. 他在身后留下了一串泥泞的脚印。
  ✎ Wherever it went, it <u>left</u> <u>behind</u> it <u>a trail of</u> dead deer and small animals like rabbits.（L1-为句式平衡而改变了语序）
+ **relief** n. 宽慰，痛苦的缓解或解脱
  ✎ find a temporary <u>relief</u> 找到了暂时的解脱
  ✎ permanent <u>relief</u> 永久的解脱
  ✎ to my great <u>relief</u> 使我大为宽心的是
  ✎ give immediate <u>relief</u> from pain 立刻缓解疼痛
+ **give way to sth.**
  1. 被（更新或更好的事物）代替
    ✎ Steam trains <u>gave way to</u> electric trains. 蒸汽火车被电力火车所代替。
    ✎ Winter <u>gave way to</u> spring. 冬去春来。
    ✎ The storm <u>gave way to</u> bright sunshine. 暴风雨被明媚的阳光代替。
  2. **give way to <u>sb./ sth.</u>** 2. 为……让路，向……屈服
  ✎ Drivers must <u>give way to</u> cyclists. 司机必须向骑自行车的让路。
  ✎ <u>Give way to</u> traffic coming from the right. 给从右边来的车辆让路。
  ✎ We must not <u>give way to</u> their demands. 我们决不应向他们的要求屈服。
+ **stretch** n. an area of land or water, esp. one that is long and narrow （狭长的）一片或一段地或水域
  **stretch of……** 一片……
  ✎ a <u>stretch of</u> plain 一片平原
  ✎ a narrow <u>stretch of</u> water 一片狭长的水域
  ✎ a beautiful <u>stretch of</u> countryside 一片美丽的田园风光
  ✎ a particularly dangerous <u>stretch of</u> road 一段特别危险的路
+ **clump** n. a group of trees, bushes, or other plants growing very close together 丛
  **a clump of** trees/ bushes/ flowers/ grass 树丛/灌木丛/花丛/草丛
+ **worse** n.[U] something worse 更糟的东西
  ◇ I’m afraid **there is worse to come**. 我担心更糟的还在后面。
  ◇ We thought the situation was bad, but **worse was to follow**. 我们原以为情况已经够糟了，但是更糟的还在后面。
  ◇ ‘What about the bride’s dress —— wasn’t it appalling?’‘I don’t know, **I’ve seen worse**.’
  “你看新娘的裙子——是不是太糟糕了？” “我不知道，我见过更糟糕的。”
+ **fissure** n. long deep crack in rock or in the earth（岩石中或土地中的）深长裂缝
+ **in response to……** 作为对……的反应/回应（to 是介词）（L18）
  ✎ The president stepped down <u>in response to</u> public pressure. 总统迫于公众压力辞职。
  ✎ Oddly shaped forms that are suspended from the ceiling and move <u>in response to</u> a gust of wind are quite familiar to everybody.（L18）
+ **renewed** a. happening again with increased interest or strength [only before noun] 更强烈的……
+ + 进出内部站不起来的交通工具
    ┏ **get out** ✎ <u>get out of</u> a <u>car/ taxi</u>（不加宾语时，用get out，out为副词；加宾语时，用get out of，of是介词）
    ┗ **get in** ✎ <u>get into</u> a <u>car/ taxi</u>（不加宾语时，用get in，in为副词；加宾语时，用get into，into是介词）
  + 进出内部能够站得起来的交通工具
    ┏ **get on** ✎ <u>get on</u> a <u>bus/ train/ ship/ plane</u>（不加宾语时，on为副词；加宾语时，on为介词）
    ┗ **get off** ✎ <u>get off</u> a <u>bus/ train/ ship/ plane</u>（off同上）
+ **extend** v. （时间或空间）延伸
  ✎ The Sahara Desert <u>extends</u> <u>for</u> miles. 撒哈拉沙漠绵延数英里。
  ✎ The show has been <u>extended</u> <u>for</u> another six weeks. 演出又延长了六周。
  ✎ My garden <u>extends</u> <u>as far as</u> the river. 我的花园一直延伸到河边。
  ✎ The driveway <u>extends</u> <u>from</u> the house <u>to</u> the high way. 车道从房子一直延伸到高速公路。
  ✎ An industrial zone <u>extends</u> <u>along</u> the river. 一个工业区沿河延伸。
+ **gear** 挡位
  ┏ automatic <u>gear</u> 自动挡
  ┗ manual <u>gear</u> 手动挡
  ✎ an automatic <u>gearbox</u> 自动变速箱
  ✎ a four-speed manual <u>gearbox</u> 四档手动变速箱
  ◇ Andy drove cautiously along **in** third **gear**. 安迪挂着三档小心翼翼地开着车。（along ad. 向前，~~沿着~~）
  ◇ Helen **changed <u>gear[英]/ gears[美]</u>** as she approached the intersection. 海伦在接近十字路口时换了档。
  **<u>go/ move/ shift</u> into…… gear** 换到了……档
  ✎ I <u>went/ moved/ shifted into</u> fourth <u>gear</u> when I got onto the highway. 当我驶入高速公路，我换到了第四档。
  **<u>put/ slam/ slip</u> sth. into…… gear** （车子）换档
  ✎ I <u>put/ slammed/ slipped</u> the car <u>into</u> fourth <u>gear</u> when I got onto the highway. 当我驶入高速公路，我切换到了第四档。
+ **speed** 以……的速度（L6，L9，L25）
  1. speed做不可数名词时，与at, with搭配均可
    ✎ <u>at/ with</u> great speed 以非常快的速度
  2. speed做可数名词时，只能与at搭配
    ✎ <u>at</u> a speed of 60 mph 以时速60英里
+ **astride** prep. with one leg on each side of sth. 跨在……上
  ✎ a photograph of my mother sitting <u>astride</u> a horse 一张我妈妈骑在马上的照片
  ✎ She sat proudly <u>astride</u> her new motorbike. 她自豪地骑在她的新摩托车上。
  ✎ The town lies <u>astride</u> a river. 这座城镇位于河的两岸。/ 这座城镇横跨一条河。
+ **zigzag** a. a pattern that looks like a line of z’s joined together “之”字形的线条（z’s 复数）
  ✎ a <u>zigzag</u> path along the cliff 沿着悬崖的“之”字形小路
+ **course** n. 方向，走向，航线
+ **consult = refer to** 查阅
+ **once more = one more time**
+ **a <u>shallow</u> pool of water** 一池浅水
  【✘】a pool of shallow water
  名词前面有量词时，如果量词需形容词修饰，则形容词要放在量词之前（L15）
  ✎ a <u>nice</u> cup of tea 一杯好茶
  ✎ a <u>beautiful</u> stretch of field 一片美丽的原野
  ✎ a <u>stagnant</u> pool of water 一潭死水
  ✎ For most of them, 50 pence is a small price to pay for a <u>nice big</u> bar of chocolate.（L15）
+ half a mile **across** 半英里宽
  two feet **wide** 2英尺宽（同义替换）（本文）
+ **charge at……** 朝……猛冲
  ✎ Suddenly the bear <u>charged at</u> us. 突然，熊向我们猛冲过来。
  ✎ He <u>charged at</u> me with his fists flying. 他挥舞着拳头向我冲来。
+ **come to a <u>stop/ halt/ standstill</u>** （汽车、马等）停，停了下来（L6）
  ✎ It <u>came to a stop</u> outside the jeweler’s.（L6）
  **come to <u>an end/ a close</u>** （电影、会议等）结束
  **come to a <u>decision/ conclusion/ agreement</u>** 做出决定/得出结论/达成一致
+ **grind** 摩擦声
  ✎ come to a <u>grinding</u> halt 吱扭一声停下来/急刹车（本文）
+ dashboard n.（汽车上的）仪表板
+ **flash angrily** 刺眼的光芒
  ✎ Sparks were emitted from small black boxes and red lamps <u>flashed</u> on and off <u>angrily</u>.（L18）

---

## **Lesson 40 - Who’s who**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>It has never been explained why university students seem to enjoy practical jokes more than anyone else. Students specialize in a particular type of practical joke: the hoax. Inviting the fire brigade to put out a nonexistent fire is a crude form of deception which no self-respecting student would ever indulge in. Students often create amusing situations which are funny to everyone except the victims.

When a student recently saw two workmen using a pneumatic drill outside his university, he immediately telephoned the police and informed them that two students dressed up as workmen were tearing up the road with a pneumatic drill. As soon as he had hung up, he went over to the workmen and told them that if a policeman ordered them to go away, they were not to take him seriously. He added that a student had dressed up as a policeman and was playing all sorts of silly jokes on people. Both the police and the workmen were grateful to the student for this piece of advance information.

The student hid in an archway nearby where he could watch and hear everything that went on. Sure enough, a policeman arrived on the scene and politely asked the workmen to go away. When he received a very rude reply from one of the workmen, he threatened to remove them by force. The workmen told him to do as he pleased and the policeman telephoned for help. Shortly afterwards, four more policemen arrived and remonstrated with the workmen. As the men refused to stop working, the police attempted to seize the pneumatic drill. The workmen struggled fiercely and one of them lost his temper. He threatened to call the police. At this, the police pointed out ironically that this would hardly be necessary as the men were already under arrest. Pretending to speak seriously, one of the workmen asked if he might make a telephone call before being taken to the station. Permission was granted and a policeman accompanied him to a pay phone. Only when he saw that the man was actually telephoning the police did he realize that they had all been the victims of a hoax.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **hoax** n. 恶作剧（骗人相信某事）
  英文释义：a kind of <u>practical joke (恶作剧)</u> in which someone makes people believe something that is not true
  相关搭配：
  **play a <u>joke/ trick</u> on sb.** 对某人恶作剧（L22）
  **make a fool of sb.** 捉弄某人，故意让某人出丑
  **cheat sb. out of sth.** 骗走某人的某物
  ✎ He <u>cheated</u> the old lady <u>out of</u> her fortune. 他骗走了老太太的一大笔钱。
  **<u>trick/ deceive</u> sb. into doing sth.** 欺骗某人去做某事
  ✎ I <u>was tricked/ deceived into</u> believing his story. 我受骗相信了他的故事。
+ **indulge**
  + vi. 沉迷于……(略贬义)；尽情享受……(中性)
    **indulge in……**
    ✎ <u>indulge in</u> bad habits 沉迷于坏习惯
    ✎ I <u>indulged in</u> <u>a hot bath/ an expensive dinner</u> after a day’s hard work. 在努力工作了一天之后，我尽情享受了一次热水澡/一顿奢侈的大餐。
  + vt. 宠爱，娇惯
    **<u>indulge/ spoil/ pamper</u> sb.**
    ✎ I don’t agree with <u>indulging</u> children. 我不同意宠孩子。
    ✎ a <u>spoilt/ pampered</u> child 一个被宠坏了的孩子（过去分词作形容词）
  + 同根词
    **indulgent** a. 放纵的；**self-indulgent** a. 自我放纵的
    **indulgence** n. 放纵；**self-indulgence** n. 自我放纵
+ **advance** a. 提前的（定语，~~表语~~）
  ✎ <u>advance</u> party 先遣队
  ✎ <u>advance</u> <u>notice/ warning/ planning</u> 提前的通知/警告/规划
  ✎ <u>advance</u> payment 预付款
  ✎ publisher: What a job! Good work, Richard!
  photographer Richard: I’m so glad you like them so much.
  p: Like them? They represent your best work.（represent 代表（L3））
  R: Really?
  p: Absolutely.
  R: Well…… what do you think? Do I have my book?
  p: You do. You do. There’s a book here. I’ll have a contract and an <u>advance payment</u> waiting for you, first thing in the morning.（《走遍美国》）
  **in advance** 提前/预先（做某事）（作时间状语）
  ✎ Rent must be paid one month <u>in advance</u>. 租金必须提前一个月支付。
  **in advance of……** 在……前面/之前（多指时间）
  ✎ Galileo’s ideas were <u>in advance of</u> the age in which he lived. 伽利略的思想超前于他所生活的那个时代。
  **advanced** a. 高级的，先进的
  ✎ <u>advanced</u> technology 先进的技术
  ✎ an <u>elementary/ intermediate/ advanced</u> English course 一个初级/中级/高级的英语课程
  ✎ <u>elementary/ intermediate/ advanced</u> English learners 初级/中级/高级英语学习者
+ **remonstrate** vi. 抗议，规劝，告诫
  **remonstrate with sb.** (fml.) 向某人抗议
  ✎ The coach angrily <u>remonstrated with</u> the referee. 教练愤怒地向裁判表示抗议。
  ✎ Shortly afterwards, four more policemen arrived and <u>remonstrated with</u> the workmen.（本文）
  形近词：
  **demonstrate** v. 展示，表明
  相关表达：
  **protest against……** 聚众抗议……
  **complain (to sb.) <u>of/ about</u> sth.** （向某人）抱怨/投诉某事
  ✎ Several people <u>complained of</u> ‘cat-like noises’ at night and a businessman on a fishing trip saw the puma up a tree.（L1）
  ✎ Almost immediately he began to <u>complain about</u> the weather, for even though it was still summer, it rained continually and it was often bitterly cold.（B2L38）
  **nag sb. to do……** 唠叨某人让其做某事
  ✎ When my wife <u>nagged</u> me <u>to</u> do something about it, I told her that either I would have to buy a new mower or let the grass grow.（L46）
  **pester sb. to do……** 纠缠某人让其做某事
  ✎ From the moment he arrived there, he kept on <u>pestering</u> his doctor <u>to</u> tell him when he would be able to go home.（L29）
+ **ironically, sarcastically** ad. 讽刺地，讥讽地（指人时，可替换，形容词、名词同理）（L11）
  ✎ At this, the police pointed out <u>ironically</u> that this would hardly be necessary as the men were already under arrest.（本文）
  ✎ ‘Perfume, eh?’ he asked <u>sarcastically</u>. ‘You should have declared that. Perfume is not exempt from import duty.’（L11）
  **ironic, sarcastic** a. 讽刺的，讥讽的
  ✎ I was almost there when a <u>sarcastic</u> voice below said, ‘I don’t think the windows need cleaning at this time of the night.’（B2L92）
  **irony, sarcasm** n. 讽刺，讥讽
  **with heavy irony/ sarcasm** 伴随着深深的讽刺
  ✎ ‘Good of you to arrive on time,’ George said, <u>with heavy irony/ sarcasm</u>. “你到得真准时呀，”乔治说，话语里带着强烈的讽刺。
  **<u>hint/ trace/ touch</u> of <u>irony/ sarcasm</u>** 讽刺的味道/语气/成分
  ✎ There was <u>a hint of irony/ sarcasm</u> in her voice. 她的话语里透着一丝讽刺。
  **sarcasm 和 irony在形容人（话语、动作、表情等）的时候，含义相同，可互换；但在形容某件事时，则仅能用irony。**
  ✎ the <u>irony</u> of fate 命运的讽刺
  ✎ It’s <u>ironic</u> that she became a teacher —— she used to hate school. 她成为了老师这件事是挺讽刺的——她以前蛮狠学校的。
  ✎ <u>Ironically</u>, his cold got better on the last day of his holiday. 讽刺的是，他的感冒到假日最后一天的时候好了。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **who’s who** 谁是谁（名字、职务等）（习语）
  ✎ You’ll soon get to know <u>who’s who</u> in the company. 你很快就会知道公司里谁是谁了。
  ✎ 《who’s who 2015》2015名人录
  类似结构的搭配：
  **which is which** 谁是谁，哪个是哪个
  ✎ The twins are so alike that I can’t tell <u>which is which</u>. 这对双胞胎长得太像了，我分不清谁是谁。
  ✎ When Scarlet returned to the farm, the old maidservant began to tell her <u>who married whom, who had what children</u> and so on.
  斯嘉丽回到农场后，老女仆开始告诉她谁嫁给了谁，谁生了哪个孩子等等。（《飘》）
+ ┏ **it has never been explained why……** 谁也无法解释……（原文）
  ┗ nobody can explain why……（人称主语，主次颠倒）
  ┏ **why…… is beyond me** 我无法理解……
  ┗ I can’t <u>understand/ explain</u> why…… 我无法理解/解释……（人称主语）
  ✎ <u>Why</u> people are prepared to tolerate a four-hour journey each day for the dubious privilege of living in the country <u>is beyond me</u>.（L41）
  ✎ <u>Why</u> Jane was prepared to marry such a lazy-bones <u>is beyond me</u>. 我无法理解Jane为什么愿意(be prepared to do)嫁给这样一个懒汉(lazy-bones)。
  **It has always been a mystery to me why……** ……对我来说一直是个谜，我无法理解……
  ✎ <u>It has always been a mystery to me why</u> city dwellers, who appreciate all these things, obstinately pretend that they would prefer to live in the country.（L41）
  ✎ <u>It has always been a mystery to me why</u> John obstinately pretends that he would prefer classical music. 我一直搞不懂John为什么偏要假装(obstinately pretend)喜欢古典乐(classical music)。
  **be a mystery to sb.** 对某人来说简直是个迷（某人无法理解某事）
  ✎ M: I was shocked when I heard you’d finished your research project a whole month early.
  W: How I managed to do it <u>is still a mystery to</u> me.
  Q: What does the woman mean?
  Answer: She’s not sure how she was able to finish so early.（托福听力真题）
  + ┏ **whether…… is a moot point at present** 人们对……尚有争议（a moot point 悬而未决的问题，有争议的问题（书面语））
    ┗ People still have different opinions about whether……（不地道）
    ✎ <u>Whether</u> the whole universe does so <u>is a moot point at present</u>.（B4L37）
    ✎ <u>Whether</u> building more roads reduces traffic congestion <u>is a moot point at present</u>. 人们对是否建造更多公路会减少交通堵塞(traffic congestion)尚有争议。
> 仿写第1句 
  谁也无法解释玛雅(Maya)文明为什么会突然从地球上消失(vanish)。
  <u>It has never been explained why</u> Maya civilization vanished from the earth.
  谁也无法解释为什么住在地中海地区的人看似比任何人都更爱吃章鱼(octopus)。
  <u>It has never been explained why</u> people who live in the Mediterranean seem to enjoy eating octopus more than anyone else.

+ **specialize in……** 专门研究……
  **specialized** a. 专业的
  ✎ <u>specialized</u> knowledge 专业知识
  ✎ <u>specialized</u> labour/ labor 专业工人
  ✎ So great is our passion for doing things for ourselves, that we are becoming increasingly less dependent on <u>specialized labour</u>.（L46）
+ ┏ **表示种类的词(kind, sort, type等) + of + 中心名词**（最正式的表达，可数名词作不可数来用；用复数也不算错，但不够正式）（L34）
  ┗ **中心名词 + of + 表示种类的词(kind, sort, type等)**（可数名词用复数）
  ┏ **a particular type of practical joke**（原文）
  ┗ **practical joke<u>s</u> of a particular type**
  ┏ <u>The more expensive kind of antique shop</u> where rare objects are beautifully displayed in glass cases to keep them free from dust <u>is</u> usually a forbidding place.（L34）
  ┗ <u>Antique shops of the more expensive kind</u> where rare objects are beautifully displayed in glass cases to keep them free from dust <u>are</u> usually forbidding places.
+ 表示**类型/种类**（类指与特指的区分）
  ① 定冠词the + 单数名词 ✎ the puma；
  ② 不定冠词a/an + 单数名词 ✎ a puma；
  ③ 复数名词 ✎ pumas。
+ **put out = extinguish** 熄灭（不强调灭火方式）
  ✎ <u>put out/ extinguish</u> the <u>fire/ cigarette/ light</u> 
  强调灭火方式的表达：
  **smother** vt. 闷熄；闷死
  **quench** vt. 浇灭；解渴
  **blow out** 吹灭
+ **crude** a. 低俗的，粗俗的，没品位的
  ✎ However, boxing was very <u>crude</u>, for there were no rules and a prizefighter could be seriously injured or even killed during a match.（L21）
+ **form** n. a type of sth. 类型，种类
  **form of……**
  ✎ a severe <u>form of</u> cancer 一种严重的癌症
  ✎ different <u>forms of</u> government 不同种类的政府
+ **no self-respecting…… would do sth.** 没有任何有自尊心的……会做某事（self-respecting 通常用于否定句）
  ✎ <u>No self-respecting</u> doctor <u>would</u> refuse to treat a sick person. 没有任何一个有自尊心的医生会拒绝治疗病人。
  ✎ <u>No self-respecting</u> government <u>would</u> yield to terrorists. 没有任何一个有自尊心的政府会向恐怖分子低头。/ 任何有自尊心的政府都不会向恐怖分子屈服。（**yield** vi. 屈服）
> 仿写第3句
  考试中作弊是一种很不光彩的行为(disgraceful behavior)，任何有自尊的学生都不会去做。
  Cheating in examinations is disgraceful behavior which no self-respecting student would ever indulge in.

+ **amusing** 与 **funny**同义替换
  ┏ Students often create <u>amusing</u> situations which are <u>funny</u> to everyone except the victims.（原文）
  ┗ Students often create <u>funny</u> situations which <u>are amusing to/ amuse</u> everyone except the victims.
+ **telephone the police** 报警
  ✎ He told him he had better return it or he would **call the police**.（L16）
  ✎ At first, she decided to **go to the police**, but……（L19）
  ✎ Mrs. Ramsay was not to **inform the police** and had to pay £1,000.（L19-课后题2b）
+ ┏ **inform sb. of sth.** 通知某人某事
  ┗ **inform sb. that……**
  ┏ **convince sb. of sth.** 使某人相信某事
  ┗ **convince sb. that……**
  ┏ **remind sb. of sth.** 使某人回忆起某事
  ┗ **remind sb. that……**
  ┏ **warn sb. of sth.** 警告某人某事
  ┗ **warn sb. that……**
  ┏ **assure sb. of sth.** 让某人对某事放心
  ┗ **assure sb. that……**
+ **dress (sb.) up as……** 装扮成……，打扮成……（L13）
  ✎ She intended to <u>dress up as</u> a ghost……（L13）
  ✎ He added that a student had <u>dressed up as</u> a policeman……（本文）
  ✎ They <u>dressed</u> him <u>up as</u> a gorilla. 他们把他打扮成了大猩猩。
  **disguise sb. as……** 把某人装扮成……
  ✎ He <u>disguised</u> himself <u>as</u> a dustman.（L4-课后题2b）
  **disguised as……** 被装扮成…… (非谓语)
  ✎ Alfred the Great acted as his own spy, visiting Danish camps <u>disguised as a minstrel</u>.（B4L9）
  ✎ …… two students <u>disguised as workmen</u> were tearing up the road with a pneumatic drill.（原文换用）
+ **tear up sth.** 开凿/挖开某物（路面等）；撕碎
  ✎ The plumbers <u>tore up</u> the road to lay a new water main. 水管工把路面挖开，铺设了一条新的主干水管。
  ✎ He <u>tore up</u> the letter with anger. 他愤怒地撕碎了那封信。
  **tear** 撕，扯
  ✎ The child’s misery <u>tore my heart</u>. 孩子的苦难让我心碎。
  **tear sth. in <u>half/ two</u>** 将某物撕成两半（类似于rip）
  **tear sth. to pieces** 将某物撕成碎片
  **tear sth. away** 将某物撕掉/扯掉/卷走
  ✎ In August, she was struck by a very heavy storm during which her rudder <u>was torn away</u>.（L25）
+ **as soon as……** 刚一……马上就……
  其它引导时间状语从句的同义/近义词：
  **<u>immediately/ directly</u>……** 刚一……就……（连词）
  **the moment……** 就在那一刻，刚一发生就……（类似连词）
  **<u>on/ upon</u>……** 刚一…… 马上就……（介词）
  **no sooner…… than……** 刚一…… 马上就……（副词+连词）
  **<u>hardly/ barely/ scarcely</u>…… <u>when/ before</u>……**（副词+连词）
  原文换用：
  ✎ <u>Immediately/ Directly</u> he had hung up,……
  ✎ <u>The moment</u> he had hung up,……
  ✎ <u>On/ Upon</u> hanging up,……
  ┏ He had <u>no sooner</u> hung up <u>than</u> he went over to……
  ┗ <u>No sooner</u> **had** he hung up <u>than</u> he went over to……（强调“刚一”，否定词置于句首，引起部分倒装）
  ┏ He had <u>hardly</u> hung up <u>when</u> he went over to……
  ┗ <u>Hardly</u> **had** he hung up <u>when</u> he went over to……（强调“刚一”，否定词置于句首，引起部分倒装）
+ **hang up** 挂断电话（L33）
  ✎ You <u>hang up</u> hurriedly and attend to baby, crockery, etc.（L33）
  同义表达：
  **put the phone down**
  **slam the phone down** 气愤地挂断电话
  **get cut off** 线路中断
  ✎ M: Did you <u>get cut off</u>?
  W: No, they asked me to <u>hang up</u> and try again later.
  Q: What has the woman been doing?
  Answer: Talking on the telephone.（托福听力真题）
+ went **over** to（比went to更强调跨度）
  ✎ He’s seen me! He’s coming <u>over</u>! 他看见我了！他过来了！
  ✎ M: Can you come over for dinner tonight?
    W: I’m up to my ears in work, so I’ll have to take a rain check.（take a rain check 改日，择期(习语)）
    Q: What does the woman mean?
    Answer: She’d enjoy coming to dinner another time.（托福听力真题）

#### 👾 **be + to do（fml.）的四种用法**
1. **打算**（比be going to do正式）
  ✎ I<u>’m to</u> see her tomorrow. 明天我打算去看她。
2. **命令**
  ✎ You<u>’re to</u> be back by 10 o’clock.  你必须在10点前回来。
  ✎ No one <u>is to</u> leave the building. 任何人不得离开大楼。
3. **能够**
  ✎ How <u>am</u> I <u>to</u> pay such a debt? 我该如何偿还这样一笔债呢？
  ✎ We Chinese people <u>are</u> not <u>to</u> be bullied. 我们中国人是不能够被吓唬的。
4. **应该**
  ✎ Such men <u>are to</u> be pitied rather than despised. 这些人应该被同情，而不是被鄙视。
  ✎ Some books <u>are to</u> be tasted, others <u>to</u> be swallowed, and some few <u>to</u> be chewed and digested. — Francis Bacon
  有些书应该浅尝即可，其他书应该囫囵吞下，只有少数书应该咀嚼和消化。（弗朗西斯·培根《论读书》）
+ **add** v. 补充说，接着说，~~做加法~~（L11）
  ✎ Then I <u>added</u> with a smile, ‘It’s a strange mixture I make myself.’（L11）
  **threaten** v. 威胁说
  ✎ When he received a very rude reply from one of the workmen, he <u>threatened</u> to remove them by force.（本文）
  **point out** 指出，提醒说
  ✎ At this, the police <u>pointed out</u> ironically that this would hardly be necessary as the men were already under arrest.（本文）
  **claim** 声称说
  ✎ However, as the evidence began to accumulate, experts from the Zoo felt obliged to investigate, for the descriptions given by people who <u>claimed</u> to have seen the puma were extraordinarily similar.（L1）
  **confirm** 证实说
  ✎ It immediately ran away when she saw it, and experts <u>confirmed</u> that a puma will not attack a human being unless it is cornered.（L1）
  **complain** 抱怨说
  ✎ Several people <u>complained</u> of ‘cat-like noises’ at night and a businessman on a fishing trip saw the puma up a tree.（L1）
  **put it** 措辞说
  ✎ …… , as one of them <u>put it</u> ‘ate like kings’.（L12）
  ✎ I don’t know how to <u>put it</u>. 这句话我不知道该怎么措辞。
  **stat** 声明说
  ✎ The writer <u>stated</u> that Rastus was in safe hands……（L19）
  **explain** 解释说
  ✎ She <u>explained</u> that Rastus was very dear to her.（L19）
  **mumble** 喃喃自语说
  ✎ He was still <u>mumbling</u> something about hospitals at the end of the party when he slipped on a piece of ice and broke his left leg.（L29）
  **nag** 数落，唠叨说
  ✎ When my wife <u>nagged</u> me to do something about it, I told her that either I would have to buy a new mower or let the grass grow.（L46）
+ **play a <u>joke/ trick</u> on sb.** 对某人恶作剧，拿某人开玩笑
  ✎ One night, the gaoler decided to <u>play a joke on</u> his colleague to find out if, after so many performances, he had managed to learn the contents of the letter by heart.（L22）
+ **all <u>sorts/ kinds/ types</u> of sth.** 各种各样的某物，~~所有种类的~~
  ✎ She has to deal with <u>all kinds of complaints</u> every day. 她每天必须要处理各种各样的投诉/抱怨。
+ **be <u>thankful/ grateful/ obliged/ indebted</u> to sb. for sth.** 因为某事而感谢某人
  ✎ I<u>’m thankful to</u> you <u>for</u> your help. 我感谢你的帮助。
  ✎ I<u>’m</u> much <u>grateful to</u> you <u>for</u> your advice. 我非常感谢你的建议。
  ✎ I<u>’m</u> deeply <u>obliged to</u> you <u>for</u> your encouragement. 我深深地感谢你的鼓励。
  ✎ I<u>’m</u> most <u>indebted to</u> you <u>for</u> this piece of advance information. 我对你提前通知我此事极其感谢。
  **I appreciate <u>your help/ it</u>.** 我感谢你的帮助。（L15）
  **I owe you (one).** 我欠你的。（用于熟人之间）（L15）
+ 【✔】an archway <u>nearby</u>（副词）
  【✔】a <u>nearby</u> archway（形容词）
  【✘】a <u>near</u> archway（表空间的近，不能作前置定语）
  【✔】The archway is very <u>near</u>. 柱廊离这非常近。（表空间的近，可作表语）
  【✔】in the <u>near</u> future 在不远的未来（表时间的近，可作前置定语）
  【✔】a <u>near</u> relative 一个近亲（表亲属关系的近，可作前置定语）
+ The student hid in an archway nearby <u>where he could watch and hear everything that went on</u>.
  形式上是定语从句，翻译上类似于并列句，甚至类似于原因状语从句。
  ✎ 我的暑假是在乡下度过的，在那儿我可以更不受打扰地生活。
  I spent my summer vacation in the country where I had more privacy.
  （参考：The monks prefer winter to summer for they <u>have more privacy</u>. 更不受打扰地生活（L8））
+ **sure enough** 果然（固定搭配）
  ✎ <u>Sure enough</u>, Rastus arrived punctually at seven o’clock that evening.（L19）
+ **on the <u>scene/ spot</u>** ① 在现场，到现场
  ✎ Meanwhile, two other actors, Rockwall Slinger and Merlin Greeves, had carried two large food baskets to <u>a shady spot</u> under some trees.（B2L74）
  **on the spot** ② 当场……，立即……
  ✎ He would invent fanciful names <u>on the spot</u>.（L52）
+ **receive + n.** 受到了……；得到了……；遭到了……
  ✎ These young people, who love the peace of mountains, always <u>receive a warm welcome</u> at St. Bernard’s monastery.（L8）
  ✎ No creature has <u>received</u> more <u>praise and abuse</u> than the common garden snail.（L23）
  ✎ This exhibition <u>received a great deal of attention</u> in the press, for though the pictures were supposed to be the work of famous artists, they had in fact been painted by Dickie.（L31）
  ✎ The majority of the patients attending the medical out-patients departments of our hospitals feel that they have not <u>received adequate treatment</u> unless they are able to carry home with them some tangible remedy in the shape of a bottle of medicine, a box of pills, or a small jar of ointment,……（B4L28）
  **receive support** 得到支持
  **receive good education** 受到良好教育
  **receive a heavy blow** 遭到重重的一击
  **receive a serious injury** 遭受重伤
+ **threaten to do** ① 威胁说…… (人作主语)；② 有……的危险 (事物作主语)
  ✎ We keep trying all four methods, but the sheer volume of rubbish we produce worldwide <u>threatens to overwhelm us</u>.（L47）
+ **please** v. 高兴，乐意
  ✎ Come whenever you <u>please</u>. 你乐意什么时候来就什么时候来。
+ **shortly afterwards = before long** 不久之后（固定搭配）（详见L26）
+ ┏ **lose one’s temper** 发火，发脾气
  ┗ **keep one’s temper** 忍住不发脾气
+ **在英语中，this和that均可前指，但一般只有this可以后指。**
  ✎ <u>He threatened to call the police.</u> At <u>this</u>, the police pointed out ironically that……（本文）
  ✎ Finding that he could not remember a word of the letter either, the gaoler replied: <u>‘The light is indeed dim, sire, I must get my glasses.’</u> With <u>this</u>, he hurried off the stage.（L22）
  ✎ <u>To be, or not to be</u>: <u>that</u> is the question. —— Shakespeare
  ✎ <u>Good friends, good books and a sleepy conscience</u>: <u>this</u> is the ideal life. —— Mark Twain
  好朋友、好书和沉睡的良心：这就是理想的生活。——马克吐温
  ✎ Of all men’s miseries the bitterest is <u>this</u>: <u>to know so much and to have control over nothing</u>. —— Herodotus
  在所有人类的痛苦中，最痛苦的是：知道的很多，却什么都不能控制。——希罗多德
+ **point out** 指出，提醒说
  ✎ Franz poured scorn on the idea, <u>pointing out</u> that his brother had been killed in action during the war.（L36）
+ **be under + n.** 处于某状态
  ◇ **be under arrest** 被捕（本文）
  ◇ The car **is under repair**. 汽车正在修理。
  ◇ The castle **is under attack**. 城堡正在遭受攻击。
  ◇ The subject **is under discussion**. 这个主题正在讨论中。
  ◇ The matter **is under consideration**. 此事正在考虑中。
  ◇ The patient **is under observation**. 病人正处在观察中。
  ◇ The case **is under investigation**. 案件正在调查中。
  ◇ The bridge **is under construction**. 桥正在建设中。
  ◇ The building **is under renovation**. 大楼正在整修中。（**renovation** 翻新，整修；**innovation** 创新）
  （以上的“中” —— 对应英文 **under**，~~in~~。其它的“中”举例：be **on** show 正在展览中）

#### 👾 **动名词的时态和语态（复制自L4）**
|时态 / 语态|主动|被动|
|:----:|----:|----:|
|**一般时**|doing|being done|
|**完成时**|having done|having been done|

┏ 一般时：不强调动作发生的顺序。
┗ 完成时：强调动作先发生。
故：能用完成时的地方，一般都能换用一般时；用一般时的地方，不一定能换用完成时。
✎ （例句详见L4）

+ ┏ **<u>give/ grant</u> (sb.) permission** 给予(某人)允许/许可（固定搭配）（grant 更正式）
  ┗ **<u>refuse/ deny</u> (sb.) permission** 拒绝/不允许(某人)做某事
  ┏ Permission was granted and a policeman……（原文）
  ┗ The police granted him permission and a policeman……（主动-显啰嗦）
> 仿写最后一段倒数2、3句
  他问老师他是否能打个电话。老师不允许他这么做，于是他只好等到下课。
  He asked the teacher if he might make a telephone call. <u>Permission was denied</u> and he had to wait until the class was over.
+ **<u>pay phone/ pay station</u>** 公共电话

#### 👾 **部分倒装复习（详见L5、L37）**
2. **“only + 状语”位于句首**
意为：只有……才……（非时间状语）；直到……才……（时间状语）


## 第二单元结束🎉
恭喜你顺利完成此次任务！请点击小地球返航！[🌏](#第三册目录)
